# physics.pop-ph [[Back]](#toc)

### [1] [Black holes and bits: A simple path to Bekenstein-Hawking entropy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.22245)
*Jorge Pinochet*

Main category: physics.pop-ph

TL;DR: 本文提供了一个简单推导黑洞熵（black hole entropy）方程的方法，该方程现称为贝肯斯坦-霍金熵（Bekenstein-Hawking entropy），并简要探讨了其物理意义及其与霍金工作的关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 20世纪70年代初，雅各布·贝肯斯坦发现黑洞具有熵，这成为20世纪下半叶最伟大的科学革命之一。本文旨在提供一个简单推导黑洞熵方程的方法。

Method: 采用部分启发式（partly heuristic）和部分几何（partly geometric）的方法，推导黑洞熵的方程。该方法结合了直观推理与几何分析。

Result: 成功推导出黑洞熵的方程，即现在所知的贝肯斯坦-霍金熵（Bekenstein-Hawking entropy）。该方程建立了黑洞热力学的基本关系。

Conclusion: 简要探讨了黑洞熵方程的物理意义，并分析了该方程与斯蒂芬·霍金（Stephen Hawking）工作的关系，深化了对黑洞热力学的理解。

Abstract: In the early 1970s, Jacob Bekenstein discovered that black holes have entropy, which became one of the greatest scientific revolutions of the second half of the 20th century. The objective of this paper is to present a simple derivation -- partly heuristic and partly geometric -- of the equation for the entropy of a black hole, which we now know as the Bekenstein-Hawking entropy. We will also briefly explore the physical implications of this equation and its relationship to the work of Stephen Hawking.

</details>


<div id='physics.flu-dyn'></div>

# physics.flu-dyn [[Back]](#toc)

### [2] [Kelvin wave and soliton propagation in classical viscous vortex filaments](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.22439)
*Elio Sterkers,Giorgio Krstulovic*

Main category: physics.flu-dyn

TL;DR: 该论文通过三维不可压缩Navier-Stokes方程的数值模拟，研究了涡旋丝（vortex filaments）中的Kelvin波传播、孤立子（solitons）存在性及其碰撞，并提出了实验室生成涡旋孤立子的实验方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 涡旋丝（vortex filaments）作为流体中高度旋转的局域化结构，具有多种激发模式。研究旨在通过数值模拟探索这些结构的动力学特性，特别是Kelvin波和孤立子的传播行为。

Method: 采用三维不可压缩Navier-Stokes方程的数值模拟方法。首先研究沿涡旋丝传播的螺旋激发（helicoidal excitations）即Kelvin波，然后基于涡旋线动力学与可积系统（integrable system）的联系，数值研究孤立子的存在性和碰撞。

Result: Kelvin波的色散关系（dispersion relation）与Lord Kelvin的原始预测高度一致。数值模拟证实了沿涡旋丝传播的孤立子的存在，并成功研究了两个此类结构的碰撞过程。

Conclusion: 研究通过数值模拟验证了涡旋丝中Kelvin波和孤立子的理论预测，并提出了实验室生成涡旋孤立子的可行实验方案，为实验研究提供了理论基础。

Abstract: Vortex filaments are highly rotating localized structures of fluids that admits several types of excitation. Here, we study them by using numerical simulations of the three-dimensional incompressible Navier-Stokes equations. We first address the propagation of Kelvin waves, helicoidal excitations propagating along the filament, and measure their dispersion relation which turns out to be in good agreement with the original Lord Kelvin predictions. Then, inspired by the connection between vortex line dynamics and an integrable system, we show numerically the existence of solitons propagating along vortex filaments and study the collision of two of such structures. Finally, we show numerically the experimental feasibility of studying vortex solitons in the lab, by proposing an experiment for their generation.

</details>


<div id='cond-mat.mtrl-sci'></div>

# cond-mat.mtrl-sci [[Back]](#toc)

### [3] [Seamlessly joining length scales: From atomistic thermal graphs to anisotropic continuum conductivity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.22256)
*C. Ugwumadu,D. A. Drabold,R. M. Tutchton*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究开发了原子到连续介质尺度模拟器集合（SCACS），通过图神经网络预测位点投影热导率（SPTC），将其粗粒化为各向异性电导率张量，并嵌入热流有限元方程，实现了从原子尺度到器件尺度的热传输模拟。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 复杂固体中的热传输受局部结构、缺陷和各向异性影响，但大多数连续介质模型仍依赖过度简化的均匀化电导率。需要建立连接原子尺度与连续介质描述的桥梁。

Method: 开发了原子到连续介质尺度模拟器集合（Simulator Collection for Atomic-to-Continuum Scales, SCACS），使用图神经网络预测大原子结构上的位点投影热导率（site-projected thermal conductivity, SPTC），将这些场粗粒化为各向异性电导率张量，并通过定制的各向异性感知自适应网格细化方案将其嵌入热流有限元方程。

Result: 应用于硅纳米结构时，所得有限元模型可作为代表性体积单元，重现体电导率，捕捉界面和缺陷驱动的各向异性，同时保持热力学一致性。SCACS还能预测实验电导趋势和场分布。

Conclusion: 该创新展示了一种新颖且通用的方法，通过基于物理的近似将原子尺度传输信息转移到器件尺度热模拟中。

Abstract: Thermal transport in complex solids is governed by local structure, defects, and anisotropy, yet most continuum models still rely on oversimplified, homogenized conductivities. Here, we bridge atomistic and continuum descriptions by building finite element (FE) models directly from the site-projected thermal conductivity (SPTC), an atomic-level decomposition of the Green-Kubo thermal conductivity. We introduce a new toolkit, the Simulator Collection for Atomic-to-Continuum Scales (SCACS), which uses a graph neural network to predict SPTC on large atomic structures, coarse-grain these fields into anisotropic conductivity tensors, and embeds them into the heat-flow FE equation with a customized, anisotropy-aware adaptive mesh refinement scheme. Applied to silicon nanostructures, the resulting FE models act as representative volume elements, reproduce bulk conductivities, and capture interfacial and defect-driven anisotropy while maintaining thermodynamic consistency. Additionally, SCACS predicts experimental conductance trends and fields. This innovation demonstrates a novel and general route for transferring atomistic transport information into device-scale thermal simulations with physics-based approximations.

</details>


### [4] [Mimicking the earth core conditions with ultrafast laser materials interaction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.22460)
*Mohamed Yaseen Noor,Aram Yedigaryan,Gabriel Calderon,Arshak Tsaturyan,Elena Kanchan,Jinwoo Hwang,Carmen S. Menoni,Jean-Philippe Colombier,Enam Chowdhury*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 飞秒激光激发非晶态二氧化硅-氧化铪多层介质，在亚表面受限区域形成了高压二氧化硅晶相（斯石英、赛弗特石、黄铁矿型高密度结构），通过实验表征和分子动力学模拟揭示了非平衡热力学路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超快激光能创造极端非平衡热力学条件，达到类似地球内部核心的压力和温度。本研究旨在探索利用飞秒激光激发在常压下合成和稳定超高密度高压二氧化硅相，无需金刚石压砧（diamond anvil cell）。

Method: 采用透射电子显微镜（TEM）、选区电子衍射（SAED）和四维扫描透射电子显微镜（4D-STEM）直接映射纳米尺度相演化，识别激光生成气泡内的晶体结构。辅以分子动力学模拟揭示相变的热力学路径。

Result: 在非晶态二氧化硅-氧化铪多层介质的亚表面受限区域内，成功形成了高压二氧化硅晶相，包括斯石英（stishovite）、赛弗特石（seifertite）和黄铁矿型高密度结构（pyrite-type high density structure）。分子动力学模拟揭示了快速电子压力引发致密化和八面体配位，随后在超快淬火过程中发生温度驱动的结晶和位移相变。

Conclusion: 飞秒激光激发是在常压下合成和稳定超高密度高压二氧化硅相的可行途径，无需金刚石压砧。这一发现对激光损伤机制、高能量密度材料和行星物理学具有重要意义，揭示了平衡处理无法实现的双阶段路径。

Abstract: Ultrafast lasers create extreme, non-equilibrium thermodynamic conditions that can transiently reach pressures and temperatures comparable to interior core of the earth. Here we show that femtosecond excitation of amorphous silica-hafnia multilayer dielectrics drives the formation of high-pressure crystalline phases of silica including stishovite, seifertite, and the pyrite-type high density structure, within confined subsurface regions.Using TEM, SAED, and 4D-STEM, we directly map nanoscale phase evolution and identify crystalline motifs embedded inside laser generated blisters.Complementary molecular dynamics simualtions reveal the thermodynamic pathway underlying these transformations, where rapid electronic pressure initiates densification and octahedral coordination, followed by temperature driven crystallization and displacive transitions during ultrafast quenching. The resulting polymorphs reflects a dual-stage pathway inaccessible under equilibrium processing. Our results establish femtosecond laser excitation as a viable route to synthesize and stabilize ultrahigh-density high pressure silica phases under ambient conditions, without a diamond anvil cell, with implications for laser-damage mechanisms, high-energy-density materials, and planetary physics.

</details>


### [5] [Many-Body effects beyond excitons in second-harmonic generation of monolayer MoS$_{2}$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.22463)
*Peio Garcia-Goiricelaya,Julen Ibañez-Azpiroz*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究通过结合多体微扰理论和含时电流密度泛函理论，定量分析了单层MoS₂中二阶谐波产生（second-harmonic generation）的多体效应，发现三粒子（trionic）关联对准确描述二维半导体二阶光学响应至关重要。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在定量分析单层二硫化钼（MoS₂）中二阶谐波产生的多体效应，包括三粒子层次的影响，以更准确地描述二维半导体的二阶光学响应特性。

Method: 采用结合多体微扰理论（many-body perturbation theory）和含时电流密度泛函理论（time-dependent current-density-functional theory）的从头算（ab initio）框架，在光学极限下研究。通过动态长程线性交换关联核（dynamical long-range linear exchange-correlation kernel）包含双粒子激子效应，并通过静态长程二次交换关联核（static long-range quadratic exchange-correlation kernel）纳入三粒子（trionic）关联。

Result: 仅包含双粒子激子效应能重现二阶谐波响应的定性特征，但低估实验报告幅度近两倍。纳入三粒子关联后，与实验结果的定量一致性显著改善，表明超越激子层次的多体相互作用对准确描述二阶光学响应至关重要。

Conclusion: 研究证实三粒子（trionic）关联在准确描述二维半导体二阶光学响应中的关键作用，强调超越激子层次的多体相互作用对定量预测二阶谐波产生的重要性。

Abstract: We present a quantitative study of many-body effects including the three-particle level on second-harmonic generation in monolayer MoS$_{2}$. Our approach combines many-body perturbation theory with time-dependent current-density-functional theory within an \textit{ab initio} framework in the optical limit. Inclusion of two-particle excitonic effects \textit{via} a dynamical long-range linear exchange-correlation kernel reproduces the qualitative features of the second-harmonic response, but underestimates the experimentally reported magnitudes by nearly a factor of two. By incorporating three-particle (trionic) correlations through a static long-range quadratic exchange-correlation kernel, we achieve significantly improved quantitative agreement with experiment. These findings highlight the role of many-body interactions beyond the excitonic level in accurately describing second-order optical responses in two-dimensional semiconductors.

</details>


### [6] [The Surface Sensitivity of X-ray Second Harmonic Generation as a Function of Energy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.22497)
*Daniel Schacher,Tod A. Pascal,Keith V. Lawler,Craig P. Schwartz*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究通过速度规范实时含时密度泛函理论（VG-RT-TDDFT）分析金刚石在X射线区域的二次谐波产生（SHG）表面敏感性和探测深度，发现能量高于C K边（~285 eV）时SHG主要由体相四极响应主导，而近C K边时测量具有显著表面敏感性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究金刚石在X射线区域的二次谐波产生（second harmonic generation, SHG）的表面敏感性和探测深度，这对于理解非线性光学过程在材料表征中的应用具有重要意义。

Method: 采用速度规范实时含时密度泛函理论（velocity gauge real-time time-dependent density functional theory, VG-RT-TDDFT）进行解析和计算分析，包含完整多极展开。通过两种方法实现：计算上改变可产生SHG的层数和位置，以及利用晶体对称性。

Result: 研究发现，在1000 eV（远高于C K边的~285 eV）时，金刚石的SHG主要由体相四极响应（bulk, quadrupole response）主导，与解析计算结果一致。体相响应随能量增加持续增强，到7000 eV时占据绝对主导。近C K边时测量具有显著表面敏感性，但随着能量增加而减弱，到1000 eV（特别是3500 eV）时SHG主要对体相敏感。晶体取向的特定细节（如比较(001)终止面和(111)终止面）对表面敏感性有显著影响。

Conclusion: 金刚石在X射线区域的SHG表面敏感性强烈依赖于光子能量：近C K边时表面敏感，而高于1000 eV时体相响应占主导。晶体取向对表面敏感性有重要影响，这为利用SHG进行材料表征提供了重要指导。

Abstract: The surface sensitivity and probe depth in the x-ray regime of diamond for second harmonic generation (SHG) was investigated both analytically and computationally with velocity gauge real-time time-dependent density functional theory (VG-RT-TDDFT), which includes a full multipole expansion. This was accomplished using two different approaches, by changing the number and location of layers that can generate SHG computationally and by exploiting the symmetry of a crystal, a similar pattern emerged. We find that by 1000 eV, well above the ~285 eV of the C $K$-edge, the SHG of diamond is dominated by the bulk, quadrupole response, in agreement with our analytic calculations. The bulk response continues to grow as the energy is increased, becoming overwhelming by 7000 eV. Near the C $K$-edge the measurement is quite surface sensitive, however, this surface sensitivity reduces as the energy increases such that by 1000 eV (and certainly by 3500 eV) SHG is largely bulk sensitive. Moreover, we find that the specific details of the crystal orientation (i.e., comparing a (001)-terminated and (111)-terminated surface) appear to have significant effects on the surface sensitivity.

</details>


### [7] [Interpretable self-driving sputter epitaxy: from black-box optimization to human-usable growth rules](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.22531)
*Yuki K. Wakabayashi,Yui Ogawa,Franz Benedict Romero,Takuma Otsuka,Yoshitaka Taniyasu*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种可解释的自驱动实验室框架，将自主优化转化为人类可用的生长规则，应用于射频磁控溅射生长高质量β-Ga₂O₃薄膜，实现了最低Urbach能量182 meV，并通过随机森林代理模型提取了可转移的生长规则。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前自驱动实验室（self-driving laboratories）虽然能探索高维工艺空间，但通常作为黑盒优化器存在，难以提供可转移的工艺理解。本研究旨在开发一个可解释的自驱动实验室框架，将自主优化结果转化为人类可用的生长规则。

Method: 结合贝叶斯优化（Bayesian optimization）与Urbach能量的自动光学评估作为亚带隙无序度量，应用于射频磁控溅射（RF magnetron sputtering）生长β-Ga₂O₃薄膜。通过训练随机森林（random forest）代理模型，将四维生长参数空间的数据转化为响应曲线和量化的成对相互作用。

Result: 自驱动系统高效识别出异质外延生长条件，实现了最低Urbach能量182 meV，这是溅射β-Ga₂O₃薄膜的最低值。优化后的生长窗口具有可转移性，无需进一步优化即可实现单晶β-Ga₂O₃同质外延，经扫描透射电子显微镜验证。分析表明衬底温度是主要控制参数，射频功率和气体流量主要起加和作用，仅存在适度的温度-氧气耦合效应。

Conclusion: 该研究建立了一条从自主实验到可转移生长规则的通用路径，通过可解释的自驱动实验室框架将黑盒优化转化为人类可理解的工艺知识，为材料生长提供了系统化的理解框架。

Abstract: Self-driving laboratories have emerged as powerful tools for navigating high-dimensional process spaces, yet systems remain black-box optimizers that yield limited transferable process understanding. Here, we demonstrate an interpretable self-driving laboratory framework that transforms autonomous optimization into human-usable growth rules. As a stringent benchmark, we apply this framework to RF magnetron sputtering, addressing a long-standing challenge of achieving high-quality beta-Ga2O3 heteroepitaxy and single-crystalline beta-Ga2O3 homoepitaxy via sputtering. By combining Bayesian optimization with automated optical evaluation of the Urbach energy as a metric of sub-bandgap disorder, the self-driving system efficiently identifies heteroepitaxial growth conditions yielding a minimum Urbach energy of 182 meV, the lowest value for sputtered beta-Ga2O3 films. Importantly, the optimized growth window is transferable, realizing single-crystalline beta-Ga2O3 homoepitaxy without further optimization, corroborated by scanning transmission electron microscopy. To convert the closed-loop dataset into interpretable growth rules, we train a random forest surrogate and distill it into response curves and quantified pairwise interactions across the four-dimensional growth-parameter space. This analysis identifies substrate temperature as the primary control knob, with RF power and gas flows acting largely additively and only a modest temperature-oxygen coupling delineating the narrow window for high-quality growth, establishing a general route from autonomous experimentation to transferable growth rules.

</details>


### [8] [Symmetry-Protected Minimum of Four Conventional Weyl Points in Nonmagnetic Crystals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.22566)
*Ze-Xin Xue,Ke-Xin Pang,Yun-Yun Bai,Yanfeng Ge,Yong Liu,Yan Gao*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究通过对称性分析与第一性原理计算，建立了非磁性晶体中实现四个传统外尔点（Weyl points）的精确条件，并预测了两种新型硼同素异形体作为理想外尔半金属材料。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 实现具有最少传统外尔点（Weyl points）和纯净费米面（clean Fermi surface）的非磁性外尔半金属（Weyl semimetals）是当前研究的核心挑战。该工作旨在解决这一材料设计难题。

Method: 结合对称性分析（symmetry analysis）与第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations），建立了非磁性晶体中容纳恰好四个传统外尔点（C = ±1）的精确条件，并以此框架指导材料预测。

Result: 确定了76个无自旋空间群和83个有自旋空间群允许这种最小外尔点配置。预测了两种新型硼同素异形体P6-B₄₈和TBIN-B₄₈作为理想外尔半金属，两者均在费米能级附近具有四个孤立外尔点，且电子结构异常纯净。

Conclusion: 该研究为最小外尔物理（minimal Weyl physics）提供了完整的基于对称性的理论基础和纯净的材料平台，预测的材料展现出独特的表面态特征，包括单费米弧和双费米弧。

Abstract: Realizing nonmagnetic Weyl semimetals (WSMs) with the minimal number of conventional Weyl points (WPs) and a clean Fermi surface remains a central challenge. Here, combining symmetry analysis with first-principles calculations, we establish the definitive conditions under which a nonmagnetic crystal can host exactly four conventional ($C = \pm 1$) WPs, identifying 76 space groups in the spinless limit and 83 in the spinful case that allow this minimal configuration. Guided by this framework, we predict two previously unknown boron allotropes, P6-B$_{48}$ and TBIN-B$_{48}$, as ideal WSMs. Both exhibits precisely four isolated WPs near the Fermi level, with exceptionally clean electronic structures. Notably, the WPs in P6-B$_{48}$ are pinned to high-symmetry points, while those in TBIN-B$_{48}$ lie along high-symmetry lines, leading to distinct and experimentally accessible surface states, including single and double Fermi arcs. Our work provides a complete symmetry-based foundation and pristine material platforms for minimal Weyl physics.

</details>


### [9] [Single Pair of Charge-two Weyl Fermions in Chiral Boron Allotropes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.22622)
*Hui-Jing Zheng,Yan Gao,Yanfeng Ge,Yong Liu,Zhong-Yi Lu*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究首次在非磁性材料中实现了仅含一对外尔点（Weyl points）的最小外尔半金属（Weyl semimetal），突破了时间反演对称性通常要求至少四个外尔点的限制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 此前，实现仅含一对Weyl点的最小Weyl半金属仅限于磁性体系，因为时间反演对称性（time-reversal symmetry）通常强制非磁性材料中至少存在四个Weyl点。本研究旨在寻找非磁性材料平台来实现这种最小Weyl半金属态。

Method: 结合第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）与对称性分析（symmetry analysis），识别出两种稳定的硼同素异形体：手性HDSBC-B$_{20}$和笼状CR-B$_{12}$。

Result: 发现这两种材料在无自旋（spinless）体系中首次实现了仅含一对拓扑荷C=2的Weyl点，这些双Weyl点（double-WPs）被钉扎在时间反演不变动量点。Weyl点沿旋转轴呈线性色散，在垂直平面呈二次色散。HDSBC-B$_{20}$中拓扑荷符号与结构手性直接相关，两种材料均具有跨越表面布里渊区的超长双费米弧（double Fermi arcs）。

Conclusion: 该研究建立了非磁性材料平台用于实现最小双Weyl费米子（double-Weyl fermions），并拓宽了非常规Weyl半金属的研究领域。

Abstract: The realization of a minimal Weyl semimetal (WSM) hosting a single pair of Weyl points (WPs) has thus far been restricted to magnetic systems, since time-reversal symmetry generally enforces a minimum of four WPs in nonmagnetic materials. Here, combining first-principles calculations with symmetry analysis, we identify two stable boron allotropes, chiral HDSBC-B$_{20}$ and cage-like CR-B$_{12}$, as the first nonmagnetic electronic materials realizing a single pair of WPs in the spinless regime. We show that the interplay between time-reversal symmetry and crystallographic rotation symmetry ($C_4$ or $C_3$) stabilizes exactly one pair of $C=2$ WPs pinned at time-reversal-invariant momenta, thereby circumventing the conventional node-quartet constraint. These double-WPs exhibit linear dispersion along the rotation axis and quadratic dispersion in the perpendicular plane. In HDSBC-B$_{20}$, the sign of the topological charge is directly correlated with structural chirality. Both materials host exceptionally long double Fermi arcs spanning the surface Brillouin zone, providing experimentally accessible signatures. Our findings establish nonmagnetic material platforms for minimal double-Weyl fermions and broaden the landscape of unconventional WSMs.

### [10] [LLM-driven discovery for carbon allotropes with bond-network entropy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.22706)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 建立了一个闭环AI框架，该框架协同结合了用于结构生成的大语言模型（Large Language Model, LLM）和用于加速评估的机器学习势（Machine Learning Potential, MLP）。引入杂化熵描述符来指导超越常规形式的搜索，利用CrystaLLM生成候选结构，并通过迭代精炼的MLP进行高保真验证。

Conclusion: 这项工作扩展了已知的碳相空间，并证明了将生成式AI与机器学习势耦合用于功能材料加速逆向设计的有效性。微观分析表明这些材料中的热输运受刚性框架和柔性连接体之间相互作用的调控。

Abstract: The discovery of novel carbon allotropes with tailored thermal and mechanical properties is critical for advanced thermal management. However, exploring the vast configurational space of carbon using \textit{ab initio} calculations remains computationally prohibitive. Driven by the rich topological landscape of carbon, where the competition between $sp, sp^2,$ and $sp^3$ hybridization states dictates material performance, we establish a closed-loop AI framework to explore this complex configurational space. We introduce a hybridization entropy descriptor to guide the search beyond conventional forms. Here, we establish a closed-loop AI framework that synergizes a Large Language Model (LLM) for structural generation with a Machine Learning Potential (MLP) for accelerated evaluation. Leveraging CrystaLLM to generate candidates and an iteratively refined MLP for high-fidelity validation, we screened thousands of structures to identify several stable allotropes with exotic properties. Specifically, we report ``yne-diamond C$_{12}$'' and ``yne-hex-diamond C$_{8}$'', which exhibit extreme thermal anisotropy and ultralow in-plane shear stiffness arising from their mixed $sp$-$sp^3$ hybridization. Furthermore, we discovered a complex $sp$-$sp^2$-$sp^3$ hybridized C$_{12}$ phase that combines metallic conductivity with an anomalous negative Poisson's ratio. Notably, we identified a superhard phase (C16_3) possessing a calculated Vickers hardness (103.3 GPa) exceeding that of diamond 96 GPa). Microscopic analysis reveals that thermal transport in these materials is governed by the interplay between rigid frameworks and flexible linkers. This work expands the known carbon phase space and demonstrates the efficacy of coupling generative AI with machine learning potentials for the accelerated inverse design of functional materials.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 本研究引入了一种方法，能够在双钙钛矿体系（Sr2InNbO6、Sr2InTaO6、Ba2InTaO6、Ba2InNbO6）中，通过电子云扩张效应（nephelauxetic effect）对Mn4+离子的2E态寿命以及绝对和相对灵敏度进行理论描述。研究进行了实证分析，开发了基于β1参数的预测模型。

Result: 研究结果明确显示，与常见假设相反，Dq/B比值并非控制Mn4+离子光谱行为或Mn4+掺杂荧光粉测温性能的主要因素。相反，电子云扩张β1参数（nephelauxetic beta1 parameter）起着主导作用。开发的预测模型能够仅基于β1参数估算SAMAX和SRMAX值。

Conclusion: 该方法代表了向理性设计具有预定测温特性的寿命型发光温度计（lifetime-based luminescence thermometers）迈出的重要一步，能够根据特定应用需求定制测温特性。

Abstract: Although the considerable potential of luminescence thermometry based on emission kinetics has been widely demonstrated, reliable tools for the intentional prediction of thermometric performance remain limited. To address this challenge, the present work introduces an approach that enables a theoretical description of the 2E state lifetime of Mn4+ ions, as well as the absolute and relative sensitivities, in terms of the nephelauxetic effect within the group of double perovskites: Sr2InNbO6, Sr2InTaO6, Ba2InTaO6, and Ba2InNbO6. Our results clearly show that, contrary to common assumptions, the Dq/B ratio is not the primary factor governing either the spectroscopic behavior of Mn4+ ions or the thermometric performance of Mn4+-doped phosphors. Instead, the nephelauxetic beta1 parameter plays the dominant role. The empirical analysis carried out in this study led to the development of a predictive model that enables estimation of SAMAX and SRMAX values based exclusively on beta1. This methodology represents a significant step toward the rational design of lifetime-based luminescence thermometers with predefined thermometric characteristics tailored to the requirements of specific applications.

### [12] [Anti-Thermal Quenching Phosphors based on Metal Halides](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.22737)

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 热淬灭（thermal quenching, TQ）普遍存在于荧光粉中，限制了其在高温/高功率应用（如户外照明和激光系统）中的使用。金属卤化物虽然晶格较软，但近年来作为抗热淬灭荧光粉显示出显著进展，需要系统总结其发展。

Method: 通过文献综述方法，回顾了2017年首次报道至今的抗热淬灭金属卤化物研究进展。分析遵循两个指导原则：增加晶格刚性以减少热膨胀；将热能转化为辐射跃迁以补偿非辐射损失。

Result: 金属卤化物因其低温合成特性和高光致发光量子产率（photoluminescence quantum yields, PLQYs），成为有前景的抗热淬灭荧光粉候选材料。软晶格金属卤化物中抗热淬灭效应的丰富光学物理过程正开始被揭示。

Abstract: Thermal quenching (TQ) generally occurs in phosphors and is ascribed to the activation of non-radiative transitions at elevated temperatures. This effect limits the use of most phosphors in high-power/high-temperature applications, such as outdoor lighting and laser systems. To achieve anti-TQ properties, structural design of phosphors is required. This usually follows two guidelines: (1) increasing lattice rigidity to minimize thermal expansion; (2) converting thermal energy into radiative transitions to compensate for the non-radiative losses. While metal oxides and metal nitrides dominate the field of commercial anti-TQ phosphors, metal halides - despite their inherently soft lattices - have shown remarkable progress as anti-TQ phosphors in recent years. Here, we review the advances in anti-TQ metal halides (covering the time span from 2017, when first reports have appeared, till today) and discuss their mechanisms and applications. We argue that the low synthesis temperatures of metal halides and their high photoluminescence quantum yields (PLQYs) make them promising candidates as anti-TQ phosphors. Furthermore, since the rich optical-physical processes underlying the anti-TQ effect in soft-lattice in metal halides are only now beginning to be unraveled, this creates opportunities for many fundamental investigations.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用Fe-25W（原子百分比）合金粉末，在定制自动化反应器中进行千克级粉末床实验；通过温度分辨的原位X射线衍射（temperature-resolved in-situ X-ray diffraction）揭示化学气相传输介导的自发泡沫化机制。

Abstract: H2-H2O redox cycling of iron powder beds at 650-800 °C offers a compact, safe, economical hydrogen storage method, but sintering-induced capacity loss has stalled its scalability for decades. Here, we show that adding redox-active tungsten to Fe powders solves this problem in static powder beds: Fe-25W (at%) alloyed powder self-foams during redox cycling via W gas-phase transport, increasing porosity and preserving capacity. In a custom automated reactor, a kilogram-scale powder bed reversibly stores 42g H2 and sustains 96+/-3% capacity utilization over 30 redox cycles. Temperature-resolved in-situ X-ray diffraction reveals a chemical-vapor-transport-mediated self-foaming mechanism that redistributes W to refine the microstructure, complemented by a contact-barrier stabilization mechanism during high-temperature holds. Partial-capacity cycling up to 90 cycles further confirms sintering resistance under incomplete redox conditions. These results establish Fe-W powder beds as a robust, scalable, and compact platform for safe, stationary hydrogen storage.

### [15] [A Comparative Study of Structural Representations for 2D Materials: Insights from Dynamic Collision Fingerprint and Matminer](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.22950)
*Raphael M. Tromer,Isaac M. Felix,Rafael Besse,Marcelo L. Pereira Junior,Marcos G. E. da Luz*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 材料科学中，结构描述符的选择对机器学习协议的预测性能和物理可解释性有重要影响。复杂描述符虽可能提高数值精度，但会增加计算负担并降低结构信息的透明度。

Method: 研究采用动态碰撞指纹（Dynamic Collision Fingerprint, DCF）框架生成简洁的物理显著表示，通过原子结构的动态探测产生描述符。使用包含120个二维碳同素异形体的数据集，将DCF与广泛使用的Matminer库进行性能比较。

Result: DCF在所有学习算法（线性回归、决策树和XGBoost）中均能轻松匹配Matminer的预测精度，但使用的描述符维度显著更低，计算成本可控。相比技术性较强的Matminer描述，DCF展现出更清晰的物理可解释性。

Conclusion: DCF作为结构表示是高维描述符库的重要替代方案，兼具计算灵活性和物理基础性。这些发现表明DCF在保持预测性能的同时，通过降低维度和增强可解释性优化了机器学习协议。

Abstract: In materials science, the selection of structural descriptors for machine learning protocols strongly influences predictive performance and the degree of physical interpretability that can be achieved from the derived models. Although more complex descriptors may improve numerical accuracy, they often represent extra computational load, also reducing transparency into the underlying structural information. A framework called the Dynamic Collision Fingerprint (DCF) was recently proposed with the goal of producing concise, physically significant representations, generating descriptors via dynamical probing of atomic structures. In this work, we benchmark DCF using a dataset composed of 120 two-dimensional carbon allotropes and compare its performance with the widely considered Matminer library. The analysis employs three regression models, linear regression, decision tree, and XGBoost, evaluated over train and test partitions ranging from 10\% to 90\% and repeated over multiple random seeds in order to characterize statistical variability. The obtained results demonstrate that DCF easily matches Matminer in terms of predicting accuracy across all learning algorithms. However, it accomplishes this using descriptors that are significantly lower dimensional, pointing to manageable computing costs. Moreover, compared to the rather technical Matminer descriptions, the DCF exhibits considerably clearer physical interpretability. These findings suggest that DCF is a significant substitute for high-dimensional descriptor libraries as structural representation since it is both computationally flexible and physically grounded.

### [16] [Growth-controlled photochromism in yttrium oxyhydride thin films deposited by HiPIMS and pulsed-DC magnetron sputtering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.22951)
*M. Zubkins,E. Letko,E. Strods,V. Vibornijs,D. Moldarev,K. Sarakinos,K. Mizohata,K. Kundzins,J. Purans*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本研究比较了通过高功率脉冲磁控溅射（HiPIMS）和脉冲直流磁控溅射（pulsed-DCMS）制备的光致变色含氧钇氢化物（YHO）薄膜，发现溅射技术显著影响薄膜的光致变色性能、光学性质和微观结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在比较两种不同溅射技术——高功率脉冲磁控溅射（HiPIMS）和脉冲直流磁控溅射（pulsed-DCMS）——对含氧钇氢化物（YHO）薄膜的光致变色性能、光学性质和结构特性的影响。通过对比分析，探索薄膜生长条件与微观结构对光致变色性能的关键作用。

Method: 采用反应性高功率脉冲磁控溅射（HiPIMS）和反应性脉冲直流磁控溅射（pulsed-DCMS）技术沉积YHO薄膜。通过光学发射光谱（optical emission spectroscopy）分析等离子体特性，测量薄膜的光学透过率、光致变色对比度、光学带隙和晶格参数，并表征薄膜的晶体结构和取向。

Result: HiPIMS放电中钇离子（Y⁺）发射强烈，表明高钇电离度和自溅射再循环，而pulsed-DCMS以氩离子（Ar⁺）为主。获得透明光致变色薄膜所需的临界工作压力（Pc）在HiPIMS中更高（约1.0 Pa vs. 0.5 Pa）。pulsed-DCMS薄膜表现出更高的相对光致变色对比度（34% vs. 9%）和更低的光学带隙（2.70 eV vs. 2.94 eV），部分归因于其较低的氧氢原子比。结构上，HiPIMS薄膜多为多晶随机取向，而pulsed-DCMS薄膜呈现显著的<100>择优取向。

Conclusion: 研究结果表明，除了化学成分外，薄膜生长条件和微观结构对YHO薄膜的光致变色性能起着关键作用。不同溅射技术通过影响等离子体特性、薄膜组成和晶体取向，显著调控了薄膜的光致变色响应和光学性质。

Abstract: The present study investigates photochromic oxygen-containing yttrium hydride (YHO) thin films deposited by reactive high power impulse magnetron sputtering (HiPIMS) and compares their photochromic, optical, and structural properties with those of films synthesized by reactive pulsed direct current magnetron sputtering (pulsed-DCMS). Optical emission spectroscopy reveals that, unlike pulsed-DCMS where Ar$^{+}$ ions dominate, HiPIMS discharges are characterised by strong Y$^{+}$ emission, evidencing high yttrium ionisation and substantial self-sputter recycling. The critical working pressure (P$_c$) required to obtain transparent and photochromic films is higher for HiPIMS (Pc $\approx$ 1.0 Pa) than for pulsed-DCMS (Pc $\approx$ 0.5 Pa). Although films deposited near Pc exhibit similar solar transmittance (~72 %) and lattice parameters (5.38--5.39 Å), the pulsed-DCMS film shows a substantially higher relative photochromic contrast (34 %) and a lower optical band gap (2.70 eV) compared with the HiPIMS film (9 % contrast and 2.94 eV). This difference is partly attributed to a lower oxygen-to-hydrogen atomic ratio in the pulsed-DCMS film. Structurally, HiPIMS films are largely polycrystalline with random out-of-plane crystallographic orientation, whereas pulsed-DCMS films exhibit a pronounced <100> out-of-plane preferred orientation. These results demonstrate that, beyond composition, thin-film growth conditions and microstructure play a crucial role in governing the photochromic performance of YHO.

</details>


### [17] [Chalcogen Impurity Barriers in 2D Systems via Semi-Empirical/Machine Learning Modeling: A Survey over 4000 Materials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.22978)
*M. L. Pereira Junior,M. G. E. da Luz,P. Cesana,A. L. da Rosa,M. J. Piotrowski,D. Guedes-Sobrinho,T. A. S. Pereira,E. A. Moujaes,A. C. Dias,R. M. Tromer*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 具有低杂质吸附能垒的二维材料在催化、传感和表面功能化等应用中至关重要，但基于第一性原理（如密度泛函理论，DFT）的大规模筛选计算成本极高。因此，需要开发一种可扩展的、计算高效的方法来预测二维材料的吸附性能。

Method: 方法整合了半经验扩展休克尔方法（Extended Huckel Method, EHM）与机器学习技术。首先，使用EHM计算杂质沿三个面内迁移路径的能量分布，以推导平均能垒；杂质与二维表面的平衡距离通过一个简单的有效唯象表达式估算，而非耗时的几何优化。然后，从Matminer库中获取物理化学描述符，并测试了四种不同的机器学习模型，其中XGBoost表现最佳。最后，使用SHAP（SHapley Additive exPlanations）对预测结果进行可解释性分析。

Result: 研究结果表明，XGBoost模型在预测吸附能垒方面性能最优。通过SHAP分析验证了预测结果，重点关注了约1500种具有最低能垒值的材料。分析确认，平均价电子数、电负性和原子序数通常是验证机器学习模型的最相关属性。此外，研究还确定了针对不同硫族原子（S, Se, Te），哪些其他少数描述符同样显著影响吸附性能。

Conclusion: 当与可解释的机器学习协议结合时，扩展休克尔方法（EHM）能够构建一个可扩展的框架，用于筛选在各种应用中表现出所需捕获/释放动力学的二维结构。该方法为大规模、高效地预测和筛选二维材料的吸附性能提供了一条可行路径。

Abstract: Adequate characterization of two-dimensional materials with low energy barriers for impurity adsorption is key for advancing applications based on catalysis, sensing, and surface functionalization. However, first-principles methods, such as DFT, are often computationally extremely expensive for feasible large-scale screenings. Given such a scenario, we address a data-driven approach which integrates the semi-empirical Extended Huckel Method with machine learning techniques to estimate adsorption energy barriers in the case of three relevant chalcogen impurities, S, Se and Te. With this aim, we consider the 4036 2D materials found in the C2DB. The scheme employs the EHM to compute energy profiles along three in-plane migration paths, from which average barriers can be derived. The equilibrium distance between the impurity and the 2D surface is not calculated from a tie-consuming geometry optimization. Instead, it is estimated from a simple effective phenomenological expression. Physicochemical descriptors are then obtained from the Matminer library for curated features. Four different ML models are tested, with the XGBoost leading to the highest performance. We further use SHAP to verify the resulting predictions, focusing on the $\sim1,500$ materials displaying the lowest barrier values. As it could be anticipated, we establish that the average valence electron count, electronegativity, and atomic number are typically the most relevant attributes to validate the ML model. But we also are able to determine, for the different chalcogen atoms, which other few descriptors likewise considerably influence the adsorption properties. Our results show that when combined with interpretable ML protocols, EHM can produce a scalable framework for choosing 2D structures that exhibit the desired capture/release dynamics pertinent in a variety of utilization.

Abstract: All-solid-state lithium-ion batteries have renewed interest in high-performance solid electrolytes. Abstract: In this study, the influence of pure dislocation and hydrogen-dislocation interactions on anelastic response or internal friction relaxation peaks in bcc-iron was investigated. These relaxations are primarily governed by thermally activated kink nucleation and kink migration events. An atomistic multiscale framework, coupling molecular dynamics (MD) and kinetic Monte Carlo (KMC) simulations, was developed to investigate the underlying atomistic mechanisms behind dislocation-relaxation peaks. MD simulations revealed that the presence of hydrogen atoms near the dislocation core facilitates the kink nucleation process by reducing the nucleation barrier while enhancing the barrier for dislocation migration. The KMC model captured Snoek-Koster peaks arising from the Cottrell atmosphere formed by hydrogen atoms and clusters around the dislocation core, providing insights into the atomistic mechanisms controlling these relaxations. Furthermore, the proposed computational scheme elucidated a unique linear relationship between hydrogen content and the internal friction loss factor, offering a methodology for hydrogen detection and quantification.

### [23] [Landau level spectroscopy in current solid state physics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.23129)
*Ana Akrap,Milan Orlita*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文综述了朗道能级光谱学（Landau level spectroscopy）的基本原理及其在凝聚态物理中的应用，重点介绍了该技术在半导体、石墨烯系统和拓扑材料等现代材料体系中的扩展应用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 朗道能级光谱学在现代凝聚态物理中扮演重要角色，但传统应用主要局限于半导体和半金属。随着石墨烯、拓扑材料等新兴窄带隙或零带隙系统的出现，需要系统回顾该技术的基本原理及其在现代材料体系中的扩展应用。

Method: 采用文献综述方法，首先阐述朗道能级光谱学的基本原理，然后通过精选的文献案例进行说明。该技术通过在量子化磁场中探测固体中的电子，通常采用光学方法进行实验探测。

Result: 朗道能级光谱学能够提供晶体材料电子性质的直接详细洞察，特别是与能带结构相关的性质。该技术能够精确提取有效质量、载流子密度、迁移率和带隙等关键参数，并作为研究固体中电子与其他准粒子相互作用的强大工具。

Conclusion: 经过七十多年的发展，朗道能级光谱学的应用范围已从传统的半导体和半金属扩展到石墨烯基系统、拓扑材料的表面和体态，以及其他具有窄带隙或消失带隙的新兴系统，成为现代凝聚态物理研究的重要工具。

Abstract: Landau level spectroscopy plays an important role in modern condensed-matter physics. In this technique, electrons in a solid are subjected to quantizing magnetic fields and probed experimentally, often through optical methods. Direct and detailed insights into the electronic properties of crystalline materials are obtained, particularly the properties related to their band structure. Landau level spectroscopy enables the precise extraction of key parameters such as effective mass, carrier density, mobility, and band gap, and serves as a powerful tool for studying interactions between electrons and other quasiparticles in solids. Over its more than seventy-year history, Landau level spectroscopy has been applied mainly to semiconductors and semimetals. Today, its scope also includes graphene-based systems, surface and bulk states in topological materials, and other emergent systems with a narrow or vanishing band gap. In this work, we review the fundamentals of Landau level spectroscopy and illustrate them with selected examples from the literature.

### [29] [Coupling of the continuum and semiclassical limit. Part I: convergence of eigenvalues](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.23156)
*Matthias Keller,Lorenzo Pettinari,Christiaan J. F. van de Ven*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 该论文研究了d维薛定谔算子在网格离散化下的半经典极限和连续极限，证明了离散算子的所有特征值收敛到连续算子的特征值，并对谐振子情形给出了完整的谱渐近分析。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用网格离散化方法，将连续薛定谔算子离散在间距为1/N的网格上，并选择半经典参数λ_N = N^{1-γ}，其中γ∈(-1,1)，使N同时控制半经典极限和连续极限。

Result: 证明了当λ_N→∞时，离散算子的所有特征值收敛到连续算子的特征值。对于谐振子（harmonic oscillator）情形，进一步分析了γ∈ℝ\\(-1,1)时的谱渐近行为，完整刻画了所有γ值下的特征值行为。

Conclusion: 该研究完整描述了薛定谔算子在网格离散化下特征值的收敛行为，特别对谐振子情形给出了所有γ参数范围内的谱渐近特征，为半经典极限与连续极限同时存在时的数值分析提供了理论基础。

Abstract: We analyze the semiclassical $d$-dimensional Schrödinger operator in the continuum $ \frac{1}{2} Δ+ λ_N^2 V$ discretized on a mesh with spacing proportional to $1/N$. The semi-classical parameter $λ_N$ is chosen as $λ_N = N^{1 - γ}$, with $γ\in (-1,1)$, which ensures that $N$ governs both the semiclassical and continuum limit simultaneously. We prove that all eigenvalues of the discrete operator converge to those of the continuum, as $λ_N\to\infty$. Beyond this semi-classical domain, in the case of the harmonic oscillator, we further discuss the spectral asymptotics for $γ\in \mathbb{R} \setminus (-1,1)$, thereby fully characterizing the eigenvalue behavior across all possible values of $γ\in\mathbb{R}$.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用基于数据压缩的信息理论度量——可计算信息密度（computable information density, CID），作为分子动力学模拟中构型熵的即时通用测量方法。该方法通过验证从简单到复杂的系统来评估其有效性。

Abstract: Entropy governs molecular self-assembly, phase transitions, and material stability, yet remains challenging to quantify and directly control in molecular systems. Here, we demonstrate that the computable information density (CID), a data compression-based information theoretic metric, provides an instantaneous general measure of configurational entropy in molecular dynamics simulations, reflecting both local and long-range structural organization. We validate the CID across systems of increasing complexity, beginning with single-component Lennard-Jones melting before examining binary phase separation, polymer condensation and dispersion, and assembly of amorphous carbon networks at multiple densities. Unlike conventional order parameters, CID requires no a priori knowledge of relevant structural features and captures entropic signatures across a variety of molecular systems and discretization resolutions. By establishing entropy as a directly accessible structural metric, this framework lays a foundation for future entropy-driven materials design and optimization strategies.

### [32] [Mesoscopic fluctuation theory of particle systems driven by Poisson noise: study of the $q$-TASEP](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.23209)
*Alexandre Krajenbrink,Pierre Le Doussal*

TL;DR: 该论文研究一维KPZ普适类中q-TASEP模型的弱噪声理论，在q→1和大时间极限下识别出新的介观弱噪声区域，通过Fredholm行列式和鞍点场论两种方法获得粒子位置的大偏差，并证明了相关经典方程的可积性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用两种主要方法：首先通过q-TASEP的Fredholm行列式公式推导渐近行为；其次将弱噪声极限映射到半离散或全离散非线性微分方程系统，这些方程作为动力学场论的鞍点经典方程出现。论文还展示了这两个系统的经典可积性，并给出了显式的Lax对。

Result: 在q→1和大时间极限下识别出新的介观弱噪声区域，其中泊松噪声（Poisson noise）仍然重要。获得了给定粒子位置的大偏差，并证明了相关经典方程的可积性。对于连续时间q-TASEP模型，首次在随机系统中发现经典可积性，并解决了其Lax对的散射问题。

Abstract: We pursue our study of integrable weak noise theories of directed polymer and interacting particle stochastic models in the 1D KPZ universality class. Here we focus on the $q$-TASEP in either continuous or discrete time. Each particle on $\mathbb{Z}$ jumps independently by $+1$ with a rate (or probability) depending on the gap to the next particle on its right. We consider initial conditions (either step or random) which are empty of particles on $\mathbb{Z}^+$, and focus on the dynamics of the $N$ rightmost particles. In the limit $q \to 1$ and at large time (and large gaps) we identify a new intermediate "mesoscopic" (i.e. finite $N$) regime which corresponds to weak noise. In that regime Poisson noise remains important. We obtain the large deviations of the position of a given particle by two methods. The first derives asymptotics of $q$-TASEP Fredholm determinant formula. The second maps the weak noise limit to a system of semi-discrete or fully discrete, non linear differential equations. These are obtained as saddle point classical equations of a dynamical field theory, and their solutions represent the optimal configurations in the large deviation regime. We show the classical integrability of these two systems, and exhibit their explicit Lax pair. In the case of the continuous time $q$-TASEP it provides the first instance of classical integrability arising in a stochastic system, with signatures of the Poisson noise persisting in the weak noise limit. For this model, we solve the scattering problem associated to its Lax pair and fully characterize the large deviations associated to the weak noise theory. Finally, we supplement this work with an Appendix on the first cumulant method to obtain the large deviations of several lattice polymer models (Strict Weak, Log Gamma, Beta).

</details>


### [33] [Dephasing-induced relaxation in tight-binding chains with linear and nonlinear defects](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.22878)
*Debraj Das,Andrea Gambassi,Stefano Iubini,Stefano Lepri*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究分析了具有在位缺陷（on-site defect）的紧束缚链（tight-binding chain）在局域退相干噪声（local dephasing noise）下的热化（thermalization）过程。通过精确解析方法，揭示了缺陷诱导的局域模式（localized modes）作为瓶颈显著减缓弛豫，弛豫速率随缺陷强度呈ε^{-2}标度。研究还利用大偏差理论（large-deviation theory）表征了稀有动力学轨迹（rare dynamical trajectories），并发现了动力学相变（dynamical phase transition）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于理解具有在位缺陷的紧束缚链在局域退相干噪声作用下的热化过程。特别关注缺陷如何影响弛豫动力学，以及系统如何通过不同的弛豫路径（relaxation pathways）达到平衡态。

Method: 研究方法包括：对具有线性缺陷的系统进行精确解析分析，获得系统谱和本征态；在作用空间（action space）中推导近似动力学方程，描述连续时间随机游走（continuous-time random walk）；利用大偏差理论分析稀有动力学轨迹；最后将分析扩展到非线性缺陷情况，通过数值模拟研究非线性离散薛定谔方程（discrete Schrödinger equation）。

Result: 主要结果包括：缺陷诱导的局域模式作为瓶颈显著减缓弛豫，弛豫速率随缺陷强度呈ε^{-2}标度；通过大偏差理论识别了与作用空间中低活动和高活动机制相关的不同弛豫路径；数值证据表明大偏差函数在ε→∞极限下存在动力学相变；非线性缺陷导致更快的平衡趋近，源于振幅依赖的缺陷弱化效应。

Conclusion: 该研究为理解随机紧束缚系统中的热化、稀有涨落和弛豫路径提供了统一框架。结果表明缺陷结构对弛豫动力学有决定性影响，而非线性效应可通过振幅依赖的缺陷弱化加速平衡过程。

Abstract: We investigate thermalization in a tight-binding chain with an on-site defect subject to local dephasing noise implemented as random phase kicks. For a single linear defect of strength $ε$, we obtain an exact analytical description of the system spectrum and formulate the dephasing-induced dynamics in the eigenstate basis. We derive an approximate kinetic equation for mode populations that describes a continuous-time random walk in action space. The walk transition rates are defined by the overlap matrix encoding the spatial structure of eigenstates that can be computed exactly. Analyzing the spectral properties of the equation, we show that defect-induced localized modes act as bottlenecks that strongly slow down relaxation, with rates scaling as $ε^{-2}$ for strong defects. Using large-deviation theory, we characterize rare dynamical trajectories and identify distinct relaxation pathways associated with low- and high-activity regimes in action space. We provide numerical evidence that the large-deviation function exhibits a dynamical phase transition in the limit $ε\to \infty$. We then extend our analysis to the nonlinear case, considering a single nonlinear defect embedded in either a linear or a fully nonlinear discrete Schrödinger equation. Numerical simulations reveal a qualitatively faster approach to equilibrium driven by the amplitude-dependent weakening of the defect. Our results provide a unified framework for understanding thermalization, rare fluctuations, and relaxation pathways in stochastic tight-binding systems.

</details>


### [34] [Thermodynamic uncertainty relation under continuous measurement and feedback with quantum-classical-transfer entropy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.23110)
*Kaito Tojo,Takahiro Sagawa,Ken Funo*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究推导了量子连续测量与反馈控制下的热力学不确定性关系（thermodynamic uncertainty relation），通过引入量子-经典转移熵（quantum-classical-transfer entropy）量化测量获得的信息，证明了电流精度受熵产生（entropy production）和信息增益（information gain）等信息热力学成本的约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统热力学不确定性关系（TUR）为经典系统的电流精度设定了界限，但量子系统中连续测量与反馈控制的影响尚未充分探索。研究旨在将信息热力学成本纳入量子系统的精度约束框架。

Method: 引入量子-经典转移熵（quantum-classical-transfer entropy）来量化连续测量获得的信息，将其与熵产生（entropy production）结合，推导出量子连续测量与反馈控制下的热力学不确定性关系。采用受驱动的两能级系统（driven two-level system）作为示例进行验证。

Result: 研究结果表明，信息增益（information gain）能够突破传统热力学不确定性关系设定的界限，提升电流精度。在受驱动的两能级系统中，反馈控制实现了更高的电流精度，同时抑制了熵产生。

Conclusion: 量子连续测量与反馈控制下的热力学不确定性关系揭示了信息增益对电流精度的增强潜力，为量子热力学与信息处理的交叉研究提供了新视角，表明反馈控制可在降低热力学成本的同时提高测量精度。

Abstract: We derive a thermodynamic uncertainty relation (TUR) under quantum continuous measurement and feedback control. By incorporating the quantum-classical-transfer entropy, which quantifies the information gained by continuous measurement, we show that the precision of currents is constrained by information-thermodynamic costs such as the entropy production and information gain. Our result shows that information gain has the potential to enhance the precision of currents beyond the bounds set by the conventional TUR. We illustrate the bound with a driven two-level system under continuous measurement and feedback, demonstrating that feedback achieves higher precision of currents while suppressing the entropy production.

</details>


### [35] [Memory-induced active particle ratchets: Mean currents and large deviations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.23327)
*Venkata D. Pamulaparthy,Rosemary J. Harris*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究分析了具有随机方向反转的连续时间随机行走模型，发现即使没有外部势场，前进和后退等待时间分布的不对称性也能产生非零电流，从而构成一种活性粒子棘轮机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在探索在没有外部势场的情况下，仅通过方向反转机制和等待时间分布的不对称性如何产生定向输运，这为理解活性粒子棘轮（active particle ratchet）提供了理论框架。

Method: 采用连续时间随机行走（continuous-time random walk）模型，结合随机方向反转机制，并利用更新理论（renewal theory）框架分析大偏差（large deviations）行为。

Result: 当重定向时间呈指数分布时，推导出了平均棘轮电流的显式表达式；建立了通用更新理论框架以获得完整的大偏差特性，并据此讨论了动力学相变（dynamical phase transitions）的可能性。

Conclusion: 该模型展示了仅通过等待时间分布的不对称性即可产生定向输运，为活性粒子棘轮机制提供了理论解释，并揭示了可能的动力学相变现象。

Abstract: We analyse a continuous-time random walk model with stochastic reversals of direction. There is no external potential but the reorientation mechanism generates a non-zero current from asymmetry in the forward and backward waiting-time distributions (even when they have the same mean); the system can therefore can be considered as a type of active particle ratchet. We derive an explicit expression for the mean ratchet current with exponentially distributed reorientation times and also develop a general renewal-theory framework to obtain the full large deviations, using this to comment on the possibility of dynamical phase transitions.

</details>

J. Zhu,W. Z. Zhu,Y. C. Zhu,Z. A. Zhu,X. Y. Zhuang,M. Zhuge,J. H. Zou*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 首次观测到单卡比玻压低衰变Λ_c^+→Σ^0K_S^0π^+，并获得了Λ_c^+→Σ^0K_S^0K^+衰变的初步证据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究粲重子Λ_c^+的单卡比玻压低衰变（singly Cabibbo-suppressed decay）过程，以检验标准模型（Standard Model）中的弱相互作用机制和卡比玻混合（Cabibbo mixing）理论。

Method: 利用BESIII探测器在质心能量4.600-4.950 GeV范围内13个能量点收集的6.4 fb⁻¹积分亮度数据样本，通过统计显著性分析确定衰变分支比。

Result: 首次观测到Λ_c^+→Σ^0K_S^0π^+衰变，统计显著性达5.9σ，分支比为(0.58±0.14_stat±0.04_syst)×10⁻³；同时首次获得Λ_c^+→Σ^0K_S^0K^+衰变的证据，统计显著性为3.7σ。

Conclusion: 该研究成功观测到Λ_c^+的单卡比玻压低衰变模式，为理解粲重子衰变机制和检验标准模型提供了重要实验数据。

Abstract: Based on a data sample corresponding to an integrated luminosity of 6.4~fb$^{-1}$ of $e^+e^-$ annihilation and collected with the BESIII detector at 13 center-of-mass energy points ranging between 4.600~GeV and 4.950~GeV, we report the first observation of the singly Cabibbo-suppressed decay $Λ_c^+ \to Σ^0 K_S^0 π^+$ with a statistical significance of 5.9$σ$. The branching fraction is determined to be $\mathcal{B}(Λ_c^+ \to Σ^0 K_S^0 π^+) = (0.58 \pm 0.14_{\rm stat.} \pm 0.04_{\rm syst.}) \times 10^{-3}$. In addition, the decay $Λ_c^+\toΣ^0K_{S}^{0} K^+$ has also been investigated, and the first evidence for this decay is obtained with a statistical significance of 3.7$σ$.

</details>

The $p_{\rm T}$-differential production cross section of the $ψ(2S)$ and its ratio to the J/$ψ$ production cross section are presented. The results extend the accessible $p_{\rm T}$ range down to 4 GeV/$c$, and a mild rise of the $ψ(2S)$-to-J/$ψ$ cross section ratio with increasing $p_{\rm T}$ is observed. The measurements are compared with theoretical predictions based on NRQCD and the ICEM model.

### [38] [Measurement of the charged-particle-jet transverse-momentum fraction carried by prompt and non-prompt J/$ψ$ mesons in pp collisions at $\sqrt{s}=13$ TeV](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.22889)
*ALICE Collaboration*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: ALICE合作组在质子-质子对撞中测量了带电粒子喷注中prompt与非prompt J/ψ携带的横向动量分数z^ch，发现PYTHIA 8模拟在z^ch接近1时高估了孤立J/ψ的比例，反映了低动量喷注强子化模拟的挑战。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在测量带电粒子喷注中prompt与非prompt J/ψ介子携带的横向动量分数z^ch，以检验微扰QCD（pQCD）计算和PYTHIA 8模拟对喷注内部J/ψ产生机制的描述能力。

Method: 使用ALICE实验在质心能量√s=13 TeV下采集的数据，对应积分亮度1.63±0.03 pb^-1。通过电子-正电子衰变道重建J/ψ，利用底强子衰变的次级顶点区分prompt与非prompt成分。采用反-k_T算法（jet resolution parameter R=0.4）重建喷注，测量范围0.3<z^ch≤1.0，喷注横向动量7<p_T^jet<15 GeV/c。

Result: 测量了prompt与非prompt J/ψ的z^ch分布，并与pQCD计算和PYTHIA 8模拟比较。PYTHIA 8在z^ch<0.9时能定性再现数据，但当z^ch接近1时模拟高估了测量值，表明对孤立J/ψ比例的过高估计。

Conclusion: 数据与模拟在最高z^ch区间的差异反映了低动量喷注强子化（hadronization）模拟的挑战，提示当前模拟框架在描述高动量分数J/ψ产生机制方面存在局限性。

Abstract: The measurement of the transverse-momentum fraction ($z^{\rm ch}$) carried by prompt and non-prompt J/$ψ$ in charged-particle jets in proton--proton collisions with a center-of-mass energy $\sqrt{s}= 13$ TeV is reported by the ALICE Collaboration at the CERN Large Hadron Collider. Inclusive J/$ψ$ mesons with transverse momentum ($p_{\rm T}$) above 1 GeV/$c$ are reconstructed at midrapidity through the electron--positron decay channel. The prompt and non-prompt J/$ψ$ contributions are separated using the secondary vertices from beauty-hadron decays. The distribution of the charged-particle jet $p_{\rm T}$ fraction carried by the prompt and non-prompt J/$ψ$ mesons, $z^{\rm ch}$, is measured in the range $0.3 < z^{\rm ch} \leq 1.0$ for the jet-$ p_{\rm T}$ range $7 < p_{\rm T}^{\rm jet} < 15$ GeV/$c$. The measured $z^{\rm ch}$ distributions for prompt and non-prompt J/$ψ$ are compared to pQCD calculations and PYTHIA 8 simulations. Prompt and non-prompt J/$ψ$ production within charged-particle jets are found to be qualitatively well reproduced by PYTHIA 8 for $z^{\rm ch}<0.9$, however, as $z^{\rm ch}$ approaches one, the simulations overshoot the measured data, indicating an overestimation of the fraction of isolated J/$ψ$. This observed tension between data and simulations in the highest $z^{\rm ch}$ bins reflects the challenge of simulating hadronization of low-momentum jets.

The results are described by perturbative QCD calculations using different sets of parton distribution functions. The production of W$^{\pm}$ bosons and azimuthally correlated associated hadrons is also measured as a function of the charged-particle multiplicity for the first time at the LHC. The former increases approximately linearly with the charged-particle multiplicity, while for the latter, there are hints of a faster-than-linear increase. ### [40] [Understanding the impact of nuclear effects on proton decay searches with the GiBUU model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.23063)
*Qiyu Yan,Akira Takenaka,Kai Gallmeister,Xianguo Lu,Ulrich Mosel,Yangheng Zheng*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本研究利用GiBUU框架重新评估了质子衰变p→e⁺π⁰通道的探测灵敏度，特别关注了核效应和系统不确定性对下一代水切伦科夫探测器（如Hyper-Kamiokande）质子衰变搜索的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 下一代水切伦科夫探测器（如Hyper-Kamiokande）的质子衰变搜索预计将探测到10³⁵年寿命区域，其中大气中微子背景和系统不确定性开始发挥越来越重要的作用。需要更精确地评估核效应对信号探测效率和背景率的影响。

Method: 采用GiBUU框架，结合水切伦科夫探测器的典型事件重建性能，重新评估质子衰变p→e⁺π⁰通道的搜索灵敏度。GiBUU框架实现了经过加速器中微子散射数据（特别是π介子产生）基准测试的复杂模型，包括平均场势（mean-field potential）和玻尔兹曼输运（Boltzmann transport）。

Result: 质子衰变信号探测效率和大气中微子背景率与当前和近期水切伦科夫实验使用临时核模型（ad hoc nuclear models）评估的结果相当。π介子末态相互作用（pion final-state interactions）的不确定性适中，而费米动量分布（Fermi momentum distribution）的选择会显著影响估计的大气中微子背景率，构成主要贡献因素。

Conclusion: 该研究提供了质子衰变搜索中核效应的独立且互补的表征，有助于在系统不确定性变得更加相关的区域中改进灵敏度估计。特别强调了费米动量分布作为主要系统不确定性来源的重要性。

Abstract: Proton decay searches in the next generation of water Cherenkov detectors, such as Hyper-Kamiokande, are expected to probe the $10^{35}$-year lifetime regime where atmospheric neutrino backgrounds and systematic uncertainties begin to play an increasingly important role. In this study, we employ the GiBUU framework and reevaluate the proton decay search sensitivity for the $\textrm{p}\rightarrow\textrm{e}^{+}π^{0}$ channel by incorporating a typical event reconstruction performance in water Cherenkov detectors. Using sophisticated models implemented in GiBUU -- most notably the mean-field potential and Boltzmann transport -- which have been benchmarked against accelerator neutrino scattering data, in particular pion production, we find that the resulting proton decay signal detection efficiency and atmospheric neutrino background rate are comparable to those previously evaluated for the current and near future water Cherenkov experiments using $\textit{ad hoc}$ nuclear models. In addition to pion final-state interactions, we evaluate the impact of differences in the Fermi momentum distribution of nucleons in the nucleus, as a source of systematic uncertainty, on the signal detection efficiency and the expected background event rate. We find that the uncertainty associated with pion final-state interactions is moderate, whereas the choice of Fermi momentum distribution can significantly affect the estimated atmospheric neutrino background rate and constitutes the dominant contribution. Our study provides an independent and complementary characterisation of nuclear effects on proton decay searches and helps to refine sensitivity estimates in the regime where systematic uncertainties become more relevant.

### [41] [Real-Time Stream Compaction for Sparse Machine Learning on FPGAs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.23281)
*Marc Neu,Isabel Haide,Torben Ferber,Jürgen Becker*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着机器学习算法（特别是图神经网络）在对撞机实验第一级触发器中的广泛应用，基于FPGA的触发器硬件需求已超出当前技术水平。为满足高吞吐量和低延迟环境的严格要求，需要解决稀疏传感器数据处理的效率问题。

Method: 提出了一种延迟优化的稀疏数据预处理概念，将来自大量FIFO接口的传感器前端数据重新排列到较少数量的FIFO接口，连接至机器学习硬件加速器。开发了针对FPGA优化的分层稀疏压缩流水线（hierarchical sparsity compression pipeline），并使用Chisel设计语言实现为开源硬件生成器。

Result: 在Belle II探测器的电磁量能器（Electromagnetic Calorimeter）中，将该模块的一个配置实现为基于GNN的第一级触发器的预处理阶段。评估了广泛参数范围内的延迟、吞吐量、资源利用率和可扩展性，证明了该方法的有效性。

Conclusion: 所提出的延迟优化预处理方法能够有效支持图神经网络硬件加速，满足对撞机实验第一级触发器的严格要求，并具有适用于其他大规模科学实验的广泛潜力。

Abstract: Machine learning algorithms are being used more frequently in the first-level triggers in collider experiments, with Graph Neural Networks pushing the hardware requirements of FPGA-based triggers beyond the current state of the art. To meet the stringent demands of high-throughput and low-latency environments, we propose a concept for latency-optimized preprocessing of sparse sensor data, enabling efficient GNN hardware acceleration by removing dynamic input sparsity. Our approach rearranges data coming from a large number of First-In-First-Out interfaces, typically sensor frontends, to a smaller number of FIFO interfaces connected to a machine learning hardware accelerator. In order to achieve high throughput while minimizing the hardware utilization, we developed a hierarchical sparsity compression pipeline optimized for FPGAs. We implemented our concept in the Chisel design language as an open-source hardware generator. For demonstration, we implemented one configuration of our module as preprocessing stage in a GNN-based first-level trigger for the Electromagnetic Calorimeter inside the Belle II detector. Additionally we evaluate latency, throughput, resource utilization, and scalability for a wide range of parameters, to enable broader use for other large scale scientific experiments.

### [42] [Generically sharp decay and blowing up at infinity for a weak null wave system](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.22749)
*Shijie Dong,Siyuan Ma,Yue Ma,Xu Yuan*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 该论文研究了满足弱零条件（weak null condition）的半线性波动方程组，建立了小数据解精确的点态衰减估计，证明了这些估计的尖锐性，并展示了能量无限增长和能量级联现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究满足弱零条件（weak null condition）的半线性波动方程组，该方程组可作为爱因斯坦真空方程（Einstein vacuum equations）的简化模型。主要目标是建立小数据解的精确点态衰减估计，包括衰减的上界和下界。

Method: 通过分析半线性波动方程组（semilinear wave equations）满足弱零条件的情况，建立解与其主导项（leading-order term）之间的差异估计。特别关注解在延迟时间变量（retarded time variable）$u=t-r$中的衰减行为。

Result: 证明了小数据解的点态衰减估计是尖锐的（sharp），适用于一类衰减足够快的初始数据。解与其主导项的差异由低阶项（lower-order terms）主导，这些项在延迟时间变量中衰减更快。

Conclusion: 这些衰减估计的应用表明，解的一个分量能量存在下界，该下界通常随时间增长至无穷大，可解释为"在无穷远处爆破（blowing up at infinity）"。此外，该分量通常表现出从高频到低频的能量级联（energy cascade）现象。

Abstract: We study a system of semilinear wave equations satisfying the weak null condition, which can be regarded as a simplified model for the Einstein vacuum equations. The main objective is to establish precise pointwise decay estimates, as both lower and upper bounds of decay, for small data solutions. Specifically, we show that the difference between the solution and its leading-order term is dominated by lower-order terms that decay faster in the retarded time variable $u=t-r$. Moreover, we prove that these pointwise decay estimates are sharp for a generic class of small initial data decaying sufficiently fast.
  As applications of these estimates, we demonstrate that the energy of one component of the solution admits a lower bound that generically grows to infinity as $t\to +\infty$, which can be interpreted as ``blowing up at infinity." Furthermore, we verify that this component generically exhibits an energy cascade from high to low frequencies.

</details>


### [43] [Long-time propagation of coherent states in a normally hyperbolic setting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.22834)
*Roméo Taboada*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种在半经典极限下描述相干态演化的方法，将近似有效性从对数时间尺度扩展到更长时间，特别是Ehrenfest时间尺度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在扩展Combescure和Robert关于相干态演化的成果，解决在长时间尺度（特别是Ehrenfest时间）下近似失效的问题。主要动机是突破现有方法的时间限制，提供更长时间有效的波包演化描述。

Method: 采用混合描述方法：在横截方向使用WKB态（WKB states），沿慢变子流形K使用压缩相干态（squeezed coherent states）。该方法要求经典动力学流Φ_t在横截方向具有双曲性，并在K邻域内满足法向双曲不变子流形条件。

Result: 成功将近似有效性扩展到Ehrenfest时间尺度（|log h|/(2λ_0)），突破了原有压缩态描述的时间限制（|log h|/(6λ_0)）。演化后的波包不再局域于单个点，而是局域于各向同性子流形（isotropic submanifold）。

Conclusion: 长时间尺度下半经典相干态演化需要混合描述框架，结合WKB方法和压缩态技术。该方法与Guillemin、Uribe和Wang提出的各向同性子流形局域波函数类相似，为长时间量子演化提供了更精确的数学描述。

Abstract: We present a method to find asymptotics for the evolution of coherent states (or Gaussian wavepackets with standard deviation $\sqrt{h}$) under semiclassical Schrödinger's equation for a given Hamiltonian. These results extend the work of Combescure and Robert, in which the evolution of coherent states can be approximated in the limit $h\to 0$ with deformed Gaussian wavepackets called squeezed coherent states. The description with squeezed states holds for times $t$ that can go to infinity as $h\to 0$, under the constraint $|t|\leq |\log h|/(6λ_0)$ where $λ_0$ is the maximal Lyapunov exponent of the classical dynamics. The breakdown of this approximation at time $|\log h|/(6λ_0)$ is related to the bending of evolved wavepackets: once propagated states spread at a scale $h^{1/3}$, squeezed states no longer provide an appropriate description. To obtain a representation of propagated states valid up to times $|t|\leq C|\log h|$ with a larger $C$ (for instance, up to Ehrenfest's time $|\log h|/(2λ_0)$ where spreading on macroscopic scales is allowed), we make additional assumptions on the flow $Φ_t$ associated to the classical dynamics, imposing constraints on directions of elongation. Namely, we work in a neighborhood of a normally hyperbolic $Φ_t$-invariant submanifold $K$, on which the dynamics is considered as slow in comparison with its transverse directions, along which $Φ_t$ is assumed to be hyperbolic. In this context, we describe the propagated state as a WKB state in transverse directions and a squeezed state along $K$. This description emphasizes the fact that propagated states should no longer be thought of as microlocalized on a point, but rather on an isotropic submanifold (corresponding to transverse unstable directions). Guillemin, Uribe, and Wang presented a similar class of wavefunctions microlocalized on an isotropic submanifold.

</details>

### [44] [Phononic enhancement and detection of hidden spin-nematicity and dynamics in quantum magnets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.22283)
*Junyu Tang,Hong-hao Song,Gang v. Chen*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种通过声子谱检测量子磁体中自旋向列相（spin nematic phase）的新方法，利用自旋-晶格耦合在声子谱中产生特征信号，为多极序的诊断开辟了新途径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自旋向列相（spin nematic phase）具有长程自旋四极矩序但缺乏偶极磁性，这使其难以通过传统实验方法检测。该研究旨在解决这一检测难题。

Method: 研究提出了一种新颖的检测方法，以自旋-1三角晶格莫特绝缘体（spin-1 triangular lattice Mott insulator）为例进行说明。通过积分掉声子自由度（phonon degrees of freedom），获得了包含自旋向列相和自旋向列-超固态相（spin-nematic-supersolid phases）显著扩大的相图。

Result: 研究证明，通过自旋-晶格耦合（spin-lattice coupling），自旋向列序的出现会在声子谱中留下独特的特征信号。这种光谱特征可通过拉曼散射（Raman）或非弹性X射线散射（inelastic X-ray scattering）进行探测。

Conclusion: 该形式化方法为揭示隐藏的自旋向列性（spin nematicity）提供了一种直接而强大的工具，为诊断量子磁体中的多极序（multipolar orders）开辟了新的途径。

Abstract: The spin nematic phase, characterized by long-range order of spin quadrupole moments in the absence of dipolar magnetism, presents a significant challenge for conventional experimental detection. We propose a novel method to detect this elusive order in quantum magnets with an illustration in the spin-1 triangular lattice Mott insulator. By integrating out the phonon degrees of freedom, we obtain a phase diagram with substantially enlarged regions for the spin-nematic and spin-nematic-supersolid phases. We then demonstrate that through the spin-lattice coupling, the emergence of spin nematic order imprints a distinctive signature onto the phonon spectra, providing a clear spectroscopic signature for the quadrupolar order accessible via Raman or inelastic X-ray scattering. Our formalism offers a direct and powerful method to uncover the hidden spin nematicity, opening a new pathway for diagnosing multipolar orders in quantum magnets.

</details>


### [45] [Atomic-Scale Quantum Control of Single Spin Defects in a Two-Dimensional Semiconductor](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.22301)
*Kwan Ho Au-Yeung,Wantong Huang,Johanna Matusche,Paul Greule,Jonas Arnold,Lovis Hardeweg,Máté Stark,Luise Renz,Affan Safeer,Daniel Jansen,Thomas Michely,Jeison Fischer,Wolfgang Wernsdorfer,Christoph Sürgers,Hannu-Pekka Komsa,Johannes Schwenk,Wouter Jolie,Philip Willke*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 固体中的单个自旋缺陷是量子技术的有前景构建单元，但其确定性创建、单独寻址和表面附近操作仍是主要挑战。二维材料因其单层厚度可直接原子尺度访问缺陷态，提供了有吸引力的替代方案。

Method: 研究结合扫描隧道显微镜（scanning tunneling microscopy, STM）和电子自旋共振（electron spin resonance, ESR）技术，在单层二硫化钼（molybdenum disulfide）中创建和操控硫空位（sulfur vacancies）和碳替代缺陷（carbon substitution defects）。通过原子操控（atomic manipulation）进一步设计和探测缺陷对之间的自旋-自旋相互作用。

Result: 实现了单缺陷水平的自旋动力学表征，包括相干控制（coherent control）。成功展示了单个自旋缺陷的确定性创建、寻址、相干操控和可控耦合，所有功能均集成于单一实验平台中。

Conclusion: 该工作确立了二维半导体中原子工程自旋缺陷作为一类多功能可控固态量子系统，并为定制化量子传感实验开辟了新途径。

Abstract: Individual spin defects in solids are promising building blocks for quantum technologies, but their deterministic creation, individual addressability, and operation near surfaces remain major challenges. Two-dimensional materials provide an attractive alternative, as their single-layer thickness enables direct atomic-scale access to defect states. Here, we demonstrate single-spin control of solid-state defects in a two-dimensional semiconductor by a combination of scanning tunneling microscopy and electron spin resonance. We create and manipulate individual sulfur vacancies and carbon substitution defects in monolayer molybdenum disulfide and characterize their spin dynamics, including coherent control, at the single-defect level. Using atomic manipulation, we further engineer and probe spin-spin interactions between defect pairs. Our results demonstrate deterministic creation, addressability, coherent manipulation, and controlled coupling of individual spin defects within a single experimental platform. This establishes atomically engineered spin defects in two-dimensional semiconductors as a versatile class of controllable solid-state quantum systems and opens a route towards tailored quantum sensing experiments.

### [46] [The Anyon Zeno Effect](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.22322)
*David F. Mross*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了在分数量子霍尔干涉实验中，通过测量流持续观测任意子（anyons）会产生量子芝诺效应（quantum Zeno effect），导致局域任意子被捕获，其隧穿率受到抑制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在探索在分数量子霍尔干涉实验中，通过测量两个相互环绕的任意子获得的量子化编织相位（braiding phase）如何影响任意子动力学，特别是如何通过实验控制任意子的寿命。

Method: 研究采用理论分析方法，聚焦于嵌入反点（antidot）的干涉仪，该结构可进入芝诺区域（Zeno regime），其中局域任意子的裸隧穿率远低于测量率。

Result: 研究发现量子芝诺效应会抑制被捕获任意子的隧穿率，该抑制程度取决于编织相位和量子点接触（quantum point contacts）的传输特性。主要预测是干涉仪电导的自相关时间会随偏置电流增加而增加。

Conclusion: 该效应可用于实验控制任意子动力学，特别是延长局域任意子的寿命，为分数量子霍尔系统中任意子的操纵提供了新途径。

Abstract: Two anyons encircling each other acquire a quantized braiding phase that is independent of their spatial separation. We show that detecting this phase in a fractional quantum Hall interference experiment results in a quantum Zeno effect: a localized anyon is trapped by constant observation from a stream of anyons supplied by the measurement current. Interferometers with an embedded antidot are ideal for accessing the Zeno regime, where the bare tunneling rate of localized anyons is much lower than the measurement rate. The Zeno-suppressed tunneling rate of the trapped anyon depends on the braiding phase and the transmission of the quantum point contacts. Our primary prediction is that the autocorrelation time of the conductance through the interferometer increases with the bias current. This effect may be used to experimentally control the anyon dynamics, in particular to increase the lifetime of localized anyons.

</details>


### [47] [Resonant Zener Interferometry in van der Waals Heterostructures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.22328)
*Nisarga Paul,Gil Refael*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在探索范德华异质结在面内电场作用下的量子干涉现象，为相干干涉动力学提供直接可观测的探针，并实现更精确的工程设计和表征。

Method: 通过施加面内电场F加速载流子通过杂化带边，利用层间齐纳隧穿（Zener tunneling）的不同路径构建固态量子干涉仪，并分析其在输运观测量中的表现。

Result: 在抛物线型双层结构中识别出两个特征信号：小场下周期为1/F的朗道-齐纳-施特克尔伯格振荡（Landau-Zener-Stuckelberg oscillations），以及由层间隧穿T0决定的共振峰（F∝T0^{3/2}）。

Conclusion: 这些特征为范德华异质结中的相干干涉动力学提供了直接可访问的探针，可用于更精确的工程设计和表征。

Abstract: We demonstrate the presence of quantum interference effects in van der Waals heterostructures subject to in-plane electric fields. The in-plane field $F$ accelerates carriers through a hybridized band edge, and interlayer Zener tunneling occurs by distinct pathways, resulting in a solid-state quantum interferometer with imprints in transport observables. For parabolic-band bilayers, we identify two characteristic signatures which are observable in lateral conductance: Landau-Zener-Stuckelberg oscillations in the band-overlap regime periodic in $1/F$ at small fields, resembling electric-field induced quantum oscillations, and a pronounced resonance at $F\propto T_0^{3/2}$ set by the interlayer tunneling $T_0$. These features provide a directly accessible probe of coherent interferometric dynamics in van der Waals heterostructures, and could be harnessed for more precise engineering and characterization.

### [48] [First-principles and tight-binding analysis of thermoelectricity in irradiated WSe$_2$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.22789)
*Cynthia Ihuoma Osuala,Tanu Choudhary,Raju K. Biswas,Sudin Ganguly,Santanu K. Maiti*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究在单色光照射下分析了锯齿形单层WSe₂纳米带的电子和热电输运特性，通过Floquet理论处理周期性驱动，结合密度泛函微扰理论计算晶格热导率，发现光诱导的跳跃重整化与自旋轨道耦合协同作用，可在宽温区内使热电优值ZT超过1。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在探索单色光照射对锯齿形单层WSe₂纳米带电子和热电输运特性的影响，特别是通过周期性驱动调控材料性能，为光控热电材料设计提供理论基础。

Method: 采用六轨道紧束缚框架描述电子结构，包含钨和硒轨道及原子自旋轨道耦合；通过Peierls substitution处理周期性驱动，在高频极限下映射到有效静态Floquet Hamiltonian；使用Landauer-Büttiker formalism中的波函数匹配方法评估相干输运；结合密度泛函微扰理论和声子玻尔兹曼输运方程的迭代解计算晶格热导率。

Result: 光诱导的跳跃重整化重塑了费米能级附近的能带色散和透射谱，改变了决定电导、热导和塞贝克系数的Landauer输运积分；结合自旋轨道驱动的能带分裂和增强的非谐散射导致的晶格热导率降低，使得热电优值ZT在宽温度范围内超过1。

Conclusion: 周期性光照射通过Floquet工程有效调控WSe₂纳米带的电子和热电输运特性，光诱导的跳跃重整化与自旋轨道耦合协同作用显著提升热电性能，为光控热电材料的设计提供了新途径。

Abstract: Electronic and thermoelectric transport in zigzag monolayer WSe$_2$ nanoribbons are studied under monochromatic irradiation. The electronic structure is described within a six-orbital tight-binding framework constructed from the relevant tungsten and selenium orbitals, with atomic spin-orbit coupling included explicitly. Periodic driving is incorporated via the Peierls substitution, and in the high-frequency limit the system is mapped onto an effective static Floquet Hamiltonian with polarization-dependent renormalized hoppings. Coherent transport is evaluated using wave-function matching within the Landauer-Büttiker formalism. The lattice thermal conductivity is obtained independently from density functional perturbation theory combined with an iterative solution of the phonon Boltzmann transport equation. Light-induced hopping renormalization reshapes the band dispersion and transmission spectrum near the Fermi level, modifying the Landauer transport integrals that determine electrical and thermal conductances and the Seebeck coefficient. Together with spin-orbit-driven band splitting and reduced lattice thermal conductivity from enhanced anharmonic scattering, this leads to a thermoelectric figure of merit $ZT$ exceeding unity over a broad temperature range.

### [50] [Dimensional and doping stability of Peierls charge density waves](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.23208)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究采用有限厚度相同链阵列模型，分析平行耦合链（parallel-coupled chains）和斜耦合链（skew-coupled chains）两种堆叠几何结构。通过考察掺杂、晶格刚度和链间耦合几何等参数对系统相图的影响。

Result: 平行耦合链表现出双稳态区域，其中正常态和二聚化态作为总能量的局部最小值共存；而斜耦合链在掺杂时显示出重入型电荷密度波序。结果表明堆叠几何结构对远离半填充时的CDW序稳定化起决定性作用。

Conclusion: 即使是最简单的耦合原子链模型，其相图也受到掺杂、晶格刚度和链间耦合几何结构的丰富控制。该研究揭示了堆叠几何在决定耦合一维系统电子相行为中的关键作用。

Abstract: The Peierls instability, the spontaneous dimerization of a one-dimensional metallic chain at half filling, is a paradigmatic mechanism for charge-density-wave (CDW) formation. Here we test its robustness under finite doping and interchain hybridization in finite-thickness arrays of identical chains. We find that the stacking geometry plays a decisive role in stabilizing CDW order away from half filling. In particular, parallel-coupled chains exhibit a bistable regime where the normal and dimerized states coexist as local minima of the total energy, while skew-coupled chains display reentrant CDW order upon doping. Our results demonstrate that even minimal models of coupled atomic chains host rich phase diagrams controlled by doping, lattice rigidity, and interchain coupling geometry.

### [51] [Extrinsic Spin Splitter Currents in Altermagnets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.23273)
*Sanjay Sarkar,Sayan Sarkar,Amit Agarwal*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究建立了反铁磁体（altermagnets）中线性外禀自旋分裂电流的统一半经典理论，揭示了不对称杂质散射是自旋分裂效应的主要机制，并在FeSb2材料中验证了该理论。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 反铁磁体（altermagnets）具有动量依赖的自旋分裂特性，但净磁化强度为零，这使其能够产生自旋分裂效应（spin-splitter effect），即外部电场通过分离相反极化的载流子产生横向自旋电流。然而，此前对自旋分裂响应的研究主要集中于对称散射机制。

Method: 研究发展了线性外禀自旋分裂电流（linear extrinsic spin-splitter currents）的统一半经典理论（unified semiclassical theory），包含了杂质诱导的侧向跳跃（side-jump）和偏斜散射（skew-scattering）贡献，并将该理论应用于d波反铁磁体FeSb2。

Result: 研究表明，不对称杂质散射（asymmetric impurity scattering）为自旋分裂电流提供了主要通道。值得注意的是，由此产生的外禀自旋电导率（extrinsic spin conductivity）是时间反演偶的（time-reversal even），这与先前研究的对称散射产生的自旋分裂响应形成对比。

Conclusion: 不对称杂质散射在反铁磁体的自旋分裂效应中起主导作用，且其外禀自旋电导率具有时间反演偶特性，这为理解和调控反铁磁体中的自旋输运提供了新的理论框架。

Abstract: Altermagnets exhibit momentum-dependent spin splitting despite having zero net magnetization. This enables a spin-splitter effect in which an external electric field generates transverse spin currents by separating oppositely polarized carriers. Here, we develop a unified semiclassical theory of linear extrinsic spin-splitter currents, incorporating impurity-induced side-jump and skew-scattering contributions, and apply it to the $d$-wave altermagnet \ch{FeSb2}. We demonstrate that asymmetric impurity scattering provides a dominant channel for spin-splitter currents. Remarkably, the resulting extrinsic spin conductivity is time-reversal even, in contrast to previously studied spin-splitter responses arising from symmetric scattering.

</details>


### [52] [Electromechanical Switching and Momentum-Selective Transport in Geometry-Defined Blue Phosphorus Homojunctions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.23298)
*Zewen Wu,Min Zhou,Yanxia Xing,Xianghua Kong*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究报道了一种在双层蓝磷（BlueP）中通过局域气泡褶皱形成的几何定义金属-半导体-金属同质结，无需化学掺杂或异质界面，并展示了其在机电开关器件中的应用潜力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 开发不依赖化学异质性的本征同质结是未来二维器件发展的关键挑战。传统方法通常需要化学掺杂或异质材料界面，而本工作旨在探索通过纯几何结构调控实现金属-半导体转变的新途径。

Method: 采用第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）研究双层蓝磷中增大层间距对能带结构的影响，并通过第一性原理量子输运模拟（first-principles quantum-transport simulations）分析气泡形成后的输运行为转变。

Result: 在金属性A₁B₁堆叠的双层蓝磷中，增大层间距会打开带隙，形成嵌入金属段之间的半导体势垒。输运模拟显示从弹道输运到隧穿输运的转变，传输率随气泡宽度指数衰减但对高度和膨胀方向不敏感。该结具有取向依赖的k空间滤波功能，产生输运各向异性和动量选择性。

Conclusion: 轨道分辨散射分析表明层内键合通道在形变下持续存在而层间杂化通道被抑制，σ型键合比π型键合具有更高电导。这些发现启发了两种机电器件概念：开关比达30的机械可切换存储元件和用于Å尺度位移传感的可重复指数电阻调谐纳米滑动变阻器。

Abstract: Developing intrinsic homojunctions without chemical heterogeneity remains a key challenge in future two - dimensional devices. Here, we report a geometry - defined metal--semiconductor--metal homojunction in bilayer blue phosphorus (BlueP) created by a localized bubble corrugation, without chemical doping or foreign - material interfaces. First - principles calculations show that enlarging the interlayer separation in the metallic A\(_1\)B\(_1\) - stacked BlueP bilayer opens a band gap, enabling a semiconducting barrier embedded between metallic segments. First - principles quantum - transport simulations reveal a crossover from ballistic to tunneling transport upon bubble formation. In the tunneling regime, transmission decreases exponentially with bubble width while remaining weakly sensitive to bubble height and bulging direction. The junction acts as an orientation - dependent \(k\) - space filter, producing transport anisotropy and momentum selectivity. Orbital - resolved scattering analysis shows that intralayer - bonding channels persist under deformation whereas interlayer - hybridized channels are quenched, and that σ- type bonding yields higher conductance than π- type bonding. These insights motivate two electromechanical device concepts: a mechanically switchable memory element with ON/OFF ratios up to 30 and a nanoscale sliding rheostat with reproducible exponential resistance tuning for Å- scale displacement sensing.

### [53] [Conformal symmetry in force-free electrodynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.22262)
*Huiquan Li,Jianyong Wang*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文证明了在闵可夫斯基时空中的无力电动力学（force-free electrodynamics, FFE）存在共形对称性（conformal symmetry）。该对称性通过莫比乌斯变换（Möbius transformations）实现，揭示了已知解之间的结构联系，并将磁层视界（magnetospheric horizon）内部区域映射到其对偶解的外部区域。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 无力电动力学是描述天体周围磁层的基础框架，其中电荷沿磁力线运动且不受洛伦兹力作用。然而，当存在源时，一般的保角共形映射（angle-preserving conformal mapping）不一定产生物理上可接受的无力场配置。本研究旨在探索在特定条件下这种不变性是否仍然存在。

Method: 通过分析无力电动力学在闵可夫斯基时空中的数学结构，证明控制流方程（governing stream equation）在莫比乌斯变换下保持不变。该方法聚焦于特定自由函数的选择，以揭示共形对称性的存在条件。

Result: 研究证实了无力电动力学中存在共形对称性，具体表现为控制流方程在莫比乌斯变换下的不变性。这一对称性建立了已知解之间的结构联系，特别地，它将一个解的磁层视界（lightsurface）内部区域映射到其对偶解的外部区域，反之亦然。

Conclusion: 无力电动力学在特定条件下具有共形对称性，这一发现通过莫比乌斯变换的不变性得以证明。该对称性不仅揭示了不同解之间的深层结构关系，还提供了磁层视界内外区域之间的对偶映射，为无力磁层理论提供了新的数学洞察。

Abstract: It is shown that conformal symmetry exists in force-free electrodynamics (FFE) in Minkowski spacetime, a foundational framework for describing magnetospheres around astronomical objects. In force-free magnetospheres, charges are constrained to move along magnetic field lines and experience zero Lorentz force, due to the everywhere perpendicular orientation of electric and magnetic fields. However, a general angle-preserving conformal mapping of force-free fields does not necessarily produce another physically admissible force-free configuration when sources are present. In this work, we demonstrate that such invariance can nevertheless arise for certain choices of the free functions. Specifically, the governing stream equation is shown to be invariant under Möbius transformations. This symmetry reveals a structural linkage between known solutions and, notably, maps the region inside a magnetospheric horizon (the lightsurface) of one solution to the exterior of its dual counterpart, and vice versa.

</details>

Result: 研究发现温度呈现非单调行为，相变依赖于模型参数。完美流体暗物质和弦云参数显著影响阴影半径和强场结构。有效势能、比能量和角动量分析揭示了粒子运动的稳定性条件，准周期振荡频率编码了可观测的天体物理特征。

Abstract: The Dymnikova black hole represents a regular spacetime solution interpolating between a de Sitter core and an asymptotically Schwarzschild geometry. In this work, we investigate a generalized Dymnikova black hole surrounded by perfect fluid dark matter (PFDM) and immersed in a cloud of strings (CS). We analyze how these additional matter sources modify the thermodynamic, optical, and dynamical properties of the spacetime.
  We derive the Hawking temperature and specific heat capacity and examine the thermal stability and phase structure of the black hole. The results reveal non-monotonic temperature behavior and parameter-dependent phase transitions. We further study photon dynamics, including the photon sphere and black hole shadow, and show that both PFDM and string cloud parameters significantly affect the shadow radius and strong-field structure.
  Additionally, we investigate the motion of massive test particles, circular orbits, and stability conditions. The corresponding effective potentials, specific energy, and angular momentum are analyzed. Finally, we explore quasi-periodic oscillations (QPOs) by computing the fundamental epicyclic frequencies and discuss how the model parameters encode observable astrophysical signatures.

*Ze-Xuan Xiong,H. Lu*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 研究发现了一个非平凡积分常数可以从近奇点几何中提取，并揭示了一个普遍模式：在大质量极限下，该积分常数渐近趋于质量与标量荷的线性组合。此外，研究还发现可能存在一个黑洞上界，限制了有质量粒子在落入Kasner奇点前能在黑洞内生存的最长时间，且史瓦西黑洞（Schwarzschild black hole）达到了这个上界。

Conclusion: 结论表明，渐近信息（质量与标量荷）显著影响Kasner奇点的性质，包括Kasner指数。研究揭示了大质量极限下积分常数与渐近参数的线性关系，并提出了关于有质量粒子在黑洞内生存时间的可能上界，其中史瓦西黑洞是达到该上界的特例。

Abstract: We study the spacelike Kasner singularity of spherically-symmetric, static and asymptotically flat black holes in Einstein gravity minimally coupled to a massless scalar with a suitable self-interacting scalar potential. We focus on how the asymptotic information such as the mass and scalar charge affect the properties of the Kasner singularity, including the Kasner exponents. We show how a nontrivial integration constant can be extracted from the near-singularity geometry and find a general pattern that this integration constant asymptotes to a linear combination of the mass and scalar charge at large mass limit. We also find that there may be a black hole upper bound on the maximum surviving time of a massive particle inside such a black hole before it falls into the Kasner singularity, and the Schwarzschild black hole saturate this bound.

  <summary>Details</summary>
