Method: 采用热场动力学（Thermo Field Dynamics）方法，将黑洞建模为AdS3中的塌缩尘埃壳（collapsing dust shell）。推导FIDO观测的壳轨迹R(t)，从Hartle-Hawking和Killing-Boulware真空态获得Wightman函数差，并计算能量密度。详细处理了连接条件（junction conditions）、Kruskal延拓、WKB模式和UV正则化（UV regularization）等中间步骤。

Result: 在视界外发现了尖锐局域化的能量密度，这与砖墙模型（brick wall picture）一致。完整的热力学分析显示纠缠熵与视界面积成正比，其数值与Bekenstein-Hawking熵相匹配。

Conclusion: 通过热场动力学方法成功计算了BTZ黑洞附近标量场的纠缠熵，验证了纠缠熵与Bekenstein-Hawking熵的数值对应关系，为黑洞熵的微观解释提供了支持。

Abstract: We compute the entanglement entropy of a real massive scalar field near a non-rotating BTZ black hole using Thermo Field Dynamics. Modeling the black hole as a collapsing dust shell in AdS3, we derive the shell trajectory R(t) as seen by a Fiducial Observer (FIDO). From the Hartle-Hawking and Killing-Boulware vacua, we obtain the Wightman function difference and compute energy density, revealing a sharply localized energy density just outside the horizon, consistent with the brick wall picture. A full thermodynamic analysis yields an entanglement entropy proportional to the horizon area, numerically matching the Bekenstein-Hawking entropy. All intermediate steps, including junction conditions, Kruskal extension, WKB modes, and UV regularization, are explicitly detailed.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用数值研究方法，将[arXiv:2210.12898]中的研究扩展到周期性稳态轴对称解。通过参数化周期L、质量M和角动量绝对值|J|>0来构建解，并提供强数值证据支持其存在性。

Result: 研究提供了强数值证据表明，具有两个等距反向旋转视界的周期性稳态轴对称解在任意视间距下均存在。这与非零总角动量情况形成鲜明对比，后者在L<4M时无法旋转。这些解在轴上无支撑结构，但非等距视界配置会产生黑洞间的支撑。

Conclusion: 本文成功构建了包含多个视界的周期性稳态轴对称解，证明了等距反向旋转视界配置在任意距离下的存在性，且无轴支撑结构。非等距配置则会产生支撑结构，其他全局性质也在文中呈现。

Abstract: In this article, we extend the numerical studies developed in [arXiv:2210.12898] to construct periodic stationary axisymmetric solutions containing multiple horizons in each fundamental domain. As a direct application, we consider periodic stationary axisymmetric solutions with two identical equidistant counter-rotating horizons. These solutions can be parametrized by the period $L$, the mass $M$, and the absolute value of the angular momentum $|J| >0$. We provide strong numerical evidence for the existence of such configurations, without any restriction in terms of the distance between horizons. This is in sharp contrast with the non-zero total angular momentum case, as it was recently established in \cite{Peraza:2024uto} that static single-horizon periodic solutions cannot be put into rotation if $L < 4M$. It is shown that these solutions do not have any struts on the axis, and it is also explicitly shown that, by taking non-equidistant horizons, struts develop between the black holes. Other global properties of the solutions are also presented.

### [58] [WKB-like approach to the Unruh temperature for arbitrary acceleration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.22534)
*Paul M. Alsing*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本研究通过隧穿势垒方法推导了在具有任意加速度a(t)的平坦闵可夫斯基时空中观测者的安鲁温度（Unruh temperature）。对于恒定加速度a(t)=a₀的情况，安鲁温度恢复为标准表达式k_bT_U=ℏa₀/(2πc)。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在将安鲁温度的概念从恒定加速度情况推广到任意时变加速度a(t)的情形。通过扩展de Gill等人的工作，探索在广义加速度条件下量子场论效应的表现。

Method: 采用广义引力WKB（Wentzel-Kramers-Brillouin）方法，推导适用于任意加速度的安鲁温度。研究指出施瓦西度规形式不适用于任意a(t)的WKB计算，转而使用广义林德勒度规（generalized Rindler metric）方法。

Result: 推导出适用于任意加速度a(t)的广义安鲁温度表达式，建立了广义林德勒坐标（generalized Rindler coordinates），并强调积分加速度χ(t)=∫a(t')dt'作为时间坐标的重要性。通过多个非平凡a(t)示例验证了该理论框架。

Conclusion: 成功建立了任意加速度情况下安鲁温度的理论框架，为研究时变加速度下的量子场论效应提供了数学工具。通过坐标变换建立了加速观测者与共形坐标之间的联系，使波动方程解的平面波结构更加清晰。

Abstract: In this work we study the Unruh temperature as arising from tunneling through a barrier for an observer in flat Minkowski spacetime with arbitrary acceleration $a(t)$. For the defining case of constant acceleration $a(t) = a_0$, the Unruh temperature (W. Unruh, Phys. Rev. D 14, 870 (1976)) is given by $k_b\,T_U =\tfrac{\hbar\,a_0}{2\,π\,c}$. Extending the work of de Gill et al. (A. de Gill, D. Singleton, V. Akhmedova and T. Pilling, Am. J. Phys. 78, 685 (2010)) we generalize the gravitational WKB approach to derive the Unruh temperature for arbitrary acceleration. We show that the often employed Schwarzschild-like form of the flat metric is not appropriate for the WKB calculation with an arbitrary $a(t)$, and instead derive a generalized Unruh temperature for the generalized Rindler metric where $a_0\to a(t)$. We derive a generalization of the Rindler coordinates appropriate for arbitrary $a(t)$, and stress the importance of the role of the integrated acceleration $χ(t) = \int^t dt'\,a(t')$, which can also act as a temporal coordinate. We explore several non-trivial examples of $a(t)$ and their generalized Unruh temperatures. We additionally develop an approximation to the Unruh temperature for small deviations away from constant acceleration by the standard approach of considering the negative frequency content of a purely positive frequency plane wave of an inertial observer, as measured by the co-moving arbitrarily accelerated observer. Lastly, we develop and explicit coordinate transformation between the arbitrarily accelerated observer and conformal coordinates, where the plane wave structure of the solutions of the wave equation is readily transparent, and analogous to the form for the inertial observer.

</details>

Abstract: In this letter, we develop a unified semiclassical framework for the thermodynamics and quantization of the Reissner--Nordström (RN) black hole (BH) based on the Misner--Sharp--Hernandez (MSH) mass. Treating the quasi-local horizon energies as the relevant thermodynamic variables, we formulate a horizon-by-horizon first law and Smarr relation. Using a reduced phase-space quantization, we obtain a discrete MSH mass spectrum for both horizons, which reproduces the minimal entropy spacing. Quantum transitions between adjacent levels yield Planck-scale corrections to the Hawking temperatures and a universal logarithmic contribution to the entropy, consistent with independent approaches to quantum gravity. We encode these corrections into a quantum-deformed RN geometry via a simple multiplicative factor that preserves the classical horizon positions while reproducing the corrected surface gravities. The associated effective stress tensor behaves as a conserved vacuum-polarization source with characteristic $r^{-4}$ falloff and a small trace, providing a compact representation of semiclassical backreaction. The deformation slightly lowers both horizon temperatures, weakens the inner-horizon instability, and induces tiny shifts in photon-sphere and shadow observables for macroscopic BHs.

Method: 方法是将Wheeler-DeWitt方程的WKB展开推广到f(R)引力理论，直至二阶展开。该方法应用于均匀各向同性的FLRW宇宙，包括零曲率和正曲率情形，适用于任意f(R)模型。

Conclusion: 结论表明，尽管跃迁概率以模型依赖的方式增减，但在所有情况下都保持了爱因斯坦引力中发现的概率一般行为，包括量子修正导致非奇异初始态的预测。

Abstract: We study Lorentzian vacuum transition probabilities between two minima of a scalar field potential within the framework of $f(R)$ gravity. The analysis extends the previously considered WKB expansion of the Wheeler-DeWitt equation to modified gravity theories, up to second order. We apply the general method for homogeneous and isotropic FLRW universes, with zero and positive spatial curvature, for any $f(R)$ model. For the flat case we obtain analytic expressions for the transition probabilities for any model if we assume a constant Ricci scalar; this assumption has been considered in previous studies, in the Euclidean approach, from symmetry arguments. On the other hand, we also obtain explicit solutions without this assumption for power-law $f(R)=R^{1+n}$ models. Moreover, in the positive curvature scenario, we obtain that the assumption of a constant Ricci scalar is not consistent, but we are able to find analytical solutions in approximated regimes. In all cases we have found that the general behavior of the probabilities already found for Einstein Gravity is preserved, including the prediction of a non-singular initial state due to quantum corrections, even though the probabilities increase or decrease in a model dependent way.

Abstract: In this work, we theoretically investigate the deflection of light for strong- and weak-field regimes in the background of an electrically charged BH described in Kalb-Ramond gravity, which introduces the Lorentz symmetry violation parameter $l$, as well as the control of the degree of nonlinearity incorporated by electrodynamics through the parameter $γ$. We analytically constructed the expansion coefficients in both limits and used them as a basis to investigate gravitational lensing effects through observables, taking into account the variation of the parameters involved in the model, both for the canonical field and the phantom case.

### [62] [Quantum Oppenheimer-Snyder Black Holes with a Cloud of Strings Surrounded by Perfect Fluid Dark Matter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.22928)
*Faizuddin Ahmed,Allan R. P. Moreira,Abdelmalek Bouzenada*

Abstract: In this study, we examine quantum Oppenheimer-Snyder black holes (BHs) embedded within a cloud of strings and immersed in perfect fluid dark matter. In this case, the thermodynamic behavior of the system is studied, including the role of string clouds and dark matter in modifying BH thermodynamic quantities. Also, the obtained results present a unified description of the combined effects of quantum corrections, nonstandard matter sources, and BH physics, with potential relevance for both observational constraints and theoretical modeling of compact objects.

### [63] [Testing the Weak Gravity Conjecture via Gravitational Lensing, Black Hole Shadows, and Barrow Thermodynamics in F(R)-Euler-Heisenberg (A)dS Black Holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.22930)
*Saeed Noori Gashti,Izzet Sakalli,Erdem Sucu,Mohammad Reza Alipour,Ankit Anand,Mohammad Ali S Afshar,Behnam Pourhassan,Jafar Sadeghi*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了F(R)-Euler-Heisenberg黑洞在反德西特（Anti-de Sitter）和德西特（de Sitter）背景下弱引力猜想（Weak Gravity Conjecture, WGC）与弱宇宙监督猜想（Weak Cosmic Censorship Conjecture, WCCC）的相互作用。通过熵-极值关系、光子球分析、引力透镜效应和黑洞阴影成像，证实了WGC与WCCC的兼容性，并在Barrow熵框架下发现了范德瓦尔斯型相变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在探究F(R)-Euler-Heisenberg黑洞在Anti-de Sitter和de Sitter背景下弱引力猜想（WGC）与弱宇宙监督猜想（WCCC）之间的相互作用关系。研究关注这两个基本理论猜想在修正引力理论中的兼容性和表现。

Method: 采用多种分析方法：建立普适的熵-极值关系（entropy-extremality relation）提供热力学证据；从测地线（geodesic）和拓扑（topological）角度进行光子球（photon sphere）分析；在强偏转和弱偏转极限下研究引力透镜效应（gravitational lensing）；构建各向同性吸积下的黑洞阴影图像；在Barrow熵框架下分析相变和焦耳-汤姆逊膨胀（Joule-Thomson expansion）。

Result: 研究发现了一个独立于f_R0和R0的普适熵-极值关系，为WGC提供了热力学证据。光子球分析证实了WGC与WCCC的兼容性，且Euler-Heisenberg耦合在裸奇点区域恢复了光子球。引力透镜分析显示光子球半径与宇宙学背景无关，而临界碰撞参数在de Sitter背景下几乎翻倍。在Barrow熵框架下发现了范德瓦尔斯型相变（van der Waals-type phase transitions），并确定小黑洞相是通过等焓冷却可达到的WGC兼容热力学区域。

Conclusion: 研究证实了在F(R)-Euler-Heisenberg黑洞中，弱引力猜想（WGC）与弱宇宙监督猜想（WCCC）可以同时兼容。Euler-Heisenberg耦合在裸奇点区域恢复了光子球结构，而Barrow熵框架下的热力学分析揭示了WGC兼容的小黑洞相可以通过等焓冷却过程达到。

Abstract: We investigate the interplay of the Weak Gravity Conjecture (WGC) and the Weak Cosmic Censorship Conjecture (WCCC) in $F(R)$-Euler-Heisenberg black holes in Anti-de Sitter and de Sitter backgrounds. The solution is characterized by the electric charge $q$, the $F(R)$ deviation $f_{R_0}$, the Euler--Heisenberg coupling $λ$, and the constant scalar curvature $R_0$. We establish a universal entropy--extremality relation that provides thermodynamic evidence for the WGC independently of $f_{R_0}$ and $R_0$. Photon sphere analysis from both geodesic and topological perspectives confirms the simultaneous compatibility of the WGC and WCCC, with the Euler--Heisenberg coupling restoring photon spheres in the naked singularity regime. Gravitational lensing in the strong- and weak-deflection limits reveals that the photon sphere radius is independent of the cosmological background while the critical impact parameter nearly doubles in de Sitter. Black hole shadow images under isotropic accretion are constructed. Within the Barrow entropy framework, we uncover van der Waals-type phase transitions and analyze Joule-Thomson expansion, identifying the small black hole phase as the WGC-compatible thermodynamic regime accessible via isenthalpic cooling.

### [64] [Charged scalar and Dirac perturbations on a global monopole Reissner-Nordström-de Sitter black hole: quasinormal modes and strong cosmic censorship](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.23083)
*Peiyang Li,Mengjie Wang,Jiliang Jing*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了带有全局单极子（global monopole）的Reissner-Nordström-de Sitter黑洞周围带电标量场和狄拉克场的微扰。通过将Teukolsky方程映射到Heun方程，采用Heun函数方法计算了准正规模谱，分析了全局单极子对三种模式的影响及其对强宇宙监督猜想（strong cosmic censorship）的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索带有全局单极子的Reissner-Nordström-de Sitter黑洞背景下，带电标量场和狄拉克场微扰的动力学行为。特别关注全局单极子对黑洞准正规模谱的影响，以及其对强宇宙监督猜想（strong cosmic censorship）的潜在影响。

Method: 首先推导了带电标量场和狄拉克场在上述背景下的运动方程，并将其统一化为Teukolsky方程。利用渐近de Sitter时空中Teukolsky方程可映射到Heun方程的特性，采用Heun函数方法求解准正规模谱，包括光子球模式（photon sphere modes）、de Sitter模式和近极端模式（near-extremal modes）。

Result: 分析发现全局单极子通过修正多极数（modified multipole number）的偏移影响谱和强宇宙监督猜想。在近极端区域，全局单极子对强宇宙监督猜想的影响存在差异：对标量微扰无影响，但对狄拉克微扰增强了强宇宙监督猜想的违反。

Conclusion: 研究表明Heun函数方法是探索渐近de Sitter黑洞与微扰场相互作用的有效且稳健的方法。全局单极子通过修正多极数的偏移影响准正规模谱，并对不同类型微扰的强宇宙监督猜想产生不同影响。

Abstract: We study perturbations of charged scalar and Dirac fields around Reissner-Nordström-de Sitter black holes with a global monopole. To this end, we first derive the equations of motion for both fields on the aforementioned background; these equations are then reformulated uniformly into the Teukolsky equation. Since the Teukolsky equation in asymptotically de Sitter spacetimes can be mapped into the Heun equation, we are able to solve quasinormal spectra by employing the Heun function method, not only for photon sphere modes but also for de Sitter and near-extremal modes. We analyze the spectra of all three types for both fields and, in particular, ascertain the effects of the global monopole. In the near-extremal regime, we find that the presence of a global monopole, on the one hand, leaves the strong cosmic censorship conjecture unaffected for scalar perturbations, while on the other hand, it enhance the violation of strong cosmic censorship for Dirac perturbations. Furthermore, we identify that the impact of the global monopole on both the spectra and the strong cosmic censorship is achieved by a shift in the modified multipole number. Our work demonstrates that the Heun function method is an efficient and robust approach for exploring the interaction between asymptotically de Sitter black holes and perturbing fields.

Method: 方法包括：1）构建适应对称性变换的晶格（lattice），使其在离散设置下最大程度保持球对称性；2）研究动力学对称性限制条件；3）识别使计算可行的子空间；4）在该子空间上显式计算辛结构（symplectic structure）和标量约束（scalar constraint）。

Abstract: This manuscript is the first in a series of instalments that investigate spherically symmetric solutions within the effective dynamics program of Loop Quantum Gravity. The choice of lattice is adapted such that it remains invariant under a set of symmetry transformations maximally mapping spherical symmetry to the discrete setting. The conditions for symmetry restriction of the dynamics are investigated and a subspace is identified to make computations feasible. Afterwards symplectic structure and scalar constraint are explicitly computed on this subspace. This lays the groundwork to target several particular solutions, such $k=1$ cosmology and black holes, which will serve as the subjects of forthcoming follow-up papers.

### [66] [Demonstrating Single Photon Counting with Kinetic Inductance Detectors from 3.8 to 25 $μ$m](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.22970)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 在四个波长下分别测得能量分辨率（E/δE）为9.9、5.9、3.2和3.3，对应的暗计数率为4、8、34和48 mHz。基于薄膜的器件在3.8 μm波长达到声子损失限制的性能，比类似固体基底器件的性能提高了一倍以上。

Conclusion: 这些结果展示了超导微波动力学电感探测器在中红外波段的探测能力以及所需精密测量装置。研究讨论了如何通过优化探测器设计和测量装置来进一步提升中红外波段的探测器性能。

Abstract: One of the primary objectives of modern astronomy is the atmospheric characterization of Earth-like exoplanets at visible and infrared wavelengths. Achieving this goal requires extremely sensitive detectors capable of measuring faint signal of the exoplanet at the single-photon level while maintaining near-zero dark count rates. In the infrared, however, conventional semiconducting detector technologies struggle to meet these stringent requirements. In this work we demonstrate single-photon counting with superconducting Microwave Kinetic Inductance Detectors at the wavelengths 3.8, 8.5, 18.5, and 25 $μ$m and measure resolving powers ($E/δE$) of 9.9, 5.9, 3.2, and 3.3, respectively, with corresponding dark count rates of 4, 8, 34, and 48 mHz. Our membrane-based devices reach phonon-loss limited performance at 3.8 $μ$m, more than doubling the performance attainable with comparable solid-substrate devices. These results showcase the detector technology in the mid-infrared and the intricate measurement setup required for these sensitive detectors. We discuss how the detector design and measurement setup can be further optimized to increase the detector performance in the mid-infrared.

### [67] [Inhomogeneous superconductivity in (001), (110) and (111) KTaO$_3$ two-dimensional electronic gas: $T_c$ driven from electronic confinement](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.22316)
*Matta Trama,Roberta Citro,Carmine Antonio Perroni*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该研究在统一微观框架下分析了KTaO₃基二维电子气在不同晶向（001）、（110）和（111）的超导性，发现临界温度的显著取向依赖性主要源于二维电子气空间扩展和费米能级态密度重分布的差异，而非配对相互作用的变化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在为KTaO₃基二维电子气在不同晶向（001）、（110）和（111）中观察到的超导性取向依赖性提供微观解释，这些实验现象需要统一的理论框架来阐明其物理起源。

Method: 采用自洽紧束缚（self-consistent tight-binding）平板模型，确定每个晶向的约束势、电子结构和轨道组成，明确包含反演对称性诱导的轨道Rashba耦合（orbital Rashba couplings），并使用局域自旋单态s波配对相互作用。

Result: 研究发现超导临界温度（superconducting critical temperature）的显著取向依赖性主要源于二维电子气（two-dimensional electron gas）空间扩展的差异以及费米能级（Fermi level）态密度（density of states）的重分布，而非配对相互作用的变化。

Conclusion: 该研究为实验观察到的KTaO₃基界面超导性的取向依赖性提供了微观解释，揭示了二维电子气空间扩展和费米能级态密度重分布是决定超导临界温度取向依赖性的关键因素。

Abstract: We investigate superconductivity in KTaO$_3$ (KTO)-based two-dimensional electron gases for the (001), (110), and (111) crystallographic orientations within a unified microscopic framework. Using a self-consistent tight-binding slab model, we determine the confinement potential, electronic structure, and orbital composition for each orientation, explicitly including inversion-symmetry-induced orbital Rashba couplings. Using a local spin-singlet s-wave pairing interaction, we find that the pronounced orientation dependence of the superconducting critical temperature primarily originates from differences in the spatial extent of the two-dimensional electron gas and the associated redistribution of the density of states at the Fermi level, rather than from changes in the pairing interaction. Our results provide a microscopic explanation for the experimentally observed orientation dependence of superconductivity at KTO-based interfaces.

### [68] [Enhancement of superconductivity by disorder in Remeika-type quasiskutterudites](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.22448)
*Andrzej Ślebarski,Maciej M. Maśka*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了原子尺度无序（atomic-scale disorder）在Remeika型准方钴矿化合物中能够增强超导性能，通过实验和理论模型证明了无序诱导的局域超导区域具有高于体相转变温度Tc的临界温度Tc*，并建立了无序作为热力学控制参数调控超导性的机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统观点认为原子尺度无序对超导性有害，但本研究旨在探索在特定条件下无序如何增强超导性能。研究聚焦于Remeika型准方钴矿（quasiskutterudites）化合物R3M4Sn13和R5M6Sn18，通过系统研究无序在复杂关联体系中的作用。

Method: 结合磁化率（magnetic susceptibility）、电阻率（electrical resistivity）和热容（heat capacity）测量与微观建模（microscopic modeling）。通过测量上临界场（upper critical field）Hc2(T)获得体相和局域超导相的不同分支，为渗流超导态（percolative superconducting state）提供直接实验证据。

Result: 增加无序导致具有增强临界温度Tc*（高于体相转变温度Tc）的局域超导区域出现。Tc*和Tc均表现出对掺杂浓度的非单调依赖，并与作为无序函数的熵等温线（entropy isotherms）强相关。显著的熵最大值与Tc*和Tc之间的最大分离度重合，表明无序是热力学控制参数。

Conclusion: 研究提出了一个微观模型，捕捉了杂质诱导的局域配对增强与无序驱动的全局超导相干性抑制之间的相互作用。该模型重现了实验观察到的Tc*随无序的非单调演化，支持基于渗流（percolation-based）的超导转变解释，表明受控原子无序可作为调控复杂关联体系中超导性的有效材料设计参数。

Abstract: Atomic-scale disorder is conventionally regarded as detrimental to superconductivity; however, under specific conditions, it can enhance superconducting properties. Here, we investigate the role of substitutional disorder in Remeika-type quasiskutterudites $R_3M_4$Sn$_{13}$ and $R_5M_6$Sn$_{18}$ ($R=$ Y, La, Lu; $M=$ Co, Rh, Ru) by combining measurements of magnetic susceptibility, electrical resistivity, and heat capacity with microscopic modeling. We demonstrate that increasing disorder leads to the emergence of locally superconducting regions characterized by an enhanced critical temperature $T_c^{\ast}$, exceeding the bulk transition temperature $T_c$.
  Both $T_c^\ast$ and $T_c$ exhibit a nonmonotonic dependence on dopant concentration and show a strong correlation with entropy isotherms measured as a function of disorder. The pronounced entropy maxima coincide with the largest separation between $T_c^{\ast}$ and $T_c$, establishing disorder as a thermodynamically controlled parameter governing superconductivity in these materials. Measurements of the upper critical field reveal distinct $H_{c2}(T)$ branches associated with the bulk and locally superconducting phases, providing direct experimental evidence for a percolative superconducting state.
  To interpret these observations, we propose a microscopic model that captures the interplay between the impurity-induced enhancement of local pairing and the disorder-driven suppression of global superconducting coherence. The model reproduces the experimentally observed nonmonotonic evolution of $T_c^{\ast}$ with disorder and supports a percolation-based interpretation of the superconducting transition. Our results demonstrate that controlled atomic disorder can serve as an effective materials-design parameter for tuning superconductivity in complex correlated systems.

</details>


### [69] [Moire Engineering of Cooper-Pair Density Modulation States](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.22637)
*Zihao Wang,Bing Xia,Stephen Paolini,Zi-Jie Yan,Pu Xiao,Jiatao Song,Veer Gowda,Hongtao Rong,Di Xiao,Xiaodong Xu,Weida Wu,Ziqiang Wang,Cui-Zu Chang*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该研究在拓扑绝缘体Sb2Te3与反铁磁FeTe的异质结中，利用莫尔超晶格（moiré superlattice）实现了库珀对密度调制（CPDM）态，并通过约瑟夫森扫描隧道显微术直接观测到其空间周期性调制。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 莫尔超晶格为调控电荷密度提供了可调谐的晶格对称性平台，为创建和控制库珀对密度调制（Cooper-pair density modulation, CPDM）态提供了新途径。研究旨在探索不同晶体对称性材料构建的异质结中CPDM态的工程化机制。

Method: 采用外延堆叠技术构建了1个五重层（1 QL）拓扑绝缘体Sb2Te3与6个晶胞（6 UC）反铁磁FeTe的双层异质结。通过扫描隧道显微术/谱学（STM/S）和约瑟夫森STM/S测量，直接观测莫尔超晶格的形成及其对超导能隙的空间调制。

Result: STM/S测量揭示了Sb2Te3的六方Te晶格与FeTe的四方Te晶格之间形成的莫尔超晶格，该结构空间调制了双层异质结的两个超导能隙。约瑟夫森STM/S直接成像了波长与莫尔超晶格周期对应的CPDM态。通过将Sb2Te3替换为Bi2Te3，实现了对CPDM态周期性和幅度的调控。

Conclusion: 该工作展示了一种从不同晶体对称性材料合成莫尔超晶格的外延策略，并揭示了在设计的双层异质结中工程化CPDM态的新机制，为调控超导序参量的空间调制提供了有效途径。

Abstract: Cooper-pair density modulation (CPDM) states are superconducting phases in which the order parameter varies periodically in real space without breaking translational symmetry. Recently, moire superlattices in layered materials have emerged as powerful platforms for engineering charge density with tunable lattice symmetry, offering a new route to creating and controlling CPDM states. In this work, we demonstrate moire-induced CPDM states in a bilayer heterostructure formed by epitaxially stacking one quintuple layer (1 QL) of topological insulator Sb2Te3 on a six-unit-cell (6 UC) antiferromagnetic FeTe layer. Scanning tunneling microscopy and spectroscopy (STM/S) measurements reveal a moiré superlattice formed between the hexagonal Te lattice of Sb2Te3 and the square Te lattice of FeTe, which spatially modulates the two superconducting gaps of the 1 QL Sb2Te3/6 UC FeTe bilayer. Our Josephson STM/S measurements provide direct real-space imaging of the CPDM states with a wavelength corresponding to the periodicity of the moire superlattice. By substituting Sb2Te3 with Bi2Te3, we achieve control over both the periodicity and magnitude of the CPDM states. Our work demonstrates an epitaxial strategy for synthesizing moire superlattices from materials with different crystal symmetries and reveals a new mechanism for engineering CPDM states in designer bilayer heterostructures.

### [70] [Emergence of chiral $p$-wave and $d$-wave states in $g$-wave altermagnets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.22736)
*Tilen Cadez,Abraham Nathan Sunanta,Kyoung-Min Kim*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该研究发现在三维g波交变磁体（g-wave altermagnets）中，交变磁性的费米面自旋劈裂能够诱导出多种非常规超导态，包括手性p波和d波超导态，为探索手性和无能隙超导性提供了新平台。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 交变磁体（altermagnets）因其电子能带结构的奇特动量依赖自旋劈裂，成为实现非常规超导性的新平台。近期实验在CrSb中发现了具有独特g波对称性的新型交变磁性，但g波交变磁性引发非常规超导性的潜力尚未被充分探索。

Method: 研究采用扩展吸引Hubbard模型（extended attractive Hubbard model）结合g波交变磁交换场，在三维六角晶格（如CrSb结构）上进行系统自洽平均场分析（self-consistent mean-field analysis）。

Result: 研究发现：在强交变磁场和高电子密度下，费米面自旋劈裂有利于手性p波态（chiral p-wave states）作为主导配对通道；弱交变磁场和中等电子密度下，手性d波态（chiral d-wave states）占主导；弱交变磁场和典型电子密度下，非手性s波、扩展s波或f波态（non-chiral s-, extended s-, or f-wave states）变得稳定。

Abstract: Altermagnets emerge as a novel platform for realizing unconventional superconductivity through their exotic momentum-dependent spin-splitting of electronic band structures. Recent experiments have uncovered a novel form of altermagnetism with distinctive $g$-wave symmetry in CrSb. However, the potential for unconventional superconductivity arising from $g$-wave altermagnetism in such systems remains largely unexplored. In this study, we discover the emergence of chiral superconducting states in three-dimensional $g$-wave altermagnetic metals. Through systematic self-consistent mean-field analysis on the extended attractive Hubbard model combined with $g$-wave altermagnetic exchange fields in a three-dimensional hexagonal lattice, as observed in CrSb, we find that the altermagnetic spin splitting of Fermi surfaces favors chiral $p$-wave states as the dominant pairing channel under strong altermagnetic fields and high electron densities, while chiral $d$-wave states become predominant under weak altermagnetic fields and intermediate electron densities. Conversely, at weak altermagnetic fields and typical electron densities, non-chiral $s$-, extended $s$-, or $f$-wave states become stabilized. We also showcase the possible experimental detection using the quasiparticle energy dispersions and the density of states to distinguish different pairing symmetries. These findings underscore the potential of $g$-wave altermagnets to host sought-after chiral and gapless superconductivity.

### [71] [Interaction and disorder effects on Cooper instability in two-dimensional fractional Dirac semimetals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.22772)
*Hua Zang,Jing Wang*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该研究通过重整化群分析，系统探讨了分数狄拉克半金属中库珀配对与无序散射的相互作用如何调控低能区的超导不稳定性。研究发现分数指数α和转移动量Q对超导相变有显著影响，而无序散射根据类型不同可促进或抑制超导不稳定性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在理解分数狄拉克半金属（fractional Dirac semimetals）中库珀配对（Cooper pairing）与无序散射（disorder scatterings）的相互作用如何调控低能区的超导不稳定性（Cooper instability）。通过系统分析这些竞争物理成分，为理解此类材料的超导性质提供理论基础。

Method: 采用重整化群分析（renormalization group analysis），允许对竞争物理成分进行无偏处理。该方法系统追踪库珀配对与无序散射的相互作用如何影响低能区的超导不稳定性，特别关注分数指数α和转移动量Q=(Q,φ)的作用。

Result: 在清洁极限下，库珀不稳定性需要超越有限相互作用阈值|λ_c|，且对分数指数α和转移动量Q敏感：较大的α值增强BCS不稳定性倾向。当α∈(0.001,0.61)时，(Q,φ)参数空间分为两个区域：Zone-I（抑制库珀不稳定性）和Zone-II（允许库珀不稳定性）。无序散射根据类型产生不同影响：Δ_1或Δ_2型无序通过降低临界相互作用阈值|λ_c|和扩大超导相空间来促进超导性；而Δ_0或Δ_3型无序则通过增加|λ_c|和缩小可用相空间来抑制库珀配对。

Conclusion: 研究揭示了分数狄拉克半金属中库珀不稳定性的复杂调控机制。虽然促进型无序（Δ_1, Δ_2）与单一抑制型无序（Δ_0或Δ_3）共存时可增强库珀不稳定性，但当所有类型无序同时存在时，Δ_0,3的抑制效应通常主导Δ_1,2的促进效应。这些结果为分数狄拉克半金属及相关材料的进一步研究提供了重要参考。

Abstract: Employing a renormalization group analysis that allows for an unbiased treatment of competing physical ingredients, we systematically trace how the interplay between Cooper pairing and disorder scatterings governs the emergence or suppression of Cooper instability in the low-energy regime of fractional Dirac semimetals.In the clean limit, we find that the emergence of Cooper instability requires surpassing a finite interaction threshold $|λ_c|$, and depends sensitively on both the fractional exponent $α$ and the transfer momentum $\mathbf{Q}=(Q,φ)$. Specifically, bigger values of $α$ enhance the tendency toward BCS instability. For $α\in(0.001,0.61)$, the $(Q,φ)$ parameter space separates into two distinct regions: Zone-\uppercase\expandafter{\romannumeral1}, where Cooper instability is suppressed, and Zone-\uppercase\expandafter{\romannumeral2}, where it is allowed. In the presence of disorders, we demonstrate that they can either promote or suppress Cooper instability. Disorder of type $Δ_1$ or $Δ_2$ enhances superconductivity by reducing the critical interaction threshold $|λ_c|$ and expanding the superconducting phase space (Zone-\uppercase\expandafter{\romannumeral2}). In sharp contrast, either $Δ_0$ or $Δ_3$ suppresses Cooper pairing by increasing $|λ_c|$ and shrinking the available phase space (Zone-\uppercase\expandafter{\romannumeral1}). Although Cooper instability can be enhanced when promotive disorders ($Δ_1$, $Δ_2$) coexist with a single suppressive disorder ($Δ_0$ or $Δ_3$), the suppressive influence of $Δ_{0,3}$ generally dominates the promotive effects of $Δ_{1,2}$ in the presence of all sorts of disorders. These results would be helpful for further studies of fractional Dirac semimetals and alike materials.

Here, we report periodic magnetoresistance oscillations, superconducting interference patterns, and interfering diode effect in unpatterned few-layer NbSe2. These phenomena emerge exclusively within the superconducting fluctuation regime of thin samples, consistent with the enhanced anomalous metallic behavior of atomically thin NbSe2. The non-monotonic temperature dependence of both the oscillation amplitude and the diode efficiency can be captured by a model in which thermally activated vortices traverse intrinsic supercurrent loops. Our results reveal that the observed interference phenomena originate from the lost of global phase coherence, providing a new route to accessing interference effects in unpatterned superconductors.

### [73] [Hourglass Dirac chains enable intrinsic topological superconductivity in nonsymmorphic silicides](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.22793)

Abstract: Nonsymmorphic crystalline symmetries provide a robust route to symmetry-protected electronic topology, yet their role in stabilizing intrinsic topological superconductivity remains largely unexplored. Here, we report \ch{TaPtSi} as a new member of the superconducting nonsymmorphic silicide family, characterized via AC transport, magnetization, heat capacity, and muon spin rotation/relaxation ($μ$SR) measurements. Zero field $μ$SR reveals spontaneous internal magnetic fields below $T_{\rm c}$, establishing time reversal symmetry breaking in \ch{TaPtSi}. The "necks" of these dispersions form Dirac nodal rings and chains that reside near or intersect the Fermi level. Guided by Ginzburg Landau symmetry analysis, we identify an internally antisymmetric non unitary triplet pairing state as the unique ground state consistent with the experimental phenomenology. Based on Bogoliubov de Gennes calculations, we further demonstrate that this state supports Majorana surface modes, establishing its intrinsically topological nature. These results reveal a systematic route by which nonsymmorphic symmetry drives the interplay between hourglass Dirac chain topology and unconventional triplet pairing, positioning equiatomic silicides as a unified materials platform for intrinsic topological superconductivity.

### [74] [Surface-localized topological superconductivity in nodal-loop materials: BdG analysis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.22837)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在理解节线半金属中表面超导性的配对对称性选择机制，特别是鼓面表面态如何影响超导配对，为解释Pd掺杂CaAgP等材料的表面敏感实验提供理论指导。

Method: 采用最小紧束缚模型（minimal tight-binding model）与层分辨Bogoliubov-de Gennes方法相结合的理论框架，在z方向开放边界的板状几何结构中引入手征p波和d_{x^2-y^2}波超导通道，并自洽确定层依赖的能隙振幅。

Result: 手征p波序参量在外层显著增强且在少数层内衰减，而d波序参量在所有层都小一个数量级以上；鼓面能带被有效打开能隙，正常表面谱中的零能峰分裂为两个相干峰，直接反映了诱导的超导能隙。

Abstract: We theoretically study surface superconductivity in a nodal-line semimetal by combining a minimal tight-binding model with a layer-resolved Bogoliubov-de Gennes approach. In the normal state, the model realizes a bulk nodal loop and an associated drumhead surface band in a slab geometry with open boundaries in the $z$ direction: the central layers reproduce the bulk-like density of states, whereas the surface layer exhibits a sharp zero-energy peak originating from the drumhead states. On top of this band structure we introduce chiral $p$-wave and $d_{x^2-y^2}$-wave superconducting channels and determine the layer-dependent gap amplitudes self-consistently. The chiral $p$-wave order parameter is strongly enhanced at the outermost layers and decays within only a few layers towards the interior, while the $d$-wave order parameter is more than an order of magnitude smaller on all layers. The quasiparticle dispersion and surface local density of states in the chiral $p$-wave state show that the drumhead band is efficiently gapped out and that the zero-energy peak in the normal surface spectrum is split into two coherence peaks, directly reflecting the induced superconducting gap. These results demonstrate that superconductivity driven by drumhead surface states is naturally biased toward a surface-localized chiral $p$-wave pairing symmetry and may offer qualitative guidance for interpreting surface-sensitive experiments on Pd-doped CaAgP.

### [75] [Pressure-induced reentrant superconductivity in a misfit layered compound $\mathrm{(SnS)_{1.15}(TaS_2)}$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.22999)
*Chutong Zhang,Jiajia Feng,Xiao Tang,Xiangzhuo Xing,Na Zuo,Xiaolei Yi,Yan Meng,Xiaoran Zhang,Rajesh Kumar Ulaganathan,Raman Sankar,Xiaofeng Xu,Xin Chen,Xiaobing Liu*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 错配层状化合物（misfit layered compounds）作为天然范德华异质结构，其过渡金属二硫化物层被非公度阻挡层解耦，为体材料实现准二维量子态提供了平台。研究旨在探索此类材料在高压下的超导、输运和结构特性。

Method: 研究对(SnS)₁.₁₅(TaS₂)化合物施加高达150 GPa的压力，系统测量其超导特性、输运性质（包括霍尔系数和正常态电阻）以及结构演化，通过综合表征分析压力效应。

Result: 低压超导相在14.7 GPa附近逐渐被抑制并消失，同时剩余电阻增加。在80 GPa以上重新出现明显的超导相并持续到最高压力。再入型超导（reentrant superconductivity）伴随着霍尔系数在60 GPa附近的符号反转和正常态电阻的非单调演化，表明发生了电子重构（electronic reconstruction）。在整个压力范围内未检测到结构相变。

Conclusion: 研究证明了压力驱动的电子重构导致错配层状化合物中出现再入型超导现象，确立了压力作为调控天然范德华异质结构中超导性和电子态的有效途径。

Abstract: Misfit layered compounds are natural van der Waals heterostructures in which electronically active transition-metal dichalcogenide layers are decoupled by incommensurate blocking layers, enabling bulk realization of quasi-two-dimensional quantum states. Here we investigate the superconducting, transport,and structural properties of the misfit compound $\mathrm{(SnS)_{1.15}(TaS_2)}$ under pressures up to 150 GPa. The low-pressure superconducting phase is gradually suppressed and disappears near 14.7 GPa,accompanied by increasing residual resistance. Remarkably, a distinct superconducting phase reemerges above 80 GPa and persists to the highest pressures achieved. This reentrant superconductivity follows a pressure-induced sign reversal of the Hall coefficient near 60 GPa and a nonmonotonic evolution of the normal-state resistance, indicating an electronic reconstruction. No structural phase transition is detected over the entire pressure range. Our results demonstrate a pressure-driven electronic reconstruction leading to reentrant superconductivity in a misfit layered compound, establishing pressure as an effective route to engineer superconductivity and electronic states in natural van der Waals heterostructures.

### [76] [Threefold error in the reported zero-field cooled magnetic moment of single crystal $La_2SmNi_2O_7$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.23240)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 论文通过分析Li等人[3]的实验数据，指出他们在计算$La_2SmNi_2O_7$超导相分数时存在三倍误差。作者认为这些测量结果本身是确认高压镍酸盐体超导性的杰出实验成果。

Result: Li等人[3]报告称ZFC模式下超导相分数为62.1%，FC模式下为14.4%，但本文作者指出这些计算存在三倍错误。作者强调这些直流抗磁态测量结果确实证实了高压镍酸盐中的体超导性。

Conclusion: 修正Li等人[3]在$La_2SmNi_2O_7$超导相分数计算中的错误以及其他错误，将对物理学界产生积极影响。这些测量结果本身是确认高压镍酸盐体超导性的重要实验证据。

Abstract: For a relatively long time, the observation of the DC diamagnetic state in highly compressed nickelate superconductors [1],[2] has been a challenging experimental problem. And recently Li et al.[3] reported on the measurements of the DC diamagnetism in zero-field-cooled (ZFC) and field-cooled (FC) pressurized single crystal $La_2SmNi_2O_7$. From the analysis of experimental data, Li et al.[3] reported that the superconducting phase fraction in their $La_2SmNi_2O_7$ sample measured in the ZFC mode is 62.1%, and the superconducting phase fraction in the FC mode is 14.4%. It should be clarified that we regard the measurements of the DC diamagnetic state [3] in $La_2SmNi_2O_7$ (and more recently in $Pr_4Ni_3O_{10}$ [4]) as outstanding experimental results confirming bulk superconductivity in pressurized nickelates. However, we should note that Li et al.[3] made a threefold error in their calculations of the superconducting phase fraction in $La_2SmNi_2O_7$. We believe that correcting this and other errors in Ref.[3] will benefit the physics community.

</details>

### [77] [Comparison of Structure-Preserving Methods for the Cahn-Hilliard-Navier-Stokes Equations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.22861)

TL;DR: 本文开发了针对具有退化迁移率（degenerate mobility）的Cahn-Hilliard-Navier-Stokes方程的保结构间断伽辽金方法，提出了SWIPD-L和SIPGD-L方法，通过参数化迁移率通量和边处理增强强制稳定性控制，证明了广义三线性形式的强制性，展示了最优收敛率同时保持质量守恒、能量耗散和离散极大值原理。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出了SWIPD-L和SIPGD-L两种间断伽辽金方法（discontinuous Galerkin methods），通过引入参数化迁移率通量（parametrized mobility fluxes）和边处理（edge-wise mobility treatments）来增强强制稳定性控制（coercivity-stability control）。

Result: 证明了广义三线性形式（generalized trilinear form）的强制性（coercivity），展示了最优收敛率（optimal convergence rates），同时保持了质量守恒（mass conservation）、能量耗散（energy dissipation）和离散极大值原理（discrete maximum principle）。与现有SIPG-L和SWIP-L方法的比较确认了相似的稳定性。

Conclusion: 在$hp$-自适应网格（$hp$-adaptive meshes）上对独立Cahn-Hilliard方程和耦合系统的验证表明，该方法在保持精度的同时实现了显著的计算节省，为具有退化迁移率的相场-流体耦合问题提供了有效的数值求解框架。

Abstract: We develop structure-preserving discontinuous Galerkin methods for the Cahn-Hilliard-Navier-Stokes equations with degenerate mobility. The proposed SWIPD-L and SIPGD-L methods incorporate parametrized mobility fluxes with edge-wise mobility treatments for enhanced coercivity-stability control. We prove coercivity for the generalized trilinear form and demonstrate optimal convergence rates while preserving mass conservation, energy dissipation, and the discrete maximum principle. Comparisons with existing SIPG-L and SWIP-L methods confirm similar stability. Validation on $hp$-adaptive meshes for both standalone Cahn-Hilliard and coupled systems shows significant computational savings without accuracy loss.

Main category: math.NA

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种数据驱动的Kohn-Sham密度泛函理论建模框架，通过构建低维基组近似电子结构子空间，避免了显式波函数优化，实现了高效的第一性原理分子动力学模拟。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为了利用第一性原理分子动力学（first-principles molecular dynamics）每一步计算中电子结构之间的冗余性，本研究旨在开发一种更高效的电子结构求解方法，避免传统方法中耗时的波函数优化过程。

Method: 该方法首先采样具有代表性的原子构型（atomic configurations），构建能够高效近似电子结构子空间的低维基组（low-dimensional basis）。随后在直接求解电子单粒子密度矩阵（electronic single particle density matrix）时使用这个约化基组，从而无需迭代波函数优化即可确定基态。

Result: 在水分子（water molecule）的Born-Oppenheimer分子动力学模拟中，该方法准确再现了完整第一性原理分子动力学获得的关键结构性质，如键长（bond lengths）和键角（bond angle）。

Conclusion: 这项工作凸显了数据驱动方法（data-driven approaches）在开发高效电子结构求解器（electronic structure solvers）用于第一性原理模拟方面的潜力，为更快速、更高效的量子化学计算提供了新途径。

Abstract: To leverage the redundancy between the electronic structure computed at each step of first-principles molecular dynamics, we present a data-driven modeling framework for Kohn-Sham Density Functional Theory that bypasses the explicit optimization of electronic wavefunctions. We sample a priori representative atomic configurations and construct a low-dimensional basis that efficiently approximates the electronic structure subspace. Subsequently, we employ this reduced basis in a direct solver for the electronic single particle density matrix, thereby enabling the efficient determination of ground state without iterative wavefunction optimization. We demonstrate the efficacy of our approach in a Born-Oppenheimer molecular dynamics of a water molecule, showing that the resulting simulations accurately reproduce key structural properties, such as bond lengths and bond angle, obtained from full first-principles molecular dynamics. This work highlights the potential of data-driven approaches to develop efficient electronic structure solvers for first-principles simulations.

### [79] [Controlled symmetry breaking of the Fermi surface in ultracold polar molecules](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.22447)
*Shrestha Biswas,Sebastian Eppelt,Weikun Tian,Wei Zhang,Fulin Deng,Christine Frank,Tao Shi,Immanuel Bloch,Xin-Yu Luo*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 该研究首次观测到超冷极性分子费米气体中偶极相互作用诱导的费米面可控形变，为探索强关联偶极费米物质提供了高度可调谐平台。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超冷极性分子间的长程各向异性偶极-偶极相互作用（long-range anisotropic dipole-dipole interactions）被预测会驱动奇异量子相，但在简并费米气体中这些相互作用的直接多体特征一直难以观测。

Method: 采用双微波屏蔽（double microwave shielding）技术制备了8×10³个$^{23}\text{Na}^{40}\text{K}$分子，温度达到0.23(1)倍费米温度，相比单微波屏蔽将非弹性损失抑制了三倍，同时保持了强弹性偶极散射。

Result: 观测到高达7%的费米面形变（Fermi surface deformations），比磁性原子中观测到的形变大两倍以上，尽管密度低了两个数量级；实现了从轴向U(1)到双轴C$_{2}$对称性（biaxial C$_{2}$ symmetry）的相互作用势连续调谐，并将此几何结构直接印刻到费米面上。

Conclusion: 实验结果与无参数哈特里-福克理论（parameter-free Hartree-Fock theory）高度吻合，确立了微波屏蔽极性分子作为探索强关联偶极费米物质（strongly correlated dipolar Fermi matter）的高度可调谐平台，为实现拓扑超流性（topological superfluidity）提供了有前景的路径。

Abstract: Long-range anisotropic dipole-dipole interactions between ultracold polar molecules are predicted to drive exotic quantum phases, yet direct many-body signatures of these interactions in degenerate Fermi gases have remained elusive. Here, we report the observation of an interaction-induced controlled deformation of the Fermi surface, providing a clear many-body signature in a deeply degenerate Fermi gas of $^{23}\text{Na}^{40}\text{K}$ molecules. Using double microwave (MW) shielding, we prepare $8 \times 10^3$ molecules at $0.23(1)$ times the Fermi temperature, achieving a three-fold suppression of inelastic losses compared to single MW shielding while preserving strong elastic dipolar scattering. We observe Fermi surface deformations of up to $7\,\%$, more than two times larger than those observed in magnetic atoms, despite operating at two orders of magnitude lower densities. Crucially, we demonstrate continuous tuning of the interaction potential from axial U(1) to biaxial C$_{2}$ symmetry, directly imprinting this geometry onto the Fermi surface. We find excellent agreement between our experimental results and parameter-free Hartree-Fock theory. These results establish MW-shielded polar molecules as a highly tunable platform for exploring strongly correlated dipolar Fermi matter and offer a promising path towards topological superfluidity.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究基于U(1)晶格规范理论（U(1) lattice gauge theory），分析弦张力与四费米耦合（four-Fermi coupling）之间的竞争，这种竞争自然出现在里德堡原子阵列（Rydberg atom arrays）中。通过受控能量匹配实现共振弦断裂（resonant string breaking），并在静态系统和Floquet驱动系统（Floquet-driven systems）中验证该机制。

Result: 研究表明初始弦态可以通过受控能量匹配实现共振熔化，这种现象被识别为共振弦断裂。在Floquet驱动系统中，周期性调制产生了一系列可调谐的边带共振（sideband resonances）。

Conclusion: 该工作为理解由长程相互作用和时变场驱动的禁闭和弦断裂机制提供了新见解，这些机制在当前多种平台的量子模拟器中是可实现的。

Abstract: Confinement and string breaking are two fundamental phenomena in gauge theories. Signatures of both are currently pursued in quantum-simulator experiments, opening a new angle on strongly interacting dynamics of gauge fields out of equilibrium, complementary to traditional particle-physics settings. In this work, we report the emergence of metastable confinement dynamics in a U(1) lattice gauge theory, originating from the competition between string tension and four-Fermi coupling - a competition that naturally arises in Rydberg atom arrays. We show that the initial string state can be resonantly melted through controlled energy matching, a phenomenon we identify as resonant string breaking. We demonstrate this mechanism for both static and Floquet-driven systems, where periodic modulation generates a spectrum of tunable sideband resonances. Our work provides new insights into the mechanisms of confinement and string breaking driven by long-range interactions and time-dependent fields, which are available in current quantum simulators on a variety of platforms.

### [81] [Macroscopic quantum self-trapping in bosonic Josephson junctions: an exact quantum treatment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.22857)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探究超越平均场理论（mean-field theory）的宏观量子自陷（macroscopic quantum self-trapping）有效性，特别关注完美对称玻色-约瑟夫森结（Bose-Josephson junction）中粒子数不平衡的完全量子演化。

Method: 采用双模玻色-哈伯德哈密顿量（two-mode Bose-Hubbard Hamiltonian）建模，利用该哈密顿量的对称性进行数学证明，并分析支配动力学的谱特性，包括特征值差异的分支行为和粒子数不平衡振幅的非平凡结构。

Result: 研究发现对于任何有限粒子数，精确量子动力学都会导致宏观量子自陷在有限时间内崩溃；识别了特征值差异的分支行为，揭示了两种明显不同的动力学机制，并阐明了在大粒子数下准宏观量子自陷机制的出现。

Conclusion: 这些发现弥合了平均场预测与精确量子动力学之间的差距，为理解有限量子多体系统中经典非线性行为的涌现提供了见解，揭示了宏观量子自陷在量子精确描述下的局限性。

Abstract: We investigate the fully quantum evolution of the population imbalance in a perfectly symmetric Bose-Josephson junction modeled by a two-mode Bose-Hubbard Hamiltonian, focusing on the validity of macroscopic quantum self-trapping beyond the mean-field theory. We show that for any finite number of particles the exact quantum dynamics leads to the breakdown of macroscopic quantum self-trapping after a finite time, regardless of the initial state. Using the symmetries of the Bose-Hubbard Hamiltonian, we provide a mathematical demonstration of this result and analyze the spectral properties governing the dynamics. We identify a branching behavior in the eigenvalues differences and a nontrivial structure of the population-imbalance amplitudes. These features allow us to distinguish two clearly different dynamical regimes and to elucidate the mechanism leading to the emergence of a quasi-MQST regime for large particle numbers. These findings bridge the gap between mean-field predictions and exact quantum dynamics and provide insight into the emergence of classical nonlinear behavior from finite quantum many-body systems.

### [82] [Equal-spin and opposite-spin density-density correlations in the BCS-BEC crossover: Gauge Symmetry, Pauli Exclusion Principle, Wick's Theorem and Experiments](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.23019)
*Nikolai Kaschewski,Axel Pelster,Carlos A. R. Sá de Melo*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 该研究建立了一个适用于任意温度、相互作用、维度和质量或粒子数状态的二分量费米气体的自旋依赖密度-密度关联（spin-dependent density-density correlations）普适理论，并通过二维零温下从BCS到玻色（Bose）区间的实例分析，揭示了集体激发、多粒子散射和顶点修正等不可约二粒子贡献对实验观测的关键作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在发展一个普适的理论框架来描述二分量费米气体的自旋依赖密度-密度关联，该框架需适用于广泛的物理条件（任意温度、相互作用、维度等）。研究动机源于需要建立与规范不变性（gauge invariance）和泡利原理（Pauli principle）一致的理论约束，并能解释实验观测到的现象。

Method: 研究基于规范不变性和泡利原理，建立了自旋依赖密度-密度关联的理论约束，确保其与涨落-耗散定理（fluctuation-dissipation theorem）和维克定理（Wick's theorem）的一致性。作为具体应用，研究以6Li实验为启发，分析了二维零温下从BCS（Bardeen-Cooper-Schrieffer）到玻色区间的关联特性。

Result: 理论分析表明，涉及集体激发（collective excitations）、多粒子散射（many-particle scattering）和顶点修正（vertex corrections）的不可约二粒子（two-particle irreducible）贡献对于准确描述实验至关重要。特别地，这些贡献是导致实验观测到的反自旋密度-密度关联（opposite-spin density-density correlations）中出现极小值的原因。

Conclusion: 研究成功建立了一个普适的自旋依赖密度-密度关联理论框架，并通过具体实例证明，超越平均场近似的多体效应（如集体激发和顶点修正）对于解释实验观测到的关联特征具有决定性作用，强调了在描述强关联费米系统时考虑这些不可约贡献的必要性。

Abstract: We develop a general theory of spin-dependent density-density correlations, that is valid for any temperature, interactions, dimensions and mass or population status of Fermi gases with two internal states. We use gauge invariance and the Pauli principle to establish constraints on the spin-dependent density-density correlations that are consistent with the fluctuation-dissipation and Wick's theorem. As an example, we study the spin-dependent density-density correlations from the BCS to the Bose regime in two dimensions at zero temperature, inspired by experiments in 6Li. We show that two-particle irreducible contributions involving collective excitations, many-particle scattering and vertex corrections, are essential to describe experiments. In particular they turn out to be responsible for the emergence of an experimentally observed minimum in the opposite-spin density-density correlations.

</details>


### [83] [Finite-time thermal refrigerator in interacting Bose-Einstein Condensates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.23074)
*Joaquín I. Ganly,Julián Amette Estrada,Franco Mayo,Augusto J. Roncaglia,Pablo D. Mininni*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 该研究通过数值模拟实现了三维弱相互作用玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体（BEC）中的有限时间热力学制冷循环，在连续循环中实现了约27%的冷却效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在探索相互作用玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体（BEC）在现实条件下能否维持有限时间量子热循环，为研究不同制冷方案、优化控制协议和绝热捷径提供平台。

Method: 采用三维弱相互作用BEC系统，包含三个空间分离的凝聚体（系统、活塞和储热器），通过时变势垒实现压缩、膨胀和接触冲程。使用随机金兹堡-朗道方程（Stochastic Ginzburg-Landau equation）生成有限温度初始态，并通过截断格罗斯-皮塔耶夫斯基方程（truncated Gross-Pitaevskii equation）演化动力学。采用动量空间测温法测量各凝聚体温度。

Result: 尽管存在质量转移和声激发，协议在连续循环中实现了成功冷却：第一循环温度降低约20%，第二循环进一步冷却但效果减弱，最终达到从初始状态约27%的冷却效果。

Conclusion: 相互作用玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体能够在现实条件下维持有限时间量子热循环，为探索不同制冷方案、优化控制协议和绝热捷径提供了可行平台。

Abstract: We study a finite-time thermodynamic refrigeration cycle realized numerically in three-dimensional, weakly interacting Bose-Einstein condensates (BECs). The setup consists of three spatially separated condensates -- system, piston, and reservoir -- coupled through time-dependent potential barriers that implement compression, expansion, and contact strokes. Finite-temperature initial states are generated with the Stochastic Ginzburg-Landau equation, and the subsequent dynamics are evolved using the truncated Gross-Pitaevskii equation. To measure temperatures we use a momentum-space thermometry method that provides estimates for each condensate. We find that despite mass transfer and sound excitations, the protocol achieves successful cooling during consecutive cycles: the first cycle lowers its temperature by ~20%, and a second cycle yields additional, though reduced, cooling, reaching a final ~27% cooling from the initial state. Our results show that interacting BECs can sustain finite-time quantum thermal cycles under realistic conditions, and provide a platform for exploring different refrigeration schemes, optimized control protocols, and shortcuts to adiabaticity.

</details>


### [84] [A Maxwell Fish-Eye Lens in a Bose-Einstein Condensate](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.23125)
*Jelte Duchêne,Elinor Kath,Floriane Arrouas,Hanyi Jang,Helmut Strobel,Markus K. Oberthaler,Jay Mehta,Liam M. Farrell,Wyatt Kirkby,Duncan H. J. O'Dell*

TL;DR: 实验上在玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体（Bose-Einstein condensate）中利用声子激发实现了光学麦克斯韦鱼眼透镜（Maxwell fish-eye lens）的声学类比，展示了梯度折射率透镜在超冷原子系统中的可行性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 麦克斯韦鱼眼透镜（MFEL）具有独特的完美聚焦特性，但在传统光学系统中实现梯度折射率透镜具有挑战性。玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体（BEC）为调控集体激发的声速提供了高度可调的平台，可用于模拟此类透镜效应。

Method: 在玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体（BEC）中利用声子（phonons）激发实现麦克斯韦鱼眼透镜（MFEL）的声学类比。通过调控集体激发的空间变化声速来设计有效折射率，并进行声子波前的时间分辨测量。

Result: 声子波前的时间分辨测量显示出聚焦行为，与解析理论和数值模拟结果吻合良好。该工作成功演示了利用超冷原子工程有效折射指数并模拟有效球面几何上波传播的能力。

Conclusion: 该研究为利用超冷原子工程有效折射指数提供了几何和物理框架，并展示了在有效球面几何上模拟波传播的可能性，拓展了梯度折射率透镜在量子模拟平台中的应用。

Abstract: We experimentally realize an analogue of the optical Maxwell fish-eye lens (MFEL) using phononic excitations in a Bose-Einstein condensate (BEC). A MFEL is characterized by a radially symmetric, spatially varying refractive index with the remarkable property that rays emitted from any point within the lens are perfectly focused at their image points. While the implementation of such gradient-index lenses is challenging in conventional optical systems, BECs offer a highly tunable platform in which the spatially varying speed of sound of collective excitations -- phonons, the acoustic-wave analogues of photons -- can be engineered and their dynamics observed in real time. Time-resolved measurements of phonon wavefronts reveal focusing behavior that shows good agreement with analytical theory and numerical simulations. This work provides both a geometric and physical framework for engineering effective refractive indices using ultracold atoms, and simulating wave propagation on effective spherical geometries.

</details>

### [85] [Twisting BFSS & IKKT](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.22318)
*Fabian Hahner,Natalie M. Paquette*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文研究了BFSS矩阵量子力学和IKKT矩阵模型在N→∞极限下的"扭曲全息术（twisted holography）"，建立了这些矩阵模型与IIA/IIB弦理论相应扭曲版本之间的对应关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在启动对涉及BFSS矩阵量子力学和IKKT矩阵模型在N→∞极限下的"扭曲全息术（twisted holography）"研究，探索这些矩阵模型与弦理论之间的扭曲对应关系。

Method: 作者识别了每个模型的可容许扭曲（admissible twists），在BV-BRST形式体系中计算了它们的上同调（cohomology），并在平面极限（planar limit）和围绕平凡背景的微扰理论中，分别将它们与IIA和IIB弦理论的相应扭曲版本对应起来。

Result: 扭曲的引力对偶揭示了某些无限维对称代数。在BFSS例子中，IIA超引力（supergravity）的扭曲也通过十一维超引力的最小（1/16-BPS）和最大（1/4-BPS）扭曲的特定零模截断获得。

Conclusion: 该研究成功建立了BFSS矩阵量子力学与IIA弦理论、IKKT矩阵模型与IIB弦理论在扭曲框架下的对应关系，为理解矩阵模型与弦理论的全息对偶提供了新的扭曲视角。

Abstract: In this note we initiate the study of ``twisted holography'' for the dualities involving the BFSS matrix quantum mechanics and the IKKT matrix model in their $N \rightarrow \infty$ limits. We identify the admissible twists of each model, compute their cohomology in the BV-BRST formalism, and identify them -- in the planar limit and in perturbation theory around the trivial background -- with corresponding twists of IIA and IIB string theories, respectively. The twisted gravitational duals make manifest certain infinite dimensional symmetry algebras. In the BFSS example, the dual IIA supergravity twists are also obtained as certain zero mode truncations of the minimal (1/16-BPS) and maximal (1/4-BPS) twists of eleven-dimensional supergravity.

</details>


### [86] [Resurgence in the Virasoro Minimal String and 3d Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.22335)
*Maximilian Schwick*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文使用厄米矩阵模型技术计算了Virasoro最小弦和三维引力的非微扰、复苏贡献，构建了完全非微扰配分函数，并研究了ZZ-与FZZT膜之间的复苏壁交叉现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于计算Virasoro最小弦（Virasoro minimal string）和三维引力（3d gravity）的非微扰贡献，特别是通过厄米矩阵模型（hermitian matrix models）技术来理解这些理论中的复苏现象（resurgent phenomena）。

Method: 采用厄米矩阵模型技术，构建了Virasoro最小弦的完全非微扰配分函数（non-perturbative partition function），使用Zak变换（Zak transform）表示。通过研究谱曲线（spectral curve）上的负张力D膜（negative tension D-branes）和反本征值（anti-eigenvalues），分析了ZZ-与FZZT膜之间的复苏壁交叉现象（resurgent wall crossing phenomena）。

Result: 发现三维引力中求和亏格（summing over the genus）会产生双指数型非微扰贡献（doubly exponential type non-perturbative contributions）。在一般厄米矩阵模型中，本征值分布边缘的渐近行为变化被识别为斯托克斯跃迁（Stokes transition），本征值密度振荡与FZZT膜的反斯托克斯行为（anti-Stokes behavior）相关。对于带世界末端膜的三维引力，该斯托克斯跃迁与黑洞行为起始一致。

Conclusion: 研究表明厄米矩阵模型技术能有效分析Virasoro最小弦和三维引力的非微扰结构，揭示了复苏现象与斯托克斯跃迁之间的深刻联系，为理解量子引力中的非微扰效应提供了新视角。

Abstract: We compute non-perturbative, resurgent contributions to the Virasoro minimal string and 3d gravity using techniques from hermitian matrix models. In particular, we construct a fully non-perturbative partition function for the Virasoro minimal string in terms of a Zak transform. In this context, negative tension D-branes appear naturally, which in the matrix model correspond to anti-eigenvalues, or instantons on the involuted sheet of the spectral curve. We further extend this analysis to resolvents and observe resurgent wall crossing phenomena between ZZ- and FZZT-branes. Using recent results that relate the Virasoro minimal string to 3d gravity with end-of-the-world branes we proceed to study the resurgent consequences of summing over the genus in 3d gravity, where we find non-perturbative contributions of doubly exponential type. These statements are then tested using resurgent large-order asymptotics. Lastly, we compute the non-perturbative eigenvalue density for generic hermitian matrix models and identify the change of asymptotic behavior at the edge of the eigenvalue distribution with a Stokes transition. This allows us to identify oscillations in the eigenvalue density with anti-Stokes behavior of FZZT-branes. In the case of 3d gravity with end-of-the-world branes we comment how this Stokes transition coincides with the onset of black hole behaviour and compute the non-perturbative primary density. Furthermore, we apply these techniques to the eigenvalue density of JT gravity to compute higher genus corrections.

</details>


### [87] [Strings on freely acting orbifolds: Spectra, moduli spaces and branes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.22354)
*George Gkountoumis*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文研究了IIB型弦理论在自由作用轨道折叠（freely acting orbifolds）上的紧致化，特别关注非几何弦紧致化的不对称轨道折叠（asymmetric orbifolds），并探讨了其超对称性、模空间、沼泽地猜想（swampland program）及D-膜谱系等关键方面。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索弦理论景观（string landscape）中非几何弦紧致化的一个有趣角落——不对称轨道折叠。这些构造提供了研究自由作用轨道折叠各种特性的平台，包括超对称性破缺、模空间结构以及与有效超重力理论的联系。

Method: 采用两种互补方法描述轨道折叠：对偶扭曲（duality twists）和格点方法（lattice approach）。首先讨论自由作用（不对称）轨道折叠的一般构造，重点关注闭弦扇区（closed string sector）。通过构建保持五维中$\mathcal{N} = 6,4,2$或$0$超对称性的具体例子，并将最轻的非扭曲轨道折叠态与有效超重力理论中的态相匹配，建立与Scherk-Schwarz约化的联系。

Result: 研究结果表明：在模空间（moduli space）的特殊点处，通常有质量的扭曲扇区态（twisted sectors）可以变为无质量；非超对称轨道折叠的谱系在远离模空间特殊轨迹时可以无快子（tachyon-free）。对于保持五维$\mathcal{N} = 2$超对称性的轨道折叠，确定了经典超多重态（hypermultiplet）和矢量多重态（vector multiplet）模空间，并通过构建对偶轨道折叠对论证了矢量多重态模空间度规无量子修正。验证了沼泽地距离猜想（swampland distance conjecture）在研究的非几何紧致化中成立，并确定了各种D-膜在轨道折叠化后存留的条件。

Conclusion: 该论文系统研究了IIB型弦理论在自由作用不对称轨道折叠上的紧致化，揭示了非几何弦紧致化的多个重要特性：包括超对称性破缺模式、模空间结构、与有效理论的对应关系、沼泽地猜想的适用性以及D-膜谱系的存留条件，为理解弦理论景观中的非几何构造提供了深入见解。

Abstract: In this dissertation, we study various aspects of type IIB string theory compactified on freely acting orbifolds. We focus particularly on asymmetric orbifolds, which are examples of non-geometric string compactifications and constitute an intriguing corner in the string landscape. We describe the orbifolds using two complementary approaches; the duality twists and the lattice approach. First, we discuss the general construction of freely acting (asymmetric) orbifolds, focusing on the closed string sector. Afterwards, we present explicit examples of orbifolds preserving $\mathcal{N} = 6,4,2$ or $0$ supersymmetry in five dimensions and we demonstrate the connection between freely acting orbifolds and Scherk-Schwarz reductions by matching the lightest untwisted orbifold states with those arising form the effective supergravity theory. Regarding the orbifold twisted sectors, we show that at special points in the moduli space, generically massive states can become massless. Furthermore, we show that the spectrum of non-supersymmetric orbifolds can become tachyon-free away from special loci in the moduli space. Next, we turn our attention to the orbifold moduli space, and we focus on orbifolds preserving $\mathcal{N} = 2$ supersymmetry in five dimensions, for which we determine the classical hypermultiplet and vector multiplet moduli spaces. Moreover, by constructing dual orbifold pairs, we argue that no quantum corrections to the metric on the vector multiplet moduli space arise. Then, we discuss aspects of the swampland program in the context of freely acting asymmetric orbifolds and we verify that the swampland distance conjecture is valid in the non-geometric compactifications of string theory studied in this thesis. Finally, we focus on the D-brane spectrum of freely acting orbifolds and we determine the conditions under which the various D-branes survive the orbifolding.

</details>


### [88] [Continuous symmetries and charge measurement of boundary operators in holography](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.22377)
*Ibrahima Bah,Federico Bonetti,Mufaro Chitoto,Enoch Leung*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该研究探讨全息对偶（holographic duality）中连续内对称性（continuous internal symmetries）的电荷测量问题，通过边界算符与体规范场（bulk gauge fields）的威尔逊线（Wilson lines）关联，以及悬挂缺陷（hanging defects）实现测量过程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于理解全息对偶框架下连续内对称性的电荷测量机制，探索边界算符与体规范场之间的对应关系，以及如何通过几何构造模拟场论中的对称性算符正则化。

Method: 采用低能有效理论方法推导电荷测量过程的普适特征，并在Type IIB弦理论和M理论中的AdS/CFT框架下提供具体的"自上而下"（top-down）实现，涵盖阿贝尔（Abelian）和非阿贝尔（non-Abelian）对称性。

Result: 研究揭示了悬挂缺陷图像如何模拟场论中连续对称性算符的增厚正则化（thickening regularization），分析了Type IIB构造中支撑电荷测量过程的膜动力学（brane dynamics），并证明了悬挂膜构型具有拓扑特性，其融合规则（fusion rules）可通过快子动力学（tachyon dynamics）解释。

Conclusion: 该工作建立了全息电荷测量的系统框架，通过具体的弦理论实现验证了理论预测，揭示了悬挂缺陷的拓扑性质及其与场论正则化过程的对应关系，为理解全息对偶中的对称性测量提供了新视角。

Abstract: We study holographic charge measurement for continuous internal symmetries. Charged boundary operators are characterized by Wilson lines of bulk gauge fields ending on the boundary, while charge measurement is performed using U-shaped defects hanging from the boundary. We derive universal features of this process from a low-energy point of view, and show how the hanging defect picture mimics the thickening regularization of continuous symmetry operators in field theory. Furthermore, we provide explicit top-down realizations in AdS/CFT setups in Type IIB string theory and M-theory, featuring Abelian as well as non-Abelian symmetries. In the case of Type IIB constructions, we analyze the brane dynamics underlying the charge measurement process. Along the way, we also characterize how hanging brane configurations can be regarded as being topological, and demonstrate how tachyon dynamics account for their fusion rules.

### [89] [Self-Dual Gauge Fields from Superstring Field Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.22420)
*Chris Hull*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 从新构建的超弦场论中推导出自对偶规范场的作用量，该理论在特定极限下简化为Sen的理论，并描述了两个解耦的自对偶规范场分别耦合到两个度规的情形。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 基于最近构建的超弦场论（superstring field theory），探索其中涌现的自对偶规范场（self-dual gauge fields）的作用量形式，并建立与Sen理论之间的联系。

Method: 通过分析新构建的超弦场论，推导出自对偶规范场的作用量，并研究其在特定极限下如何简化为Sen的理论框架。

Result: 发现该理论描述了两个解耦的自对偶规范场，每个场仅耦合到一个度规，同时存在背景度规，且与这三个度规的非线性耦合是非标准的。理论具有两个自旋为二的规范不变性，微分同胚（diffeomorphisms）来自对角子群。

Conclusion: 新构建的超弦场论在特定极限下还原为Sen的理论，同时为自对偶规范场提供了新的作用量描述，揭示了其与多个度规的非标准耦合关系及规范对称性结构。

Abstract: The action for self-dual gauge fields that emerges from the recently constructed superstring field theory is found. The new superstring field theory reduces to that of Sen in a certain limit, and in this limit the new action for self-dual gauge fields reduces to Sen's action for such fields. The theory describes two decoupled self-dual gauge fields that couple to two metrics, with each gauge field coupling to only one of the metrics. The action also features a background metric, and the non-linear coupling to these three metrics is non-standard. There are two spin-two gauge invariances, and diffeomorphisms arise from the diagonal subgroup.

</details>


### [90] [Three-Dimensional Modified Klein--Gordon Oscillator in Standard and Generalized Doubly Special Relativity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.22444)
*Abdelmalek Boumali,Nosratollah Jafari*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究双狭义相对论（DSR）在三维克莱因-戈登振子（Klein-Gordon oscillator）中的实现，通过分析变形色散关系对束缚态能谱的影响，获得了闭式能谱和普朗克尺度修正，为不同DSR方案在三维设置中的直接比较提供了分析框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 双狭义相对论（Doubly Special Relativity, DSR）在不变光速c之外引入了第二个观测者无关的尺度（通常与普朗克尺度相关），本文旨在量化该原理在典型可精确求解束缚态问题中的效应，为不同DSR实现方案提供直接比较的基础。

Method: 研究采用三维克莱因-戈登振子作为原型系统，分析两种标准DSR实现（Amelino-Camelia和Magueijo-Smolin）以及基于普朗克长度一阶展开的广义DSR框架。通过定态约化和球坐标分离，保持未变形振子的广义拉盖尔函数和球谐函数结构，同时DSR变形了代数量子化条件。

Result: 对于标准DSR情况获得了闭式能谱，对于广义模型推导了普朗克尺度抑制的微扰修正。在所有实现中，变形诱导了正负能量解的分支依赖偏移，这些偏移随激发增加而增大，并在k→∞或l_p→0极限下平滑消失。

Conclusion: 本文成功提取了分析能谱和普朗克尺度修正，使得在完全三维设置中直接比较不同DSR方案成为可能，为理解DSR原理在束缚态系统中的具体表现提供了定量框架。

Abstract: Doubly Special Relativity (DSR) augments special relativity by introducing, alongside the invariant speed of light $c$, a second observer-independent scale typically associated with the Planck regime. At the level of effective wave equations this principle manifests itself through deformed dispersion relations and energy-dependent spatial operators. Here we quantify such effects in a prototypical exactly solvable bound-state problem: the three-dimensional Klein--Gordon oscillator generated by a non-minimal momentum coupling that yields isotropic harmonic confinement while preserving rotational symmetry. We analyze two standard DSR realizations (Amelino--Camelia and Magueijo--Smolin, parametrized by an invariant energy scale $k$) as well as a generalized DSR framework based on a first-order expansion in the Planck length $l_p$. After stationary reduction and separation in spherical coordinates, the eigenfunctions retain the generalized-Laguerre and spherical-harmonic structure of the undeformed oscillator, whereas DSR deforms the algebraic quantization condition that relates the principal oscillator number $N=2n+\ell\in\mathbb{N}_0$ to the relativistic energy. Closed-form spectra are obtained for the standard DSR cases, and perturbative Planck-suppressed shifts are derived for the generalized model. In all realizations the deformation induces branch-dependent shifts of both positive- and negative-energy solutions, which increase with excitation and vanish smoothly in the limits $k\to\infty$ or $l_p\to0$. The main goal of this paper is to extract analytic spectra and Planck-suppressed shifts that enable a direct comparison between different DSR prescriptions in a fully three-dimensional setting.

</details>

*Guillaume Bossard,Nicolas Boulanger,Josh O'Connor*

Method: 在E11异常场论（E11 exceptional field theory）框架内，从伪拉格朗日量出发，构造了与三形式场、六形式场和对偶引力子相关的所有高阶梯度对偶场的母作用量（parent actions）。

Abstract: It has been conjectured that there exists an E11-invariant formulation of eleven-dimensional supergravity in which the propagating fields of the theory are realised through an infinite tower of higher duals. In this work, we prove this conjecture explicitly within E11 exceptional field theory at the linearised level. Starting from the pseudo-Lagrangian, we construct parent actions for all higher gradient dual fields that are associated with the three-form, the six-form, and the dual graviton. We show that the resulting Euler-Lagrange equations constrain the Stueckelberg fields to be pure curls, ensuring that the higher duals propagate the same physical degrees of freedom as the original supergravity fields. The additional Stueckelberg fields, which are not predicted by the tensor hierarchy algebra, are shown to play a specific role as sources for the Labastida tensors of the higher dual fields.

We identify the quantum effects coming from Lorentz violation in an explicitly gauge invariant way. Nonlinear Lorentz-violating contributions that may affect photon-photon scattering are explicitly evaluated.

### [93] [A Perfectoid Duality Between M-Theory and F-Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.22503)
*Arshid Shabir,Bobby Eka Gunara,Mir Faizal*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种非奇异的、定义层面的F理论（F-theory）表述，通过用基于完美胚几何（perfectoid geometry）和凝聚数学（condensed mathematics）的塔完备化圆（tower-completed circle）上的紧致化，替代传统的M理论（M-theory）收缩纤维极限。该框架为模数据（modular data）提供了内在的十一维载体，并建立了精确的M理论/IIB型理论字典。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统F理论表述依赖于M理论的收缩纤维极限，这导致了奇异性问题。本文旨在提供一个非奇异的、定义层面的F理论基础，避免传统方法中的数学困难。

Method: 采用完美胚几何和凝聚数学工具，将M理论在塔完备化圆（tower-completed circle）上紧致化，而非传统的收缩纤维极限。该构造包含规范的倾斜（tilting）和比较程序，将椭圆几何（elliptic geometry）作为输出而非辅助输入。

Result: 建立了精确的M理论/IIB型理论字典，表明物理轴子-伸缩子（axio-dilaton）由十一维几何和拓扑数据固定。在十维玻色有效作用量层面验证了对应关系，包括从十一维继承的拓扑耦合。塔完备化几何自然地组织了广义上同调（generalized cohomology）中的全局扇区，电荷数据由K理论（K-theory）支配并展示规范的素数幂挠结构（prime-power torsion structure）。

Conclusion: 该框架为F理论及其扩展提供了连贯的非奇异基础，可推广到变耦合背景、对偶缺陷（duality defects）、自然阿德尔完备化（adelic completion）以及更高秩和U对偶几何（U-duality geometries）。还讨论了全息方面和对偶群在玻色截断之外的异常精细化扩展。

Abstract: We present a non-singular, definition-level formulation of F-theory by replacing the traditional shrinking-fiber limit of M-theory with compactification on a tower-completed circle described using perfectoid geometry and condensed mathematics. This construction provides an intrinsic eleven-dimensional carrier for modular data and admits a canonical tilting and comparison procedure that yields elliptic geometry as an output rather than an auxiliary input. Using this framework, we establish a precise M-theory/Type IIB dictionary in the constant-coupling sector, showing how the physical axio-dilaton is fixed by eleven-dimensional geometric and topological data. The correspondence is tested at the level of the ten-dimensional bosonic effective action, including its topological couplings inherited from eleven dimensions. The tower-completed geometry naturally organizes global sectors in generalized cohomology, with charge data governed by K-theory and exhibiting a canonical prime-power torsion structure. We further show how this framework extends to varying-coupling backgrounds and duality defects, admits a natural adelic completion with prime-independence, and generalizes to higher-rank and U-duality geometries. We also discuss holographic aspects and the anomaly-refined extension of the duality group beyond the bosonic truncation. Together, these results provide a coherent, non-singular foundation for F-theory and its extensions.

</details>


### [94] [Geodesic equation in noncommutative space: a field theory perspective](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.22726)
*Carolina Matté Gregory,Tajron Jurić,Aleksandr Pinzul*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文通过场论方法推导了Moyal型非对易时空中的测地线方程，发现所有非对易效应被吸收到一个有效的位置依赖质量函数中，导致测地线方程出现额外的固定外力项。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究非对易时空（noncommutative spacetime）中点粒子的传播动力学，特别是从场论角度推导其测地线方程（geodesic equation），以理解量子时空结构对经典粒子运动的影响。

Method: 采用基于非对易克莱因-戈尔登方程（noncommutative Klein-Gordon equation）准经典极限的场论方法，从协变拉普拉斯-贝尔特拉米算子（covariant Laplace-Beltrami operator）的扭曲几何构造出发，推导非对易哈密顿-雅可比方程（Hamilton-Jacobi equation）。

Result: 所有非对易效应被吸收到有效的位置依赖质量函数M(x)中，测地线方程获得额外外力项F_NC^μ = -½ g^{μν}∂_νM²(x)。微扰计算显示奇数次修正恒为零，对于(r-θ)扭曲的球对称背景，主要修正出现在Θ²阶且与探测粒子质量成正比，无质量粒子不受影响。

Conclusion: 非对易时空中的粒子动力学可通过有效质量函数完全描述，测地线方程获得由量子时空本质产生的固定外力项，为理解量子引力效应提供了新的理论框架。

Abstract: We derive the geodesic equation for point particles propagating in Moyal-type noncommutative spacetimes using a field-theoretic approach based on the quasi-classical limit of the noncommutative Klein-Gordon equation. Starting from a twisted-geometric construction of the covariant Laplace-Beltrami operator, we obtain the noncommutative Hamilton-Jacobi equation and show that all noncommutative effects are absorbed into an effective, position-dependent mass function $M(x)$ appearing in an otherwise standard relativistic dispersion relation. The corresponding particle dynamics then acquires an additional term in the geodesic equation that takes the form of a fixed external force $F_{\text{NC}}^μ= -\frac{1}{2} g^{μν}\partial_νM^2(x)$, sourced entirely by the quantum nature of spacetime. We compute this effective mass perturbatively up to fourth order in the noncommutativity parameter for a general metric, proving that all odd-order corrections vanish identically. For the specific case of an $(r-θ)$ twist applied to spherically symmetric backgrounds, we obtain explicit expressions demonstrating that the leading correction to geodesic motion appears at $Θ^2$ order and is proportional to the probe particle's mass, while massless particles remain unaffected.

</details>


### [95] [Magnetized BPS lumps in the $CP^1$ model with Maxwell coupling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.22957)
*I. B. Cunha,F. C. E. Lima,Aldo Vera*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了$CP^1$模型与Maxwell规范场最小耦合中的BPS拓扑构型，通过数值求解BPS方程，发现了由$CP^1$目标空间几何纯几何起源的规则、磁局域且能量稳定的磁化lump构型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探究$CP^1$模型与Maxwell规范场最小耦合中的Bogomolnyi-Prasad-Sommerfield (BPS)拓扑构型，特别关注从非线性$O(3)$ sigma模型到$CP^1$表述的经典映射，以及由Fubini-Study目标空间几何内禀产生的局部$U(1)$规范对称性。

Method: 方法包括：从非线性$O(3)$ sigma模型显式构造到$CP^1$表述的经典映射；在静态扇区分析磁化BPS lump构型；通过拓扑边界条件证明磁通量子化；在BPS框架内识别自对偶构型所需的自相互作用势；对lump核心和空间无穷远处的渐近行为进行详细分析；数值求解BPS方程。

Result: 研究发现：磁通是量子化的，完全由规范场的渐近行为决定；有限能量解必然对应$CP^1$目标空间中的lump-like BPS构型，标量场渐近消失；数值求解BPS方程得到的构型是规则的、磁局域且能量稳定的；与Abelian Higgs涡旋不同，这些构型不依赖于自发对称性破缺，而是纯几何起源。

Conclusion: 结论表明，在$CP^1$模型与Maxwell规范场最小耦合中，存在由$CP^1$目标空间几何刚性控制的BPS拓扑构型，这些构型的内部结构完全由几何决定，与基于自发对称性破缺的传统Abelian Higgs涡旋机制形成鲜明对比。

Abstract: We investigate Bogomolnyi-Prasad-Sommerfield (BPS) topological configurations in the $CP^1$ model minimally coupled to a Maxwell gauge field. Starting from the nonlinear $O(3)$ sigma model, we explicitly construct its classical mapping to the $CP^1$ formulation, emphasizing the emergence of a local $U(1)$ gauge symmetry intrinsically linked to the Fubini-Study target-space geometry. Focusing on the static sector, we analyze magnetized BPS lump configurations. By examining the topological boundary conditions, we show that the magnetic flux is quantized and fully determined by the asymptotic behavior of the gauge field. Within the BPS framework, we identify the specific self-interaction potential required for the existence of self-dual configurations. A detailed analysis of the asymptotic behavior, both near the lump core and at spatial infinity, demonstrates that finite-energy solutions necessarily correspond to lump-like BPS configurations in the $CP^1$ target space, with the scalar field vanishing asymptotically. The resulting BPS equations are solved numerically, and the main physical properties of the solutions are presented. We find that these configurations are regular, magnetically localized, and energetically stable, with their internal structure rigidly controlled by the geometry of the $CP^1$ target space. In contrast to Abelian Higgs vortices, the configurations discussed here do not rely on spontaneous symmetry breaking but arise purely from the geometry of the $CP^1$ target space.

</details>


### [96] [Holomorphic Quantization in Constant Curvature Backgrounds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.22984)
*Dmitri Bykov,Viacheslav Krivorol*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种自由点粒子在二维常曲率黎曼背景上的全纯量子化方案，该方法基于将粒子构型空间嵌入背景等距群余伴随轨道的乘积中，并以平面、环面、球面和双曲平面为例进行了验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在为二维常曲率黎曼背景上的自由点粒子开发一种全纯量子化方案（holomorphic quantization scheme），以统一处理平面、环面、球面和双曲平面等不同几何背景下的量子化问题。

Method: 方法基于拉格朗日嵌入（Lagrangian embedding），将粒子构型空间嵌入背景等距群（isometry group）的余伴随轨道（coadjoint orbits）的乘积中，并通过具体例子（包括有无单极场的情况）详细阐述了该方法。

Result: 通过该方法成功恢复了这些空间上的哈密顿量谱（Hamiltonian spectrum）和波函数，并作为副产品获得了Repka关于$\mathbf{SL}(2,\mathbb{R})$离散级数表示张量积分解结果的几何与物理解释。

Conclusion: 该全纯量子化方案为二维常曲率黎曼背景上的自由点粒子提供了统一的量子化框架，不仅能够恢复已知的哈密顿量谱和波函数，还为相关数学结果提供了物理和几何解释。

Abstract: We present a holomorphic quantization scheme for free point particles on two-dimensional constant curvature Riemannian backgrounds. The procedure is based on a Lagrangian embedding of the particle configuration space into a product of coadjoint orbits of the background isometry group. Examples are provided by particles on the plane, torus, sphere, and hyperbolic plane, with or without a monopole field. We elaborate the method by recovering the Hamiltonian spectrum and the wave functions on such spaces. As a by-product, we obtain a geometric and physical interpretation of Repka's result on the decomposition of tensor products of $\mathbf{SL}(2,\mathbb{R})$ discrete series representations.

</details>


### [97] [CFT derivation of entanglement phase transition in pseudo entropy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.22994)
*Hiroki Kanda,Tadashi Takayanagi,Zixia Wei*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究了共形场论（CFT）中伪熵（pseudo entropy）的纠缠相变，特别关注由边界条件改变算符（boundary condition changing operators）连接的不同边界态（boundary states）情况，发现伪熵随算符共形权重的变化呈现相变，并在全息CFT中与AdS计算结果一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在探讨共形场论中伪熵的纠缠相变现象，特别关注当输入态（in-state）和输出态（out-state）为通过边界条件改变算符连接的不同边界态时的情况。

Method: 采用边界共形场论（BCFT）方法计算伪熵，分析其随边界条件改变算符的共形权重（conformal weight）变化的行为，并在全息CFT（holographic CFTs）中验证结果。

Result: 研究发现伪熵随边界条件改变算符的共形权重变化呈现相变（phase transition），在全息CFT中，CFT计算结果与AdS（Anti-de Sitter space）中的评估结果一致。

Conclusion: 本文成功揭示了共形场论中伪熵的纠缠相变现象，特别在边界条件改变算符影响下的行为，并在全息对偶框架下验证了CFT与AdS计算结果的一致性。

Abstract: In this paper, we discuss the entanglement phase transition of pseudo entropy in CFTs. We focus on the case where the in-state and the out-state are different boundary states related by boundary condition changing operators. We compute the pseudo entropy with BCFT methods and find a phase transition with respect to the conformal weight of the boundary condition changing operators. For holographic CFTs, we confirm that the CFT results match that evaluated in AdS.

### [98] [On BRST Lagrangian description of partially massless bosonic fields](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.23091)
*I. L. Buchbinder,S. A. Fedoruk,V. A. Krykhtin*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文提出了四维空间中部分无质量（partially massless）玻色子场的完整BRST拉格朗日描述，证明了BRST电荷的厄米性和幂零性仅在dS空间中成立，并构建了包含(s-t)个Stückelberg场的规范不变拉格朗日量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于为四维空间中的部分无质量玻色子场提供完整的BRST拉格朗日描述，特别是在(A)dS空间中构建规范不变的场论框架。

Method: 采用两分量自旋张量（two-component spin-tensors）表述基本场，将部分无质量场的质量壳（mass shell）重新表述为Fock空间矢量约束，并开发了将第二类约束（second-class constraints）转换为第一类约束（first-class constraints）的转换程序。

Result: 成功构建了厄米且幂零的BRST电荷，证明厄米性和幂零性限制了理论参数条件，这些条件仅在dS空间中满足，而在AdS空间中不兼容。构建的规范不变拉格朗日量仅包含(s-t)个Stückelberg场，其运动方程精确再现质量壳条件。

Conclusion: 该研究为四维(A)dS空间中的部分无质量玻色子场提供了完整的BRST拉格朗日描述，揭示了BRST电荷的厄米性要求与AdS空间的不兼容性，并展示了规范变换与Stückelberg场排除之间的对应关系。

Abstract: We present an exhaustive BRST lagrangian description of partially massless bosonic fields in four-dimensional space. The basic fields are formulated in terms of two-component spin-tensors in (A)dS space where the tracelessness conditions are automatically fulfilled. The mass shell of partially massless fields is reformulated in terms of constraints on Fock space vectors including the second-class constraints. A conversion procedure for transforming second-class constraints into first-class ones is developed, allowing one to construct a Hermitian and nilpotent BRST charge in the Fock space under consideration. It is proven that the hermiticity and nilpotency restrict the conditions on the theory parameters, which are fulfilled only in dS space. The hermiticity of the BRST charge is incompatible with AdS space. The gauge invariant Lagrangian is constructed on the basis of the BRST charge, and for spin $s$ and depth $t$ the allowed states in the Lagrangian include only $(s-t)$ Stückelberg fields. Their exclusion leads to gauge transformations of degree $(s-t)$ for the physical fields. The Lagrangian equations of motion exactly reproduce the mass shell conditions. The Lagrangian in terms of conventional spin-tensor fields is also presented.

</details>
