### [99] [Probing the influence of topological and geometric disorder on the spectrum of the differential Laplacian operator on networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.22341)
*Charles Emmett Maher,Jeremy L. Marzuola,Katherine A. Newhall*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 该研究利用二维超均匀点模式的空间镶嵌生成紧凑度量网络结构，并分析这些网络上拉普拉斯算子的特征值谱结构，发现可通过控制边长分布和三角形面数量来调节谱隙宽度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 度量网络（metric networks）作为一维网络结构，可用于模拟共轭分子、光子晶体、波导网络量子力学和声学超材料等多种物理系统。研究旨在探索具有超均匀点模式结构的度量网络，这些结构在其他背景下已展现出奇异的物理特性。

Method: 采用二维超均匀点模式（hyperuniform point patterns）的空间镶嵌生成紧凑度量网络结构，这些点模式相对于典型无序点模式具有抑制的大尺度密度涨落。随后分析这些网络上微分拉普拉斯算子（Laplace operator）的特征值谱结构。

Result: 研究发现这些网络的特征值谱中可形成谱隙（spectral gaps），其宽度随边长分布变窄和三角形面数量增加而增大。许多考虑的结构可在欧几里得空间中实现，适用于超材料设计等实际应用。

Conclusion: 该工作可为设计具有可调宽度和位置的谱隙的度量网络系统提供指导，特别适用于需要特定频谱特性的超材料等实际应用场景。

Abstract: Metric networks are network-shaped, one-dimensional structures on which one can solve differential equations to simulate a wide range of physical systems including conjugated molecules, photonic crystals, quantum mechanics in waveguide networks, and acoustic metamaterials. More concretely, a metric network is a network whose edges are each assigned a notion of length and a coordinate describing position. One can then define function spaces and differential operators on these objects to model the aforementioned systems. Recent software advancements have made it feasible to analyze partial differential equations on large, compact metric networks with a vast array of structures. Here, we generate compact metric network structures using the spatial tessellations of two-dimensional hyperuniform point patterns, which have suppressed large-scale density fluctuations relative to typical disordered point patterns. This choice of structure is inspired by the exotic physical properties of network materials with these structures in other contexts. Then, we characterize the eigenvalue spectrum structure of the differential Laplace operator on these networks. In particular, we find that gaps can form in the eigenvalue spectra of these networks whose widths increase when the distribution of edge lengths is narrow and as the number of triangular faces increases. Importantly, many of the structures we consider are realizable in Euclidean space, meaning they are well-suited for practical applications in, e.g., metamaterial design. This work can thus be used to inform the design of metric network-based systems with spectral gaps with tunable widths and locations.

</details>


### [100] [Impact of Stealthy Hyperuniform Magnetic Impurity Configurations on Bulk Magnetism in a Two-dimensional Heisenberg Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.22484)
*K. Asakura,K. Yamamoto,A. Koga*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 研究高自旋磁性杂质在方形晶格反铁磁海森堡模型中的影响，比较随机、隐超均匀（stealthy hyperuniform）配置对体磁性的影响，发现三角晶格状排列能增强平均交错磁化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在阐明随机和隐超均匀（stealthy hyperuniform）杂质配置如何影响方形晶格反铁磁量子海森堡模型的体磁性质，特别关注高自旋磁性杂质的作用。

Method: 采用混合自旋模型的线性自旋波理论（linear spin-wave theory），通过广义成本函数生成隐超均匀配置，该函数能在方形晶格状和三角晶格状排列之间插值。

Result: 三角晶格状排列比随机和方形晶格状配置产生更大的平均交错磁化（average staggered magnetization）。这种增强源于亚晶格效应：方形晶格状配置由于其二分结构强制最近邻杂质占据相反亚晶格，而三角晶格状排列允许相同亚晶格的最近邻对，从而加强了协同磁增强。

Conclusion: 杂质配置的几何结构显著影响磁性增强效果，三角晶格状排列通过允许相同亚晶格的最近邻杂质对，提供了更强的协同磁增强机制。

Abstract: We investigate an antiferromagnetic quantum Heisenberg model on a square lattice with high-spin magnetic impurities to clarify how random and stealthy hyperuniform impurity configurations influence the bulk magnetic properties. Stealthy hyperuniform configurations are generated using generalized cost functions that interpolate between square-lattice-like and triangular-lattice-like arrangements. Using linear spin-wave theory for the mixed-spin model, we demonstrate that triangular-lattice-like arrangements yield a larger average staggered magnetization than both random and square-lattice-like cases. This enhancement originates from sublattice effects: while the square-lattice-like configuration enforces nearest-neighbor impurities to occupy opposite sublattices due to its bipartite structure, the triangular-lattice-like arrangement allows same-sublattice nearest-neighbor pairs, thereby strengthening cooperative magnetic enhancement.

</details>


### [101] [Exact mapping of a spin glass with correlated disorder to the pure Ising model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.22657)
*Hidetoshi Nishimori*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 该研究引入了一个具有关联无序（correlated disorder）的伊辛自旋玻璃模型，该模型在纯铁磁伊辛模型和具有对称无序的爱德华兹-安德森模型之间连续插值。研究证明了西岛线（Nishimori line）上的物理量可以通过纯伊辛模型在有效温度下的相应量精确表达，并揭示了该多临界点的临界行为类似于纯伊辛模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究的动机是探索自旋玻璃中相对未被充分研究的关联无序（correlated disorder）主题。通过引入一个在纯铁磁伊辛模型和标准爱德华兹-安德森模型之间连续插值的新模型，旨在理解无序关联如何影响多临界点的临界行为。

Method: 研究引入了一个具有关联无序的伊辛自旋玻璃模型，该模型包含一个连续插值参数。通过分析该模型在西岛线（Nishimori line）上的性质，证明了物理量可以通过纯伊辛模型在有效温度下的相应量精确表达。该方法适用于任意维度和任意晶格结构。

Result: 研究获得了多个精确关系：西岛线上的能量等于纯伊辛模型在有效温度下的能量（相差常数和简单因子）；比热等于纯伊辛模型在有效温度下的能量（而非比热）；磁化强度和关联函数等规范非不变（gauge-noninvariant）量也精确等于纯伊辛模型在有效温度下的对应量。这些关系表明，该关联无序模型在多临界点的临界行为类似于纯伊辛模型，而非标准爱德华兹-安德森模型的传统多临界普适类。

Conclusion: 该研究证明了具有关联无序的自旋玻璃模型在西岛线上展现出与纯伊辛模型相似的临界行为，这与标准爱德华兹-安德森模型的多临界普适类形成鲜明对比。这些结果为进一步探索自旋玻璃及相关问题中无序关联的相对未被充分研究的主题提供了动力。

Abstract: We introduce an Ising spin-glass model with correlated disorder which continuously interpolates between the pure ferromagnetic Ising model and the Edwards-Anderson model with symmetric disorder. For this model, we prove that physical quantities on the Nishimori line (NL) can be expressed exactly in terms of those of the pure Ising model at an effective temperature on any lattice in any dimension. For example, the energy on the NL is equal to the energy of the pure Ising model at the effective temperature up to a constant and a trivial factor. More remarkably, the specific heat on the NL equals the energy, not the specific heat, of the pure Ising model at the effective temperature, again up to a constant and a trivial factor. Gauge-noninvariant quantities such as the magnetization and correlation functions are exactly equal to the corresponding quantities of the pure Ising model at the effective temperature. These exact relations imply that the leading critical behavior at that multicritical point for the disorder-correlated model is pure-Ising-like, in contrast to the conventional multicritical universality class of the standard Edwards-Anderson model. Our results motivate further investigations of the relatively unexplored topic of correlations in disorder in spin glasses and related problems.

</details>


### [102] [Dynamics of neural scaling laws in random feature regression with powerlaw-distributed kernel eigenvalues](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.23039)
*Jakob Kramp,Javed Lindner,Moritz Helias*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文通过发展动态平均场理论（dynamical mean-field theory），统一了神经网络高斯过程回归（Neural Network Gaussian process regression）中多种学习机制，揭示了高维网络动力学的低维序参数描述，并解释了幂律谱数据上的神经缩放定律（neural scaling laws）和早停（early stopping）效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型神经网络训练中出现的神经缩放定律（neural scaling laws）揭示了高维学习的普适行为，但需要建立对神经网络高斯过程回归（Neural Network Gaussian process regression）动力学中泛化误差典型行为的原理性理解。

Method: 发展了动态平均场理论（dynamical mean-field theory），统一了高斯过程上的贝叶斯推断（Bayesian inference）、带或不带权重衰减（weight-decay）的梯度流（gradient flow）以及随机朗之万训练动力学（stochastic Langevin training dynamics）等多种学习机制。

Result: 该框架将高维微观网络动力学简化为低维序参数（order parameters）描述，显示集体训练动力学可分解为N个独立本征模（eigenmodes）的动力学，其演化方程仅通过集体响应函数（collective response functions）和有效独立噪声的统计特性耦合。

Conclusion: 通过连接幂律谱（power law spectra）数据上学习的光谱和动态特性，该方法能够定量解释泛化误差的动力学，包括神经缩放定律（neural scaling laws）和早停（early stopping）效应等现象。

Abstract: Training large neural networks exposes neural scaling laws for the generalization error, which points to a universal behavior across network architectures of learning in high dimensions. It was also shown that this effect persists in the limit of highly overparametrized networks as well as the Neural network Gaussian process limit. We here develop a principled understanding of the typical behavior of generalization in Neural Network Gaussian process regression dynamics. We derive a dynamical mean-field theory that captures the typical case learning dynamics: This allows us to unify multiple existing regimes of learning studied in the current literature, namely Bayesian inference on Gaussian processes, gradient flow with or without weight-decay, and stochastic Langevin training dynamics. Employing tools from statistical physics, the unified framework we derive in either of these cases yields an effective description of the high-dimensional microscopic behavior of networks dynamics in terms of lower dimensional order parameters. We show that collective training dynamics may be separated into the dynamics of N independent eigenmodes, those evolution equations are only coupled through collective response functions and a common statistics of an effective, independent noise. Our approach allows us to quantitatively explain the dynamics of the generalization error by linking spectral and dynamical properties of learning on data with power law spectra, including phenomena such as neural scaling laws and the effect of early stopping.

### [105] [First measurement of the strong interaction scattering parameters for the $\mathbf{K^-d}$ and $\mathbf{K^+d}$ systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.22833)
*ALICE Collaboration*

Main category: nucl-ex

TL;DR: 该研究首次测量了K⁻d和K⁺d粒子对在铅-铅碰撞中的飞米尺度关联函数，提取了强相互作用散射长度，为低能区手征QCD动力学提供了首个实验基准。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 带电K介子-氘核相互作用为低能QCD的奇异数（strangeness）领域提供了灵敏探针，但K⁻d系统的实验约束一直缺失，尽管已有理论预测。本研究旨在填补这一空白。

Method: 利用ALICE探测器在LHC上记录的√s_NN=5.02 TeV铅-铅碰撞数据，首次测量了K⁻d⊕K⁺d̅和K⁺d⊕K⁻d̅粒子对的飞米尺度关联函数（femtoscopic correlation functions）。在三个中心度类别中分析关联函数，并采用Lednický-Lyuboshitz模型拟合以提取源尺寸和强相互作用散射长度。

Result: K⁻d散射长度的实部为ℜf₀ = -1.44±0.15(stat.)^{+0.10}_{-0.10}(syst.) fm，虚部为ℑf₀ = 1.34±0.33(stat.)^{+0.21}_{-0.15}(syst.) fm。K⁺d散射长度的实部为ℜf₀ = -0.68±0.16(stat.)^{+0.09}_{-0.09}(syst.) fm。这些结果为K⁺d相互作用建模提供了首个实验约束。

Conclusion: 该研究首次对K⁺d相互作用在低能区的建模提供了实验约束，为测试手征QCD动力学（chiral QCD dynamics）提供了期待已久的实验基准，填补了该领域长期存在的实验空白。

Abstract: Charged kaon--deuteron interactions offer a sensitive probe of the strangeness sector of QCD at low energy, particularly through their scattering parameters. Despite available theoretical predictions, experimental constraints remain absent, particularly for the $\rm K^{-}d$ system. The first measurement of femtoscopic correlation functions for $\rm K^{-}d \oplus K^{+}\overline{d}$ and $\rm K^{+}d \oplus K^{-}\overline{d}$ particle pairs in Pb--Pb collisions at $\sqrt{s_{\rm NN}}=5.02$ TeV recorded by ALICE at the LHC is presented. Correlation functions for both systems are analyzed in three centrality classes and fitted using the Lednický--Lyuboshitz model to extract the source size and strong interaction scattering lengths. The $\rm K^{-}d$ scattering length is found to be $\Re f_0 = -1.44 \pm 0.15\text{ (stat.)}^{+0.10}_{-0.10}$ (syst.) fm and $\Im f_0 = 1.34 \pm 0.33$ (stat.)$^{+0.21}_{-0.15}$ (syst.) fm, while for $\rm K^{+}d$ the value $\Re f_0 = -0.68 \pm 0.16$ (stat.)$^{+0.09}_{-0.09}$ (syst.) fm is obtained. These results provide the first constraints on the $\rm K^{\pm} d$ interaction modeling at low energy, delivering a long-awaited experimental benchmark for testing chiral QCD dynamics.

### [106] [Adaptive Patching for Tensor Train Computations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.22372)
*Gianluca Grosso,Marc K. Ritter,Stefan Rohshap,Samuel Badr,Anna Kauch,Markus Wallerberger,Jan von Delft,Hiroshi Shinaoka*

Main category: physics.comp-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种自适应分块方案（adaptive patching scheme），利用块稀疏的量子张量链（Quantics Tensor Train, QTT）结构，通过分治法降低大键维数（bond dimensions）下的计算成本，为大规模QTT计算提供了实用途径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子张量链（QTT）操作如矩阵乘积算符收缩（matrix product operator contractions）在大键维数（bond dimensions）下计算成本过高，限制了其在大规模计算中的应用。

Method: 提出自适应分块方案（adaptive patching scheme），利用块稀疏QTT结构，通过分治法（divide-and-conquer）自适应地将张量划分为具有减小键维数的小块（patches）。

Result: 对于尖锐局域化函数（sharply localized functions）展示了显著改进，并实现了气泡图（bubble diagrams）和Bethe-Salpeter方程的高效计算。

Conclusion: 该方法为先前无法实现的大规模基于QTT的计算打开了实用之门，解决了大键维数下的计算瓶颈问题。

Abstract: Quantics Tensor Train (QTT) operations such as matrix product operator contractions are prohibitively expensive for large bond dimensions. We propose an adaptive patching scheme that exploits block-sparse QTT structures to reduce costs through divide-and-conquer, adaptively partitioning tensors into smaller patches with reduced bond dimensions. We demonstrate substantial improvements for sharply localized functions and show efficient computation of bubble diagrams and Bethe-Salpeter equations, opening the door to practical large-scale QTT-based computations previously beyond reach.

### [107] [Detector-level assessment of alternative target nuclei for CEvNS experiments under realistic experimental conditions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.22234)
*Yusuf Havvat*

Main category: physics.ins-det

TL;DR: 本文通过探测器级模拟评估了相干弹性中微子-核散射（CEvNS）在真实实验条件下的可观测性，重点分析了探测器响应效应如何影响可测量的反冲能谱。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: CEvNS为低动量转移下的中微子相互作用提供了灵敏探针，但其实验观测受到探测器相关效应（如能量阈值、分辨率、噪声和事件选择标准）的严重制约。需要在实际实验条件下评估CEvNS核反冲可观测性。

Method: 采用基于Geant4的详细模拟，对一系列从轻到中等质量范围的替代靶核建模CEvNS相互作用。通过简化的探测器响应链传播真实核反冲能量分布，该链包含能量展宽、噪声诱导涨落、阈值截断和基于否决的事件选择。

Result: 探测器响应效应显著改变了可观测的CEvNS信号，特别是在大多数反冲事件集中的近阈值区域。效率开启行为和重建能量分布的差异突显了相同探测器条件下CEvNS可观测性的靶核依赖性。

Conclusion: 本研究强调探测器效应对信号可及性和靶核性能的相对影响，而非绝对事件率预测。所提出的框架为在探测器级评估和比较潜在CEvNS靶材料提供了一致方法，为未来低阈值CEvNS实验和探测器设计优化提供实用指导。

Abstract: Coherent Elastic Neutrino-Nucleus Scattering (CEvNS) provides a sensitive probe of neutrino interactions at low momentum transfer, but its experimental observation is strongly constrained by detector-related effects such as energy threshold, resolution, noise, and event-selection criteria. In this work, we perform a detector-level assessment of CEvNS nuclear recoil observability under realistic experimental conditions, with particular emphasis on the role of detector response in shaping measurable recoil spectra. Using detailed Geant4-based simulations, CEvNS interactions are modeled for a set of alternative target nuclei spanning light to intermediate mass ranges. The true nuclear recoil energy distributions are propagated through a simplified yet realistic detector-response chain incorporating energy smearing, noise-induced fluctuations, threshold cuts, and veto-based event selection. We present a systematic analysis of recoil energy spectra before and after detector effects, response matrices linking true and reconstructed energies, and energy-dependent selection efficiencies. The results demonstrate that detector response effects significantly modify the observable CEvNS signal, particularly in the near-threshold region where most recoil events are concentrated. Differences in efficiency turn-on behavior and reconstructed energy distributions highlight the target-nucleus dependence of CEvNS observability under identical detector conditions. Rather than focusing on absolute event-rate predictions, this study emphasizes the relative impact of detector effects on signal accessibility and target performance. The presented framework provides a consistent methodology for evaluating and comparing prospective CEvNS target materials at the detector level, offering practical guidance for future low-threshold CEvNS experiments and detector design optimization.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统TCAD仿真面临挑战，特别是当传感器专有工艺细节（如掺杂分布或注入几何结构）不可获取时，需要开发更高效的仿真方法。该方法旨在为高计数率粒子追踪和高粒度量热学应用中的数字传感器设计优化提供支持。

Method: 采用数据驱动的电荷收集与传播参数化建模方法，基于在CERN SPS使用MALTA光束望远镜获取的MALTA2传感器数据。该传感器采用180 nm CMOS成像技术制造，基于30 μm外延硅衬底。

Result: 模型能够高精度复现测量的像素内效率，实现了既真实又计算轻量的模拟像素仿真。该方法为传感器设计优化提供了有效的仿真工具。

Conclusion: 该快速仿真方法将用于优化数字传感器设计，特别适用于高计数率粒子追踪和高粒度量热学应用领域，为传感器性能评估和设计改进提供了高效的计算框架。

Abstract: A fast simulation method is presented for a depleted monolithic active pixel sensor, which uses a data driven parameterization of the charge collection and propagation. This approach provides an efficient alternative to TCAD simulations, particularly for sensors whose proprietary process details - such as doping profiles or implant geometries - are unavailable. Data was obtained with a MALTA2 sensor fabricated in a 180 nm CMOS imaging technology on 30 μm epitaxial silicon using the MALTA beam telescope at CERN SPS. The model reproduces the measured inpixel efficiency with high accuracy and enables a realistic yet computationally lightweight analog pixel simulation. This method will be further employed in optimizing the digital sensor design for applications in high-rate particle tracking and high-granularity calorimetry.

</details>

### [110] [Discrete turn strategies emerge in information-limited navigation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.23324)
*Jose M. Betancourt,Matthew P. Leighton,Thierry Emonet,Benjamin B. Machta,Michael C. Abbott*

Main category: physics.bio-ph

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了生物体在感知梯度导航中最优行为策略的选择问题，发现无方向信息时突然转向优于渐进转向，并观察到不同策略随信息量变化的最优转换。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在理解生物体在感知梯度导航中选择不同行为策略（如翻滚、反向或转向）的驱动因素，将其框架化为在单位时间内使用给定感知信息量的前提下最大化上梯度速度的问题。

Method: 研究通过理论分析框架，比较不同行为策略在最大化上梯度速度方面的性能，特别关注策略在有限感知信息条件下的优化选择。

Result: 研究发现：无方向信息时，突然转向策略优于渐进转向；随着信息量增加，最优策略从方向反转变为完全重新定向的翻滚；在复杂重新定向策略中，离散转向角度最优，且最优策略采用的离散角度数量存在转换点。

Conclusion: 研究揭示了感知梯度导航中行为策略选择的优化原则，表明策略性能取决于可用信息量，离散转向角度在复杂重新定向策略中具有优势，这为理解生物导航策略的演化提供了理论依据。

Abstract: Navigation up a sensory gradient is one of the simplest behaviours, and the simplest strategy is run and tumble. But some organisms use other strategies, such as reversing direction or turning by some angle. Here we ask what drives the choice of strategy, which we frame as maximising up-gradient speed using a given amount of sensory information per unit time. We find that, without directional information on which way to turn, behavioural strategies which make sudden turns perform better than gradual steering. We see various transitions where a different strategy becomes optimal, such as a switch from reversing direction to fully re-orienting tumbles as more information becomes available. And, among more complex re-orientation strategies, we show that discrete turn angles are best, and see transitions in how many such angles the optimal strategy employs.

</details>

### [111] [IDS for subordinate Brownian motions in Poisson random environment on nested fractals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.22348)
*Hubert Balsam,Kamil Kaleta,Mariusz Olszewski,Katarzyna Pietruska-Pałuba*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 该研究建立了具有良好标记性质的无界嵌套分形上随机薛定谔算子的积分态密度（IDS）的Lifshitz奇异性，通过将泊松随机势简化为合金型势分析，扩展了相对论模型在分形上的处理能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于建立分形上随机薛定谔算子的积分态密度（integrated density of states, IDS）的Lifshitz奇异性，特别是针对先前方法无法处理的相对论模型（relativistic models）。

Method: 方法核心是将泊松随机势（Poissonian random potential）$V^ω$有效简化为合金型势（alloy-type potential），其中位点不再是经典$\mathbb{Z}^d$情况下的格点，而是分形复合体（fractal complexes）。这使研究者能够应用在泊松随机场（Poissonian random fields）背景下新颖的方法。

Result: 主要结果是在具有良好标记性质（Good Labeling Property）的平面无界嵌套分形（planar unbounded nested fractals）上，对广泛类别的Bernstein函数$φ$建立了积分态密度（IDS）的Lifshitz奇异性（Lifshitz singularity）。特别地，该方法覆盖了相对论模型（relativistic models）的情况$φ(λ)=(λ+m^{d_w/\vartheta})^{\vartheta/d_w}-m$。

Conclusion: 该研究的主要贡献在于开发了一种新方法，能够处理分形上先前无法触及的相对论模型，通过将泊松随机势简化为合金型势分析，扩展了随机薛定谔算子积分态密度奇异性研究的适用范围。

Abstract: We establish the Lifshitz singularity of the integrated density of states (IDS) for random Schrödinger operators \[ H^ω = φ(-\mathcal{L}) + V^ω \] on planar unbounded nested fractals with the Good Labeling Property. Here, $\mathcal{L}$ is the Laplacian on the fractal, $φ$ is an operator monotone function with mild regularity, and $V^ω$ is a Poissonian random potential with a sufficiently regular profile. The main novelty of our work lies in showing that the study of $V^ω$ can be effectively reduced to the analysis of certain alloy-type potential, where the sites are no longer lattice points as in the classical $\mathbb{Z}^d$ case, but fractal complexes. This observation enables us to apply an approach, new in the setting of Poissonian random fields, which allows us to treat a broad class of Bernstein functions $φ$. In particular, it covers the case $φ(λ)=(λ+m^{d_w/\vartheta})^{\vartheta/d_w}-m$, $\vartheta \in (0,d_w)$, $m>0$, corresponding to relativistic models, which were previously unattainable on fractals by known methods.

</details>


### [112] [Spin Glass Concepts in Computer Science, Statistics, and Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.23326)
*Andrea Montanari*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 该论文探讨了自旋玻璃理论（spin glass theory）如何为高维统计学、统计学习和优化算法的平均案例分析提供新的视角和方法，特别是在研究随机函数的近最小值结构方面。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 论文旨在展示自旋玻璃理论如何为计算机科学、统计学和机器学习中的传统问题提供新的研究思路。这些领域关注随机函数的近最小值结构，但这些问题在物理学和数学物理中通常未被充分探讨。

Method: 论文采用理论综述的方法，解释自旋玻璃理论中的思想如何启发和推动相关领域的最新发展。通过分析随机函数在高维空间中的子水平集和最小值结构，建立跨学科的理论联系。

Result: 论文指出自旋玻璃理论的思想已经为高维统计学、统计学习和优化算法的平均案例分析等领域播下了发展的种子。这些跨学科联系为解决传统问题提供了新的理论框架。

Conclusion: 自旋玻璃理论为研究高维随机函数的近最小值结构提供了重要工具，其思想正在计算机科学、统计学和机器学习领域产生深远影响，促进了这些学科的交叉发展。

Abstract: Spin glass theory studies the structure of sublevel sets and minima (or near-minima) of certain classes of random functions in high dimension. Near-minima of random functions also play an important role in high-dimensional statistics and statistical learning, where minimizing the empirical risk (which is a random function of the model parameters) is the method of choice for learning a statistical model from noisy data. Finally, near-minima of random functions are obviously central to average-case analysis of optimization algorithms. Computer science, statistics, and machine learning naturally lead to questions that are traditionally not addressed within physics and mathematical physics. I will try to explain how ideas from spin glass theory have seeded recent developments in these fields.
  (This article was written on the occasion of the 2024 Abel Prize to Michel Talagrand.)

</details>

### [113] [Cloaking Cosmic Light](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.20248)
*Nemanja Kaloper*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 该论文研究了光穿过暗畴壁（dark domain walls）时转化为暗光子（dark photons）的现象，这一效应完全局域于畴壁上，无需额外机制。转化率是光子频率的锐函数，在紫外截断（ultraviolet cutoff）以上消失，并可能产生偏振旋转、影响宇宙微波背景（cosmic microwave background）功率谱及违反Etherington互易关系（reciprocity relation）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究光与暗畴壁相互作用的基本物理效应，特别是光转化为暗光子的机制及其对宇宙学观测的影响。这些效应可能影响哈勃常数（Hubble rate）的宇宙学测定。

Method: 通过理论分析光穿过暗畴壁的物理过程，该畴壁源化一个顶形式（top form）并与可见和暗U(1)规范场的Chern-Simons项耦合。研究完全局域于畴壁上的转化机制，无需额外成分。

Result: 发现光转化为暗光子的转化率是光子频率在畴壁静止参考系中的锐函数，在顶形式扇区的紫外截断以上消失。部分遮蔽（cloaking）可能产生约10^{-3}弧度的偏振旋转，修改宇宙微波背景功率谱，并在低频违反Etherington互易关系。

Conclusion: 这些效应为暗物质（dark matter）与可见光相互作用提供了新的理论机制，可能影响宇宙学参数（如哈勃常数）的测定，为实验观测提供了可检验的预测。

Abstract: Light crossing dark domain walls that source a top form coupled to gauge Chern--Simons terms mixing visible and dark $U(1)$ gauge fields generically converts into dark photons. The effect is entirely localized on the wall and requires no additional ingredients. The conversion rate is a sharp function of the photon frequency in the wall rest frame, vanishing above the ultraviolet cutoff of the top form sector. Partial cloaking may also induce a rotation of the polarization of transmitted light of order $Δ\vartheta \sim 10^{-3}$ radians, modify the cosmic microwave background power spectrum, and violate Etherington's reciprocity relation at low frequencies. These effects can impact cosmological determinations of the Hubble rate.

</details>


### [114] [Shadows of Giants: Constraints on Stupendously Large Black Holes from Negative Sources against the Cosmic Microwave Background](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.22587)
*Brian C. Lacki*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 该研究提出利用宇宙微波背景（CMB）探测超大质量黑洞（SLABs）的新方法，通过其巨大阴影在微波数据中表现为负源的特征，对SLABs的丰度设定了强有力的限制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超大质量天体黑洞（SLABs）作为质量超过万亿太阳质量的假设性黑洞，其存在可能产生的可观测后果最近才被认真考虑，目前对其丰度的约束相对较少。本研究旨在建立对SLABs的简单而强大的约束方法。

Method: 该方法基于SLABs在宇宙微波背景（cosmic microwave background, CMB）上产生的巨大阴影效应，这些阴影在微波数据中表现为负源（negative sources）。研究分析了固定质量SLABs的阴影随红移变化的可探测性。

Result: 研究发现，SLABs的阴影在红移超过1.6后更容易被探测。该方法排除了最后散射面内质量≳10¹⁷ M☉的SLABs存在，并得出在10¹⁵-10¹⁸ M☉质量范围内Ω_BH ≲ 10⁻⁵的丰度限制。

Conclusion: 该研究通过CMB阴影效应为SLABs丰度设定了强有力的观测限制，并讨论了吸积效应（包括SLAB增长、正吸积光度以及遮蔽物质）对这些限制的影响。

Abstract: Stupendously large astrophysical black holes (SLABs) are hypothetical black holes with masses of more than a trillion Suns. Because observable consequences of their existence have only recently been seriously considered, there have been relatively few constraints on their abundance. This work motivates a simple yet powerful constraint on SLABs: their huge shadows are visible against the cosmic microwave background. SLABs could thus appear as negative sources in microwave data. In fact, the shadow of a SLAB with a fixed mass becomes easier to detect with increasing redshifts past $1.6$. The limits are powerful enough to rule out SLABs of mass $\gtrsim 10^{17}\ M_{\odot}$ within the last scattering surface, and imply $Ω_{BH} \lesssim 10^{-5}$ for masses $10^{15}$--$10^{18}\ M_{\odot}$. I also discuss the effects of accretion and their implications for the limits: SLAB growth, positive accretion luminosity, and obscuring material.

</details>


### [115] [Redshift evolution of the Hubble constant: Constraints and new insights from an interacting dark energy model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.22840)
*Xinyi Dai,Yupeng Yang,Yicheng Wang,Yankun Qu,Shuangxi Yi,Fayin Wang*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种修正的相互作用暗能量（IDE）模型，用于研究哈勃常数（H₀）随红移的演化，以应对哈勃张力问题。该模型通过暗能量与暗物质之间的能量交换机制，使H₀呈现红移依赖性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机源于哈勃张力（Hubble tension）问题，即早期宇宙与晚期宇宙测量得到的哈勃常数存在显著差异。本文旨在通过构建相互作用暗能量（interacting dark energy, IDE）框架，为H₀的红移演化提供理论解释。

Method: 方法包括：1）开发修正的相互作用暗能量（IDE）模型，其中暗能量与暗物质之间的能量交换导致H₀的红移依赖性；2）使用综合观测数据评估模型，包括DESI DR2和SDSS的重子声学振荡（BAO）、宇宙计时器、Pantheon样本的Ia型超新星以及Planck CMB距离先验。

Result: 晚期宇宙数据分析得到参数α=0.0107^{+0.0032}_{-0.011}，最佳拟合值约为10^{-2}，显示H₀随红移增加而减小的趋势，支持超越ΛCDM模型的幂律演化。加入CMB数据后约束进一步收紧至10^{-5}量级，这归因于高红移时暗区相互作用的抑制，这是强重子-光子耦合的结果。

Conclusion: 结论表明，相互作用暗能量（IDE）框架为描述H₀的红移演化提供了理论一致且观测可行的机制，为缓解哈勃张力问题提供了有前景的途径。

Abstract: We develop a modified interacting dark energy (IDE) model to study the redshift evolution of the Hubble constant ($H_0$), in light of the Hubble tension. In this framework, the energy exchange between dark energy and dark matter induces a redshift dependence of $H_0$. We evaluate the model against a comprehensive suite of observations, including baryon acoustic oscillations (BAO) from DESI DR2 and SDSS, cosmic chronometers, type Ia supernovae from the Pantheon sample, and Planck CMB distance priors. Analysis of late-Universe data yields $α= 0.0107^{+0.0032}_{-0.011}$, with the best-fit value on the order of $10^{-2}$, revealing a decreasing trend of $H_0$ with redshift. This supports a power-law evolution beyond $Λ$CDM. Incorporating CMB data further tightens the constraint to the order of $10^{-5}$, which we attribute to the suppression of dark-sector interactions at high redshifts, a consequence of the strong baryon--photon coupling. These results indicate that the IDE framework provides a theoretically consistent and observationally viable mechanism for describing the redshift evolution of $H_0$, offering a promising avenue toward alleviating the Hubble tension.

</details>


### [116] [(1+1)-Dimensional Schrödinger-Poisson equation with contact interaction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.22795)
*Óscar Rodríguez-Villalba,Ivan Saychenko,Massimo Pietroni,Sandro Wimberger*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文研究接触相互作用（contact interactions）在一维模糊暗物质（fuzzy dark matter）动力学中的作用，通过数值模拟分析吸引和排斥相互作用对静态解、弛豫过程和引力坍缩的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 虽然ΛCDM（Lambda cold dark matter）范式在大尺度结构形成方面解释成功，但其小尺度预测与观测存在张力。模糊暗物质（FDM）提供了替代框架，其中局域自相互作用（local self-interactions）可能进一步影响结构的形成和演化。

Method: 研究基于薛定谔-泊松方程（Schrödinger-Poisson equation）在一维空间中对模糊暗物质建模，通过数值模拟（numerical simulations）探索静态和膨胀背景下的吸引与排斥接触相互作用。分析聚焦于三个关键场景：最低能量定态解（lowest-energy stationary solution）性质、局域初态的弛豫（relaxation）以及非局域态的引力坍缩（gravitational collapse）。

Result: 接触相互作用改变了定态解的密度轮廓（density profile），并影响了引力坍缩特征阶段（特别是壳层交叉事件（shell-crossing event））的发生。在一维模型中，即使包含局域自相互作用，弛豫过程也不会收敛到最低能量定态解。

Conclusion: 局域自相互作用在塑造模糊暗物质的非线性动力学中扮演重要角色，这为在更高维度和更符合宇宙学现实的设置中进行进一步研究提供了动机。

Abstract: We investigate the role of contact interactions in the dynamics of fuzzy dark matter (FDM) modeled through the Schrödinger-Poisson equation in one spatial dimension. While the $Λ$CDM paradigm successfully explains structure formation on large scales, its small-scale predictions remain in tension with observations. FDM offers an alternative framework, where local self-interactions can further influence the formation and evolution of structures. We explore both attractive and repulsive contact interactions in static and expanding backgrounds. Using numerical simulations, we examine their impact on three key scenarios: the properties of the lowest-energy stationary solution, the relaxation of localized initial states, and the gravitational collapse of nonlocalized states. Our results show that contact interactions modify the density profile of the stationary solution and affect the onset of characteristic stages of gravitational collapse, particularly the shell-crossing event. In the (1+1) model, we confirm that relaxation does not converge to the lowest-energy stationary solution, even when local self-interactions are included. Taken together, local self-interactions play a relevant role in shaping the nonlinear dynamics of FDM and motivate further studies in higher-dimensional and cosmologically realistic settings.

</details>

### [117] [The shape of transverse momentum spectra in hybrid hydrodynamic models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.22490)
*Thiago S. Domingues,Fernando G. Gardim,Cicero D. Muncinelli,Andre V. Giannini,Gabriel S. Denicol,Tiago Nunes da Silva,David D. Chinellato,Giorgio Torrieri,Mauricio Hippert,Jun Takahashi,Matthew Luzum*

Main category: nucl-th

TL;DR: 该研究通过分析四种不同粒子化模型下17个参数对横向动量标度谱的影响，发现谱形对体粘滞系数、自由流时间和核子宽度参数w最为敏感，但模型整体对谱形观测量的描述灵活性有限，且存在参数间的显著张力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探究从已观测到的普遍性谱形中能获取何种物理信息，该谱形在实验数据和流体动力学模拟中均表现出跨中心度和碰撞系统的惊人普适性。研究旨在评估谱形对不同模型参数的敏感性。

Method: 方法包括在广泛的参数空间内研究标度化横向动量谱，分析四种不同粒子化（particlization）模型中17个参数的敏感性。研究关注从流体描述切换到动力学理论后处理（afterburner）时的参数影响。

Result: 研究发现谱形对体粘滞系数（bulk viscosity）、自由流时间（free-streaming time）和T$_\mathrm{R}$ENTo核子宽度参数w最为敏感。尽管参数众多，模型对谱形观测量的描述灵活性却出人意料地有限，且在同时描述动量积分观测量时存在显著张力。

Conclusion: 结论指出在常用的T$_\mathrm{R}$ENTo+自由流+流体动力学+后处理模拟模型中存在模型张力，并推测其起源及可能缺失的物理机制。研究发现大核子宽度参数w有利于平均横向动量，而小w值则与实验测量的标度谱一致，揭示了参数间的内在矛盾。

Abstract: We study the scaled transverse momentum spectra over a wide parameter space of state-of-the-art hydrodynamic simulation models in order to learn what information can be obtained from the shape of identified-particle spectra -- previously observed to be surprisingly universal across centrality and collision systems in both experimental data and hydrodynamic simulations. We study its sensitivity to each of 17 model parameters in the context of 4 different models for particlization when switching from the hydro description to the kinetic theory afterburner. We find that the strongest sensitivity is to parameters relating to bulk viscosity, free-streaming time, and the $\texttt{T$_\mathrm{R}$ENTo}$ nucleon width parameter $w$. However, we find that the model generally has surprisingly little flexibility in describing the scaled spectrum observable, despite the large number of parameters.
  Within this small range of parameter dependence, we further find significant tension in a simultaneous description of momentum-integrated observables. In particular, while the mean transverse momentum prefers a large value of the nucleon width parameter $w$, a small value is required to obtain scaled spectra that are consistent with experimental measurements. We speculate on the origin of these model tensions and possible missing physics in the commonly-used $\texttt{T$_\mathrm{R}$ENTo}$+free streaming+hydro+afterburner simulation model.

</details>

# hep-ph [[Back]](#toc)

### [118] [NASDUCK': Laboratory Limits on Ultralight Dark-Photon Dark Matter with Null-Axis Magnetometry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.22308)
*Joel Barir,Itay M. Bloch,Yair Goldszeft,Gal Goldstein,Constantine Feinberg,Or Katz,Tomer Volansky*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该研究使用三轴磁力计在大型导电屏蔽室内搜索暗光子暗物质，在4×10⁻¹²-2×10⁻⁹ eV质量范围内设定了新的实验室限制，将动力学混合参数ε的约束提高了三个数量级。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 暗光子（dark photon）是一种有良好理论动机的超轻暗物质候选者，可能通过动力学混合（kinetic mixing）与标准模型耦合。研究旨在搜索特定质量范围内的暗光子暗物质，改进现有实验室约束。

Method: 采用三轴磁力计（three-axis magnetometer）置于大型导电屏蔽室内进行探测。利用几何定义的零响应轴作为噪声参考，通过减法程序降低噪声基底并提高灵敏度。

Result: 在质量范围mA'c² = 4×10⁻¹²-2×10⁻⁹ eV（1-500 kHz）内设定了新的实验室限制，将动力学混合参数ε的约束相比先前实验室界限提高了最多三个数量级。

Conclusion: 这些结果建立了该质量范围内最强的实验室约束，并展示了零轴磁力测量（null-axis magnetometry）如何扩展对超轻矢量暗物质的地面搜索能力。

Abstract: The dark photon is a well-motivated ultralight dark-matter candidate that may couple to the Standard Model through kinetic mixing. We search for dark-photon dark matter in the mass range $m_{A'}c^2 = 4\times10^{-12}$-$2\times10^{-9}\,\mathrm{eV}$ (1-500 kHz) using a three-axis magnetometer inside a large conductive shielded room. We set new laboratory limits on the kinetic-mixing parameter $ε$, improving upon previous laboratory bounds by up to three orders of magnitude. Our search exploits a geometry-defined null response along one axis as a noise reference; a subtraction procedure reduces the noise floor and improves sensitivity. These results establish the strongest laboratory constraints in this mass range and illustrate how null-axis magnetometry can broaden terrestrial searches for ultralight vector dark matter.

</details>


### [119] [One Sum To Rule Them All: A Second Order Master Rate Sum Rule for Charm Decays](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.22320)
*Margarita Gavrilova,Yuval Grossman,Guglielmo Papiri,Stefan Schacht*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该论文证明了在标准模型（Standard Model）框架下，任何通过U-自旋（U-spin）相关的强子弱粲衰变系统都满足一个速率求和规则：CF和DCS衰变的CKM无因子速率之和除以SCS衰变的CKM无因子速率之和等于1，该规则在U-自旋破缺的二级近似下成立。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究强子弱粲衰变中U-自旋对称性及其破缺效应，旨在建立精确的理论框架来检验标准模型并预测未测量的衰变速率。

Method: 在标准模型框架内，利用U-自旋对称性分析强子弱粲衰变系统，推导出CKM无因子（CKM-free）衰变速率的求和规则，该规则考虑了U-自旋破缺至二级近似。

Result: 理论推导表明该求和规则在所有情况下都成立，且与现有实验数据良好吻合；对于部分未测量的衰变速率，该规则可用于预测缺失数据。

Conclusion: 该求和规则为检验标准模型和预测未测量的强子弱粲衰变速率提供了有力工具，证明了U-自旋对称性在描述这些衰变过程中的有效性。

Abstract: We show that within the Standard Model any system of hadronic weak charm decays related by $U$-spin satisfies the following rate sum rule: (sum of CF and DCS CKM-free rates) divided by (sum of SCS CKM-free rates) = 1, which holds up to second order in $U$-spin breaking. We test this sum rule against available data and find that it is well satisfied in all cases. For systems in which some decay rates have not yet been measured, we use this sum rule to predict the missing rates.

</details>


### [120] [Robust Calibration of Non-Perturbative Models with History Matching](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.22324)
*Andrew Iskauskas,Max Knobbe,Frank Krauss,Steffen Schumann*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 首次将贝叶斯线性仿真（Bayes Linear Emulation）和历史匹配（History Matching）应用于蒙特卡洛事件生成器中非微扰模型的校准，替代传统的"蒙特卡洛调谐"方法，系统量化参数不确定性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统蒙特卡洛调谐（Monte Carlo tuning）方法仅提供最佳拟合和椭球参数不确定性估计，无法正确处理参数空间中可能存在的多个不相交区域产生相似结果的情况，需要更系统稳健的参数不确定性量化方法。

Method: 采用贝叶斯线性仿真和历史匹配方法，该方法不寻求单一最佳拟合，而是识别所有与数据一致（consistent with data）的参数空间区域，特别适用于处理参数空间中不同（可能不相交）区域产生相似结果的挑战性情况。

Result: 该方法能够系统稳健地量化模型中的参数不确定性，在Sherpa中的强子化模型（hadronisation models）上展示了其有效性，包括内置的团簇碎裂模型Ahadic和通过接口连接的Pythia弦碎裂模型。

Conclusion: 历史匹配方法为蒙特卡洛事件生成器中非微扰模型的校准提供了优于传统调谐方法的新途径，特别是在处理参数空间多解问题时表现出更强的系统性和稳健性。

Abstract: We apply, for the first time, Bayes Linear Emulation and History Matching to the calibration of non-perturbative models in Monte Carlo event generators. In contrast to the usual approach of "Monte Carlo tuning", History Matching does not result in best-fit plus ellipsoidal parameter uncertainty estimates but instead identifies all parameter space regions that are consistent with data. This approach leads to a systematic and robust quantification of parametric uncertainties in the models, especially in those challenging cases where different, possibly disjoint, regions of parameter space deliver similar results, which are usually not properly treated with current methodology. We highlight the power of this method with the hadronisation models available through Sherpa: the built-in cluster fragmentation Ahadic and string fragmentation through an interface to Pythia.

</details>


### [121] [Flavorful Lepton Number Violation at the EIC](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.22355)
*Sebastián Urrutia Quiroga,Vincenzo Cirigliano,Wouter Dekens,Kaori Fuyuto,Emanuele Mereghetti*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本研究探讨在电子-离子对撞机（EIC）上通过重中性轻子（HNLs）的共振产生来探测味道相关的轻子数破坏过程，分析信号与背景的分布特征，并评估EIC在特定质量范围内的探测灵敏度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索电子-离子对撞机（Electron-Ion Collider, EIC）探测味道相关的轻子数破坏（flavorful lepton number violation）的潜力，特别是在νSMEFT框架下，通过重中性轻子（heavy neutral leptons, HNLs）的共振产生来寻找超出标准模型的新物理信号。

Method: 研究方法基于νSMEFT框架（Standard Model Effective Field Theory augmented with n singlet HNLs），重点关注质量在10-100 GeV范围内的HNLs，通过其与轻中微子的混合机制产生。研究分析了信号与背景的动理学分布，包括强子化和探测器效应，并提出一组切割条件以最小化背景。

Result: 研究结果表明，在考虑的质量范围内，具备μ子探测能力且积分亮度为100 fb⁻¹的EIC可以达到与最强直接（LHC）和间接约束相当的灵敏度。在νSMEFT框架中，特别是超出四维算子的情况下，EIC的探测尤其相关。

Conclusion: 本研究为评估EIC的μ子探测能力和τ子强子重建提供了进一步研究的动机，同时建议在有效理论中开展涉及更高维算子介导的产生机制的更一般性理论分析。

Abstract: We explore the prospects of detecting flavorful lepton number violation at the Electron-Ion Collider (EIC) through resonant production of heavy neutral leptons (HNLs), resulting in $e^- p \to \ell^+_α+ k\, j+X$, where $α\in \{e, μ, τ\}$ and $k$ denotes the number of jets. We work in the $ν$SMEFT framework of the Standard Model Effective Field Theory augmented with $n$ singlet HNLs, one of which is in the mass range $10-100$~GeV, within kinematic reach of the EIC. To explore the EIC sensitivity, we focus on the HNL production mechanism induced by mixing with light neutrinos. We study kinematic distributions for signal and backgrounds, including hadronization and detector effects, and suggest a set of cuts to minimize backgrounds. In the mass range considered, we find that the EIC with muon detection capabilities and an integrated luminosity of $100~\mathrm{fb}^{-1}$ can reach sensitivities comparable to the strongest direct (LHC) and indirect constraints, and is especially relevant in the $ν$SMEFT framework beyond dimension four. Our study motivates further assessment of muon detection capabilities at the EIC and $τ$ hadronic reconstruction, as well as a more general theoretical analysis involving production mechanisms mediated by higher-dimensional operators in the effective theory.

</details>


### [122] [Testing beyond the Standard Model scenarios in next-generation long-baseline neutrino oscillation experiments](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.22849)
*Pragyanprasu Swain*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该论文评估了下一代长基线中微子振荡实验（DUNE、T2HK、T2HKK）对三种超越标准模型（BSM）物理场景的灵敏度，包括长程中微子-物质相互作用、洛伦兹不变性破坏和活性-惰性中微子振荡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 论文旨在评估未来长基线中微子振荡实验对超越标准模型（Beyond the Standard Model, BSM）物理的探测能力。这些实验不仅能够解决中微子质量顺序、CP破坏相角δ_CP和混合角θ_{23}的八分性问题，还能为BSM物理提供强有力的探测手段。

Method: 研究评估了三种BSM场景：1）由超轻矢量玻色子介导的、味道依赖且无反常的规范重子-轻子对称性引起的长程中微子-物质相互作用；2）洛伦兹不变性破坏（Lorentz invariance violation, LIV），推导了CPT守恒和CPT破坏LIV参数对基线长度和能量的解析依赖关系；3）在广泛的Δm^2_{41}范围内的活性-惰性中微子振荡，针对基准Δm^2_{41}值推导了CP相的灵敏度。

Result: 研究发现：DUNE和T2HK能够约束、发现并在有利情况下区分不同的规范对称性；DUNE在探测所有LIV参数方面具有优越性，而T2HK对CPT守恒的LIV参数基本不敏感；对于活性-惰性振荡，研究建立了排除限并强调了近探测器的作用。这些结果表明未来长基线设施是BSM物理的有力探针。

Conclusion: 未来长基线中微子振荡实验不仅是解决中微子质量顺序、CP破坏相角和θ_{23}八分性等标准振荡参数的关键设施，还能为超越标准模型物理提供强大的探测能力，涵盖长程相互作用、洛伦兹不变性破坏和惰性中微子等多个前沿研究领域。

Abstract: In this thesis, we assess the sensitivity of next-generation long-baseline neutrino oscillation experiments, DUNE, T2HK, and T2HKK, to three popular beyond the Standard Model (BSM) scenarios. Within the three BSM studies, we examine: (i) long-range neutrino-matter interactions induced by flavor-dependent, anomaly-free gauged baryon-lepton symmetries mediated by ultra-light vector boson, showing that DUNE and T2HK can constrain, discover, and in some favorable cases distinguish among different symmetries; (ii) Lorentz invariance violation (LIV), where we derive analytical dependencies of CPT-conserving and CPT-violating LIV parameters on baseline and energy, highlighting the superior reach of DUNE in probing all the LIV parameters, in contrast to T2HK, which is essentially blind to the CPT-conserving LIV parameters; and (iii) active-sterile oscillations over a broad range of $Δm^2_{41}$, where we derive sensitivity to CP phases for benchmark choices of $Δm^2_{41}$ and establish exclusion limits, emphasizing the role of near detectors. Together, these studies show that future long-baseline facilities not only resolve the neutrino mass ordering, value of $δ_{\rm CP}$, and $θ_{23}$ octant, but also provide powerful probes of BSM physics.

</details>


### [123] [ACT-Consistent B-L Higgs Inflation in Supergravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.22473)
*C. Pallis*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种基于最小超对称标准模型（MSSM）的可重整化扩展模型，该模型具有R对称性和规范化的B-L对称性，通过四次势驱动的混沌暴胀实现宇宙暴胀，同时解释了MSSM中的μ项并通过非热轻子生成实现重子生成。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究的动机是构建一个可重整化的MSSM扩展模型，该模型能够同时实现混沌暴胀、解释MSSM中的μ项参数，并提供重子生成机制。模型需要与ACT（Atacama Cosmology Telescope）观测数据保持一致。

Method: 方法包括：1）构建具有R对称性和规范化B-L对称性的MSSM扩展模型；2）采用由导致U(1)B-L自发破缺的希格斯超场驱动的四次势混沌暴胀；3）引入包含两个自由参数(p,N)的分数平移对称Kähler势，参数范围分别为1.355<p<6.7和6×10⁻⁵<N<0.7。

Result: 研究结果表明：1）模型与ACT观测数据一致；2）在超势中相关参数较小的条件下，能够解释MSSM中的μ项；3）重子生成通过非热轻子生成实现，暴胀子衰变为最轻和/或次轻的右手中微子，适用于正常排序的轻中微子质量。

Conclusion: 该研究成功构建了一个统一的框架，将暴胀、MSSM参数解释和重子生成机制整合在一个具有R对称性和规范化B-L对称性的可重整化MSSM扩展模型中，同时满足当前宇宙学观测约束。

Abstract: We consider a renormalizable extension of the minimal supersymmetric standard model (MSSM) endowed by an R and a gauged B - L symmetry. The model incorporates chaotic inflation driven by a quartic potential, associated with the Higgs superfields which lead to a spontaneous breaking of U(1)B-L. Consistency with the ACT data is achieved by considering a fractional shift-symmetric Kaehler potential which includes two free parameters (p,N) constrained in the ranges 1.355<p<6.7 and 6x10^-5<N<0.7. An explanation of the mu term of the MSSM is also provided, under the condition that a related parameter in the superpotential is somewhat small. Baryogenesis occurs via non-thermal leptogenesis which is also realized by the inflaton's decay to the lightest and/or next-to-lightest right-handed neutrinos for normal ordered light neutrino masses.

</details>


### [124] [Bottom-charmed meson states in inverse problem of QCD](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.22872)
*Halil Mutuk,Duygu Yıldırım*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文采用逆矩阵QCD求和规则（inverse matrix QCD sum rules）框架，对底粲（B_c）介子谱进行了全面分析，直接重构强子谱密度并计算了不同量子数的B_c介子质量和衰变常数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于改进传统QCD求和规则方法，避免使用唯象连续谱参数化或夸克-强子对偶假设，从而更精确地分析重夸克偶素系统的谱学性质。

Method: 采用逆矩阵QCD求和规则（inverse matrix QCD sum rules）形式体系，将传统QCD求和规则重新表述为逆问题，直接从第一性原理重构强子谱密度（hadronic spectral densities）。

Result: 计算了量子数J^P = 0^-、1^-、0^+和1^+的常规B_c介子质量和衰变常数，结果与现有实验测量值高度一致，且与各种理论和唯象方法的预测相符。

Conclusion: 逆矩阵形式体系相对于标准实现表现出改进的数值稳定性和降低的系统不确定性，突显了其在重夸克偶素系统精密谱学研究中的适用性。

Abstract: We present a comprehensive analysis of the bottom-charmed ($B_c$) meson spectrum within the inverse matrix QCD sum rules formalism. In this framework, conventional QCD sum rules are recast as an inverse problem, allowing for the direct reconstruction of hadronic spectral densities from first principles without invoking phenomenological continuum parametrizations or quark-hadron duality assumptions. We compute the masses and decay constants of conventional $B_c$ mesons with quantum numbers $J^P = 0^-$, $1^-$, $0^+$, and $1^+$. The obtained results are in close agreement with available experimental measurements and are consistent with predictions from various theoretical and phenomenological approaches. The inverse matrix formulation exhibits improved numerical stability and reduced systematic uncertainties relative to standard implementations, highlighting its suitability for precision spectroscopy of heavy quarkonium systems.

</details>


### [125] [NNLO QCD corrections to hadron production in DIS at finite transverse momentum](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.22972)
*Liang Dong,Shen Fang,Jun Gao,Hai Tao Li,Ding Yu Shao,Yu Jiao Zhu*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该研究首次完成了深度非弹性散射中有限横向动量强子产生的完整次次领头阶计算，通过q_T减除框架解决了半包含过程中的红外发散问题，显著改善了微扰展开的稳定性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机是解决半包含过程中有限横向动量强子产生的红外发散长期挑战，为即将到来的电子-离子对撞机时代提供高精度理论基础，并建立探索核子三维结构的新基准。

Method: 采用基于无反冲喷注定义的q_T减除框架，利用赢者通吃重组方案实现强子-喷注关联产生的一致因子化，从而能够包含α_s^3阶修正。

Result: 结果显示微扰展开显著改善稳定，尺度不确定性相比之前的次领头阶预测有所降低，NNLO修正对于精确描述ZEUS合作组的高精度多重数数据至关重要。

Conclusion: 该工作为电子-离子对撞机时代提供了高精度理论基础，建立了探索核子三维结构的新基准，表明NNLO修正是实现强子产生过程精确描述的必要条件。

Abstract: We present the first complete calculation of hadron production in deep-inelastic scattering (DIS) at finite transverse momentum to next-to-next-to-leading order (NNLO) in perturbative QCD. To overcome the long-standing challenge of infrared divergences in semi-inclusive processes with identified final state hadrons at finite transverse momentum, we implement the recently developed $q_T$-subtraction framework based on the recoil-free jet definition. By utilizing the winner-take-all recombination scheme, we achieve a consistent factorization for hadron-jet associated production, enabling the inclusion of $\mathcal{O}(α_s^3)$ corrections. Our results demonstrate a significantly improved stabilization of the perturbative expansion and a reduction in scale uncertainties compared to previous next-to-leading order predictions. We find that the NNLO corrections are essential for a robust description of high precision multiplicity data from the ZEUS collaborations. This work provides a high precision theoretical foundation for the upcoming Electron-Ion Collider era and establishes a new benchmark for the exploration of the nucleon's three-dimensional structure.

</details>


### [126] [Charmed nuclei and exotic charmed meson production at CBM@FAIR and ALICE@LHC](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.22676)
*Thanaporn Chimruang,Christoph Herold,Ayut Limphirat,Yupeng Yan,Jan Steinheimer,Benjamin Dönigus,Tom Reichert,Volodymyr Vovchenko,Marcus Bleicher*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该研究预测了在SIS100和LHC束流能量下Au+Au碰撞中奇异粲强子（exotic charmed hadrons）和粲核（charmed nuclei）的预期产额，使用UrQMD输运模型和Thermal-FIST模型进行计算。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在评估CBM实验探测奇异粲强子和粲核的能力，特别是在高重子密度条件下这些粒子的产额情况，为未来实验提供理论预测。

Method: 采用UrQMD输运模型获取轻强子和粲夸克产生信息，并应用Thermal-FIST模型进行热统计计算，预测SIS100和LHC束流能量下Au+Au碰撞中的粒子产额。

Result: 预测显示CBM实验能以每3秒1个的速率探测χ_{c0}(1P)和χ_{c1}(1P)，每3分钟1个的速率探测X(3872)。尽管CBM总粲夸克产额远低于LHC，但由于其更高的重子密度，粲核在CBM和LHC中的丰度相当。

Conclusion: CBM实验具备探测奇异粲强子和粲核的能力，高重子密度环境使粲核研究成为可能，为探索这些奇异态提供了新的实验机会。

Abstract: We make predictions for the expected multiplicities of exotic charmed hadrons and charmed nuclei in Au+Au collisions at SIS100 and LHC beam energies, using input on light hadron and charm production from the UrQMD transport model, and applying the Thermal-FIST model. We demonstrate that the CBM experiment has the capability to explore these states with production rates of one per 3 seconds for $χ_{c0}(1P)$ and $χ_{c1}(1P)$, and one every 3 minutes for $X(3872)$ at the expected data taking rates. Due to the higher baryon density at CBM compared to the LHC, charmed nuclei, if they exist, will be equally abundant at CBM as at the LHC, even though the total charm production at CBM is much lower.

</details>

### [127] [Tuning the magnetic properties of Kitaev materials via the antiferromagnetic proximity effect: Novel phases and application to an $α$-RuCl$_3$/MnPS$_3$ bilayer](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.22310)
*Pedro M. Cônsoli,Ezra Day-Roberts,Johannes Knolle,Antia S. Botana,Onur Erten*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 结合微扰理论（perturbation theory）、精确对角化（exact diagonalization）和经典能量最小化方法（classical energy-minimization method）进行理论分析，并应用第一性原理模拟（first-principle simulations）评估α-RuCl₃与易轴反铁磁体MnPS₃异质双层结构的具体实现前景。

Conclusion: 通过理论分析和第一性原理模拟，证实了在α-RuCl₃与MnPS₃异质双层结构中实现该物理设置的可行性，为利用范德华异质结构调控Kitaev材料量子相提供了理论依据。

Abstract: In recent years, the increasing level of control over van der Waals (vdW) heterostructures has opened new routes to tune the properties of quantum materials. Motivated by these developments, we examine the potential consequences of interfacing a Kitaev honeycomb magnet, such as $α$-RuCl$_3$, with a nearly lattice-matched vdW antiferromagnet. By combining perturbation theory, exact diagonalization, and a classical energy-minimization method, we show that an effective staggered magnetic field originating from the vdW antiferromagnet can drive a monolayer of a Kitaev material into various novel phases, including an antichiral Kitaev spin liquid, a nonmagnetic nematic phase, and different types of skyrmion crystals. ### [128] [Hidden $Z_{2}\times Z_{2}$ subspace symmetry protection for quantum scars](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.22397)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用谱生成代数（Spectrum Generating Algebra, SGA）理论分析疤痕态；构造Lieb-Schultz-Mattis（LSM）扭算符区分疤痕态与遍历态；通过Loschmidt回波和量子费舍尔信息（Quantum Fisher Information, QFI）分析不同微扰下的稳定性。

Result: 疤痕子空间具有对称性保护平凡（symmetry-protected trivial, SPt）特性，源于隐藏的Z₂×Z₂对称性；LSM扭算符在疤痕态取值为-1，在遍历态趋于零；QFI分析显示疤痕态比邻近热态对微扰更敏感。

Conclusion: 基于QFI和不同LSM扭算符的分析，获得了对保持SGA和破坏SGA的微扰的分类，深化了对量子多体疤痕态稳定性机制的理解。

Abstract: We study the paradigmatic spin-1 XY chain under open boundary conditions, which hosts exact quantum many-body scars generated by an emergent Spectrum Generating Algebra (SGA). We show that the scar subspace possesses a symmetry-protected trivial (SPt) character that we attribute to a hidden $Z_{2}\times Z_{2}$ symmetry of another model, namely the commutant Hamiltonian, for which the scars are the ground states. We construct a Lieb-Schultz-Mattis (LSM) type twist operator, which, for scar states, takes the value $-1,$ and, for ergodic states, approaches zero in the thermodynamic limit. A complementary understanding of the stability of the scars under different perturbations is obtained by analyzing the Loschmidt echo and Quantum Fisher Information (QFI) of the scars. Finite-size scaling analysis of the QFI reveals that the scars are much more sensitive to perturbations as compared to the nearby thermal states. Based on the analysis of QFI and different LSM twist operators, we obtain a classification of different SGA-preserving and SGA-breaking perturbations.

Here we demonstrate that a heavy-fermion state can also compete with charge order, such as the charge density wave (CDW) state typical in the van der Waals $4f$ rare-earth tritellurides (RTe$_3$). We extend the tritelluride tight-binding model to include Kondo coupling and quantify the Fermi surface reconstruction. Consistent with the destruction of nesting, we observe no CDW in $β$-UTe$_3$. Our expansion of the Kondo phase diagram beyond spin-mediated competition opens new possibilities for proximity-induced phase engineering in correlated van der Waals heterostructures.

Abstract: Quantum geometry quantifies how the single-particle Bloch wavefunction changes in phase and amplitude across the Brillouin Zone. In this work, we show that Mott metal-insulator transitions, as well as transitions between different magnetic orders within the Mott insulating phase, can be driven by the quantum geometry of the underlying Bloch band, thereby providing a mechanism complementary to conventional bandwidth-tuned Mott transitions. By studying the Kane-Mele-Hubbard model using exact diagonalization, we demonstrate that in in half-filled and topologically-trivial bands, quantum geometric properties of the Bloch states alone can act as a tuning knob for Mott metal-to-insulator and affect the competition between ferromagnetism and antiferromagnetism. We show that both transitions may be heuristically understood via non-local Coulomb scattering in a basis of exponentially localized Wannier functions. These results highlight the role of quantum geometry beyond topological settings as a governing principle for conventional Mott and magnetic physics in multi-orbital and moiré materials.

### [131] [Symmetry-enforced agreement of Kohn--Sham and many-body Berry phases in the SSH--Hubbard chain](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.22578)
*Kai Watanabe*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了密度匹配Kohn-Sham描述在相关绝缘体中能否重现多体Berry相位，发现尽管密度在通量和相互作用范围内保持恒定，但多体波函数展现出非平凡的几何响应，且KS与多体Berry相位在整个能隙区一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探究密度匹配Kohn-Sham（KS）描述能否在相关绝缘体中重现多体Berry相位，尽管几何相位是波函数的泛函。这涉及理解密度泛函理论（density functional theory）在拓扑相描述中的局限性。

Method: 以一维SSH-Hubbard链在环上的受控相互作用拓扑模型为研究对象，引入U(1)扭曲θ（通量插入）。通过密度矩阵重整化群（density-matrix renormalization group, DMRG）计算完整扭曲循环中的多体基态，并将在位相互作用U从非相互作用调节到强耦合区域。

Result: 在半填充的反演对称能隙区，DMRG计算显示密度在整个(θ,U)范围内保持恒定，不依赖于通量θ或相互作用强度U。然而，多体波函数展现出非平凡的几何响应：与θ参数化基态流形相关的量子度量在中间U时依赖于θ，在强U时被强烈抑制。有趣的是，KS与多体Berry相位在整个能隙区从弱到强耦合调节U时保持一致。

Conclusion: KS与多体Berry相位的一致性最好理解为对称性强制ℤ₂扇区匹配，而非密度编码多体Berry连接（Berry connection）的证据。这表明密度约束将KS参考系统坍缩为U无关的几何诊断的SSH型二次代表。

Abstract: We study when a density-matching Kohn--Sham (KS) description can reproduce a many-body Berry phase in a correlated insulator, despite the fact that geometric phases are functionals of the wave function. Focusing on the one-dimensional SSH--Hubbard chain on a ring as a controlled interacting topological model, we introduce a $U(1)$ twist $θ$ (flux insertion). The many-body ground state along the full twist cycle is computed by the density-matrix renormalization group (DMRG), while the onsite interaction $U$ is tuned from the noninteracting to the strong-coupling regime. At half filling in the inversion-symmetric gapped regime, our DMRG calculations show that the density remains constant within numerical accuracy over the entire $(θ,U)$ range studied. Thus, the density has no dependence on either the flux $θ$ or the interaction strength $U$. Accordingly, the symmetry-preserving density constraint collapses the KS reference to an SSH-type quadratic representative with $U$-independent geometric diagnostics. Nevertheless, the many-body wave function exhibits a nontrivial geometric response: the quantum metric associated with the $θ$-parametrized ground-state manifold depends on $θ$ at intermediate $U$ and is strongly suppressed at large $U$, consistent with the charge fluctuation freezing. Intriguingly, the KS and many-body Berry phases coincide throughout the gapped regime as $U$ is tuned from weak to strong coupling. We show that this agreement is best understood as symmetry-enforced $\mathbb{Z}_2$ sector matching, rather than as evidence that the density encodes the many-body Berry connection.

### [132] [Memory-Dominated Quantum Criticality as a Universal Route to High-Temperature Superconductivity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.22626)
*Byung Gyu Chae*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了高温超导的动力学起源，提出了一种由弛豫模式时间尺度态密度（TDOS）控制的新型记忆主导临界动力学（memory-dominated criticality）普适类，为高温超导提供了统一的理论框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解高温超导的动力学起源是强关联量子物质研究的核心挑战。传统量子临界性（quantum criticality）方法假设过阻尼马尔可夫耗散（overdamped Markovian dissipation）由欧姆朗道阻尼（Ohmic Landau damping）主导，但这可能无法准确描述实际系统的红外集体动力学行为。

Method: 研究采用Martin-Siggia-Rose-Janssen-De Dominicis形式体系，推导出集体响应函数（collective susceptibility）基于弛豫模式时间尺度态密度（time-scale density of states, TDOS）的精确谱表示。通过分析有限红外TDOS，定义了记忆主导临界动力学（memory-dominated criticality）的新普适类。

Result: 研究发现记忆主导临界动力学具有长时核函数K(t)∼1/t和非解析动力学响应特征。这种谱重组（spectral reorganization）导致粒子-粒子通道（particle-particle channel）的强烈红外放大，将BCS和Eliashberg理论的边际不稳定性（marginal instabilities）转化为代数超导转变（algebraic superconducting transitions）。转变温度与慢集体模式的红外谱权重呈线性比例关系，自然产生超导穹顶（superconducting domes）和Uemura标度律（Uemura scaling）。

Conclusion: 该研究确立了动力学谱组织（dynamical spectral organization）作为量子临界物质的基本原理，并识别出记忆主导临界性（memory-dominated criticality）是通往高温超导的普适路径。同一慢模式库（slow-mode reservoir）也支配着反常正常态动力学，包括长时关联和奇异金属行为（strange-metal behavior），为关联超导体中的热力学和动力学现象提供了统一描述。

Abstract: Understanding the dynamical origin of high--temperature superconductivity remains a central challenge of strongly correlated quantum matter. Conventional approaches to quantum criticality assume overdamped Markovian dissipation governed by Ohmic Landau damping. Here we show that infrared collective dynamics is instead generically controlled by the time--scale density of states (TDOS) of relaxation modes. Within the Martin--Siggia--Rose--Janssen--De Dominicis formalism, we derive an exact spectral representation of the collective susceptibility in terms of the TDOS. A finite infrared TDOS defines a new universality class of memory--dominated critical dynamics characterized by long--time kernels $K(t)\sim1/t$ and nonanalytic dynamical response. This spectral reorganization produces a strong infrared amplification of the particle--particle channel, converting the marginal instabilities of BCS and Eliashberg theories into algebraic superconducting transitions. As a result, the transition temperature scales linearly with the infrared spectral weight of slow collective modes, naturally yielding superconducting domes and Uemura scaling without invoking bosonic glue or fine tuning. The same slow--mode reservoir governs anomalous normal--state dynamics, including long--time correlations and strange--metal behavior, providing a unified description of thermodynamic and dynamical phenomena in correlated superconductors. Our results establish dynamical spectral organization as a fundamental principle of quantum critical matter and identify memory--dominated criticality as a generic route to high--temperature superconductivity.

Abstract: The interaction-driven evolution from a Fermi liquid to a Mott insulator is a hallmark of strongly correlated fermion systems. By jointly analyzing thermodynamic and dynamical observables, we establish the crossover diagram of the model in the temperature-interaction ($T$-$U$) plane. With increasing $U$, our numerical results reveal an extended crossover regime, which we refer to as the {\it Bad Metal}, that separates the Fermi liquid and Mott insulator. During the crossover, we also examine the antiferromagnetic spin correlations and observe pronounced nodal-antinodal dichotomy in the momentum-resolved single-particle spectral functions. Furthermore, we investigate the temperature dependence of several commonly used observables in the model. As representative results, we achieve an accurate map of the thermal entropy across the crossover diagram, and identify the parameter regions in which the model exhibits the Pomeranchuk cooling, characterized by an adiabatic cooling with increasing $U$. Beyond offering a more refined understanding of the crossover phenomenon, our work also provides valuable benchmark and guideline for future optical lattice experiments on the square-lattice Hubbard model.

Conclusion: 研究结果为LaCoO₃中高自旋与低自旋Co³⁺态的动态关联提供了动量分辨证据，建立了自旋态涨落与异常声子重整化（anomalous phonon renormalization）之间的直接联系。

Comparison with quasi-harmonic $ab-initio$ lattice-dynamical calculations helps reveal anomalous softening of a $\approx 10\,\mathrm{meV}$ oxygen phonon, confined to the temperature interval $T_{1} \leq T \leq T_{2}$ and localized in momentum space at $\boldsymbol{q}_{\mathrm{SSO}} = \left( \frac{1}{2},\frac{1}{2},\frac{1}{2} \right)_{c}$. This wave vector corresponds to the spin-state ordering originally proposed by Goodenough [J. Phys. Chem. Solids 6, 287-297 (1958)]. Our results therefore provide momentum-resolved evidence for dynamic correlations of high-spin and low-spin Co$^{3+}$ states in LaCoO$_{3}$, linking spin-state fluctuations to anomalous phonon renormalization.

</details>


### [135] [Quantum magnetic phase transitions in a Kugel-Khomskii model including spin-orbit coupling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.23011)
*D. E. Chizhov,P. A. Igoshev,V. Yu. Irkhin*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文推导了包含自旋轨道耦合的有效Kugel-Khomskii模型哈密顿量，精确考虑了晶体场引起的$t_{2g}$多重态分裂。通过解析求解获得了任意哈伯德排斥与晶体场分裂关系下的解，构建了包含自旋轨道耦合、洪德交换和哈伯德相互作用的基态相图。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于精确处理晶体场引起的$t_{2g}$多重态分裂，并建立能够插值描述莫特-哈伯德（Mott-Hubbard）绝缘体和电荷转移（charge-transfer）绝缘体的理论框架。这需要综合考虑自旋轨道耦合、洪德交换和哈伯德相互作用对轨道序和磁序的影响。

Method: 采用赝自旋（pseudospin）和同位旋（isospin）算符形式体系，推导了包含自旋轨道耦合的有效Kugel-Khomskii模型哈密顿量。通过解析求解方法，处理了哈伯德排斥与晶体场分裂的任意关系，并使用八极矩（octupole moments）描述轨道序。

Result: 获得了基态相图，揭示了隐藏磁序和轨道长程序状态与具有减小磁矩的铁磁态伴随反铁磁轨道序之间的量子相变。研究表明洪德交换和自旋轨道耦合的协同效应导致了易平面型各向异性（easy-plane-type anisotropy）。

Conclusion: 该研究成功建立了能够统一描述莫特-哈伯德和电荷转移绝缘体的理论框架，精确处理了晶体场效应。结果表明自旋轨道耦合与洪德交换的协同作用对系统的磁性和轨道性质具有重要影响，特别是导致了易平面型各向异性。

Abstract: Using the formalism of pseudospin and isospin operators the Hamiltonian of an effective Kugel-Khomskii model with spin-orbit coupling is derived with an exact account of the $t_{2g}$ multiplet splitting by the crystal field. An analytical solution is obtained for an arbitrary relation between the Hubbard repulsion and crystal field splitting, i.e., interpolating the cases of Mott-Hubbard and charge-transfer insulators. A description of orbital orders is given in terms of octupole moments. The ground-state phase diagram is constructed in the parameter space spanned by spin-orbit coupling, Hund's exchange, and Hubbard interaction. We investigate a quantum phase transition between a state exhibiting hidden magnetic and orbital long-range order and a ferromagnetic state with a reduced magnetic moment accompanied by antiferroorbital order. It is shown that the cooperative effect of Hund's and spin-orbit interactions gives rise to an easy-plane-type anisotropy.

### [136] [$Z_3$ confined and deconfined Coulomb liquids in $S_{\rm eff} = 3/2$ pyrochlore magnets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.23041)
*Jay Pandey,Souvik Kundu,Kedar Damle*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究在烧绿石磁体中识别出一个特殊物理区域，其中自旋轨道和晶体场效应产生两个低能磁双态，可建模为有效自旋S=3/2。研究发现两个拓扑不同的零场库仑相，由一阶Z3禁闭相变分隔，并预测实验系统在冷却至临界温度以下时会展现此拓扑相变特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究烧绿石磁体中自旋轨道和晶体场效应产生的特殊物理区域，其中两个低能磁双态可建模为有效自旋S=3/2，并存在主导易轴反铁磁交换与强单离子各向异性之间的竞争。

Method: 通过分析T/J→0极限，以w≡exp(-μ/T)作为控制变量进行精确研究。在此极限下，系统可描述为粗粒度无散极化场的涨落。

Result: 发现两个拓扑不同的零场库仑相，由一阶Z3禁闭相变在wc≈2.02处分隔。其中一个相中极化场通量限制为3的整数倍，仅3的倍数的电荷退禁闭；另一相中所有整数通量和电荷均退禁闭。

Conclusion: 具有小负μ值的实验系统在冷却至Tc≈1.42|μ|以下时，预计会展现此拓扑相变的特征，为烧绿石磁体的拓扑性质提供了新的理论预测。

Abstract: We identify an interesting regime in the physics of pyrochlore magnets in which spin-orbit and crystal field effects lead to {\em two} low-lying magnetic doublets that can be modeled as an effective spin $S=3/2$ degree of freedom that sees a dominant easy-axis antiferromagnetic exchange $J>0$ favoring the local $[111]$ axes, which competes with a comparably strong single-ion anisotropy $Δ= J+μ/2$ (with $|μ| \ll J$) favoring the perpendicular planes. For a precise analysis, we study the $T/J \rightarrow 0$ limit in which $w \equiv \exp(-μ/T)$ is the control variable. In this limit, we find {\em two topologically distinct} zero-field Coulomb phases separated by a first-order $Z_3$ confinement transition at $w_c \approx 2.02$. Both Coulomb phases admit a description in terms of the fluctuations of a coarse-grained divergence-free polarization field. However, the flux of this polarization field is restricted to integer multiples of $3$, and only charges that are multiples of 3 are deconfined in one of these phases, while all integer fluxes are allowed and all integer charges are deconfined in the other phase. Experimental systems with small negative $μ$ ({\em i.e.}, $-J \ll μ< 0$) are therefore predicted to exhibit signatures of this topological transition when cooled below $T_c \approx 1.42|μ|$.

### [137] [Extended Ashkin-Teller transition in two coupled frustrated Haldane chains](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.23187)
*Bowy M. La Rivière,Natalia Chepiga*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究报道了具有三体交换相互作用的两个自旋-1 Haldane链在之字形梯子上的丰富基态相图，揭示了多种量子相变类型和相之间的复杂关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索两个自旋-1 Haldane链在之字形梯子（zig-zag ladder）结构中的复杂量子相行为，特别是当系统受到三体交换相互作用（three-site exchange）和反铁磁海森堡相互作用（antferromagnetic Heisenberg interaction）耦合时的基态相图。

Method: 研究方法基于对两个自旋-1 Haldane链在之字形梯子上的理论分析，考虑了链间反铁磁海森堡相互作用和链内三体交换相互作用，通过分析不同相互作用参数下的基态性质来构建相图。

Result: 研究发现了极其丰富的基态相图，包括斑块相（plaquette phase）、均匀无序相（uniform disordered phase）、二聚化相（dimerized phase）和Haldane相。这些相之间通过多种量子相变分离，包括Ashkin-Teller普适类（Ashkin-Teller universality class）的扩展相变、拓扑高斯相变（topological Gaussian transition）、非磁性伊辛相变（non-magnetic Ising transition）和拓扑弱一级相变（topological weak first-order transition）。

Conclusion: 在链间相互作用减小的极限下，中间无序相消失，系统呈现二聚化相。当两条链完全解耦时，系统恢复到一个量子临界点，对应两个Wess-Zumino-Witten SU(2)₂临界性的副本，总中心荷（central charge）c=3。

Abstract: We report an extremely rich ground state phase diagram of two spin-1 Haldane chains frustrated with a three-site exchange and coupled by the antiferromagnetic Heisenberg interaction on a zig-zag ladder. A particular feature of the phase diagram is the extended quantum phase transition in the Ashkin-Teller universality class that separates the plaquette phase, which spontaneously breaks translation symmetry, and the uniform disordered phase. The former is connected to the Haldane phase, stabilized by large inter-chain coupling, via the topological Gaussian transition. Upon decreasing the inter-chain interactions, this intermediate disorder phase vanishes, giving place to a dimerized phase separated from the plaquette phase on one side via a non-magnetic Ising transition and from the Haldane phase on the other side by a topological weak first-order transition. Finally, in the limit of two decoupled chains, we recover a quantum critical point that corresponds to two copies of the Wess-Zumino-Witten $\mathrm{SU(2)}_2$ criticality with a total central charge $c=3$.

### [138] [Magnetic order and excitations in Ce$_3$TiBi$_5$ and Ce$_3$ZrBi$_5$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.23316)
*Pyeongjae Park,Qianli Ma,Wei Tian,Stuart Calder,Matthias Frontzek,G. Sala,D. Mandrus,Shirin Mozaffari,Andrew D. Christianson,Matthew B. Stone*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究通过中子散射技术系统研究了Ce3TiBi5和Ce3ZrBi5两种局域非中心对称Kondo晶格化合物的磁结构、晶体电场和低能激发，揭示了其非常规的螺旋反铁磁序和显著的Kondo杂化效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: R3MBi5稀土金属间化合物为探索Kondo杂化、RKKY交换、磁阻挫和破缺反演对称性如何协同产生非常规磁行为提供了多功能平台。研究旨在理解这些相互作用在局域非中心对称Kondo晶格化合物中的集体效应。

Method: 采用综合中子散射技术，包括粉末和单晶中子衍射确定磁结构，以及非弹性中子散射测量晶体电场激发和低能响应。研究聚焦于Ce3TiBi5和Ce3ZrBi5两种化合物。

Result: Ce3TiBi5显示非公度螺旋反铁磁序，传播矢量k = (0, 0, 0.388)，有序磁矩降低至m = 0.53(3)μB。两种化合物均显示两个清晰分离的晶体电场激发，确认了良好隔离的Kramers双重态基态。低能区观察到宽准弹性磁响应，其动量依赖性与局域磁矩的传统集体激发预期不符。

Conclusion: 这些化合物处于局域反演对称性破缺、各向异性晶体电场效应以及竞争性Kondo和RKKY相互作用共同产生非常规磁序的区域。Kondo温度估计TK ~ 3-5 K与TN相当，表明显著的Kondo杂化，解释了磁矩降低和涉及磁硬方向的螺旋磁序。

Abstract: The R3MBi5 rare-earth intermetallics (R = rare earth, M = Ti, Zr, Sc) provide a versatile platform to explore how Kondo hybridization, RKKY exchange, magnetic frustration, and broken inversion symmetry may cooperate to generate unusual magnetic behavior. We present a comprehensive neutron scattering investigation of the magnetic structure, crystal electric field (CEF), and low-energy excitations in the locally noncentrosymmetric Kondo-lattice compounds Ce3TiBi5 and Ce3ZrBi5. Powder and single-crystal neutron diffraction reveals incommensurate cycloidal antiferromagnetic order in Ce3TiBi5 with propagation vector k = (0, 0, 0.388) and a reduced ordered moment of m = 0.53(3)$μ_{B}$. Ce3ZrBi5 exhibits a qualitatively similar magnetic diffraction profile, with k $\simeq$ (0, 0, 0.37). Inelastic neutron scattering measurements resolve two clear, well-separated CEF excitations in both compounds with nearly the same profile, confirming a well-isolated Kramers doublet ground state. At low energies, a broad, quasi-elastic magnetic response is observed at T $\simeq$ TN, whose momentum-dependence is inconsistent with that expected from conventional collective excitations of localized moments. This discrepancy, along with a Kondo temperature estimate TK ~ 3--5 K -- comparable to TN -- indicates sizable Kondo hybridization, which accounts for the moment reduction and the spiral magnetic order that appears to involve the magnetic hard direction. Our results place these compounds in a regime where local inversion symmetry breaking, anisotropic CEF effects, and competing Kondo and RKKY interactions collectively give rise to unconventional magnetic order.

</details>


### [139] [Arrested Relaxation in a Disorder-Free Coulomb Spin Liquid](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.23362)
*Souvik Kundu,Arnab Seth,Sthitadhi Roy,Subhro Bhattacharjee,Roderich Moessner*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了自旋-3/2冰（spin-3/2 ice）中的库仑自旋液体（Coulomb spin liquids）具有新颖特性，包括由晶体场激发（crystal-field excitations）与磁单极子（magnetic monopoles）相互作用导致的动力学阻滞（dynamical arrest）现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索自旋-3/2冰中扩展的局域希尔伯特空间（on-site Hilbert space）如何产生新型库仑自旋液体相，超越传统自旋-1/2冰中的磁单极子物理。

Method: 通过研究热淬火（thermal quench）后的动力学过程，分析自旋自关联（spin autocorrelations）中的非热平台（athermal plateau）现象，揭示复合激发结构（composite excitation structures）和动力学约束弛豫路径（kinetically constrained relaxation pathways）的作用机制。

Result: 研究发现系统在热淬火后表现出显著的动力学阻滞，自旋自关联呈现指数级长寿命的非热平台，这是短程相互作用、无淬火无序（quenched disorder）系统中罕见的动力学阻滞实例。

Conclusion: 研究结论表明高自旋冰（higher-spin ice）为实现非常规库仑自旋液体和无淬火无序条件下的动力学阻滞提供了肥沃平台，揭示了由独特复合激发结构和需要激活过程的动力学约束弛豫路径所导致的阻滞动力学起源。

Abstract: We investigate Coulomb spin liquids in classical spin-3/2 ice and show that the enlarged on-site Hilbert space gives rise to a qualitatively new class of such phases. Beyond the conventional magnetic monopoles of spin-1/2 ice, the system hosts additional low-energy crystal-field excitations, whose interplay with monopoles significantly modifies both equilibrium and non-equilibrium properties. Following a thermal quench, we find a pronounced dynamical arrest manifested in an exponentially long-lived {athermal} plateau in spin autocorrelations. This constitutes a rare example of dynamical arrest in a short-range interacting, disorder-free system. We demonstrate that the arrested dynamics originate from novel composite excitation structures unique to spin-3/2 ice and from kinetically constrained relaxation pathways that require activated processes. Our results establish higher-spin ice as a fertile platform for realising unconventional Coulomb spin liquids and dynamical arrest without quenched disorder.

### [140] [Taxonomy of Integrable and Ground-State Solvable Models: Jastrow Wavefunctions on Graphs and Parent Hamiltonians](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.22315)
*Nilanjan Sasmal,Adolfo del Campo*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该研究引入了一类基于图结构的连续变量多体系统，其基态波函数具有广义Jastrow形式，哈密顿量包含由图的邻接矩阵决定的二体相互作用和基于图中所有2-路径的三体相互作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究旨在构建一类基于图结构的连续变量多体系统，将量子流体和自旋系统统一到同一理论框架中。当图完全连接且配对函数具有良好定义的置换对称性时，这些系统描述量子流体；一般情况下，它们提供了图上自旋系统的连续变量推广。

Method: 研究引入了一类可区分连续变量粒子的多体系统，其中粒子间相互作用由图的邻接矩阵设定。基态波函数采用广义Jastrow形式，包含图上边集配对相关函数的乘积。利用图论工具，研究绘制了模型图谱，并推导了相应的父哈密顿量。

Result: 研究结果表明，相应的父哈密顿量包含两部分：(a) 由图的邻接矩阵决定的二体相互作用；(b) 图上所有可能2-路径的三体相互作用。通过图论分析，研究恢复了文献中的已知实例，并提供了大量新的基态可解模型示例。

Conclusion: 该研究成功构建了一类基于图结构的连续变量多体系统理论框架，统一了量子流体和自旋系统的描述。通过图论方法，研究系统性地探索了模型空间，为基态可解模型提供了新的理论工具和实例。

Abstract: We introduce a family of many-body systems of distinguishable continuous-variable particles in which interparticle interactions are set by the adjacency matrix of a graph. The ground-state wavefunction of such systems is of a generalized Jastrow form involving the product of pair-correlation functions over the edge set of the graph. These systems describe quantum fluids when the graph is complete, and the pair function has a well-defined permutation symmetry. In general, they provide the continuous-variable generalization of spin systems on graphs, with broken permutation symmetry. The corresponding parent Hamiltonian is shown to include (a) two-body interactions determined by the graph adjacency matrix and (b) three-body interactions over all possible 2-paths on the graph. Employing elements of graph theory, we chart the landscape of models, recovering known instances in the literature and providing numerous new examples of ground-state solvable models for which the system Hamiltonian, ground-state wavefunction, and corresponding energy eigenvalue are specified.

</details>


### [141] [Fundamental Limits on QBER and Distance in Quantum Key Distribution](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.22319)
*Stefano Pirandola*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该研究确立了量子密钥分发（QKD）的最大量子比特误码率（QBER）容限，并推导出通信距离的上界，阐明了QKD的终极噪声鲁棒性和安全量子通信的基本边界。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子密钥分发（QKD）虽能实现信息论安全通信，但其对噪声的最终容限和可达传输距离仍受基本限制。研究旨在明确QKD的安全边界，为实际应用提供理论基础。

Method: 基于量子比特泡利信道（qubit Pauli channels）的基本容量阈值，推导出适用于基于两个或多个互不正交基（mutually unbiased bases）协议的理论框架，涵盖单光子源和弱相干源（weak coherent sources）两种方案。

Result: 建立了与安全QKD兼容的最大量子比特误码率（QBER），并推导出相应的通信距离上界。通过将信息论极限与现实物理噪声模型连接，获得了光纤和自由空间链路中可达距离的普适边界，包括与深空量子通信相关的衍射限制约束。

Conclusion: 研究结果阐明了QKD的终极噪声鲁棒性，并划定了安全量子通信的基本边界，为评估不同QKD协议的性能极限和实际部署提供了理论依据。

Abstract: Quantum key distribution (QKD) enables information-theoretic secure communication, yet its ultimate tolerance to noise and achievable transmission distance remain fundamentally constrained. We establish the maximum quantum bit error rate (QBER) compatible with secure QKD and derive corresponding upper bounds on communication distance. Our results follow from a fundamental capacity threshold for qubit Pauli channels and apply to protocols based on two or more mutually unbiased bases, using either single-photon or weak coherent sources. By connecting information-theoretic limits to realistic physical noise models, we obtain universal bounds on achievable distances in fiber and free-space links, including diffraction-limited constraints relevant to deep-space quantum communications. These findings clarify the ultimate noise robustness of QKD and delineate the fundamental boundaries of secure quantum communication.

### [142] [Quantum simulation of massive Thirring and Gross--Neveu models for arbitrary number of flavors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.22313)
*Bojko N. Bakalov,Joao C. Getelina,Raghav G. Jha,Alexander F. Kemper,Yuan Liu*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该研究针对一维晶格上的大N_f费米子量子场论模型，计算了量子门复杂度，实现了高达20量子比特系统的基态制备，并分析了这些模型的动力学李代数分类。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究费米子量子场论对于在量子计算机上实现粒子物理标准模型具有重要意义。本文旨在为手征对称性破缺、维度嬗变和共形窗口探索等物理现象的大N_f费米子量子场论实时动力学量子模拟提供具体步骤。

Method: 采用哈密顿量表述，将具有任意费米子味数N_f的大质量Thirring和Gross-Neveu模型离散化在一维空间晶格上。使用高阶乘积公式、块编码/量子化及量子奇异值变换计算门复杂度，并采用自适应变分量子虚时算法制备基态。

Result: 在大N_f和L极限下计算了门复杂度，成功制备了N_f=1,2,3,4、系统规模达20量子比特的基态且保真度优异。分析表明这些相对论性费米子模型的动力学李代数属于相同的同构类。

Conclusion: 该工作为在近期和早期容错量子计算机上模拟大N_f费米子量子场论的实时动力学提供了具体进展，有助于研究手征对称性破缺、维度嬗变和场论共形窗口等物理现象。

Abstract: The study of fermionic quantum field theories is an important problem for realizing the standard model of particle physics on a quantum computer. As a step towards this goal, we consider the massive Thirring and Gross--Neveu models with arbitrary number of fermion flavors, $N_f$, discretized on a spatial one-dimensional lattice of size $L$ in the Hamiltonian formulation. We compute the gate complexity using the higher-order product formula and using block-encoding/qubitization and quantum singular value transformations in the limit of large $N_f$ and $L$. We also prepare the ground states of both models with excellent fidelity for system sizes up to 20 qubits with $N_f = 1,2,3,4$ using the adaptive-variational quantum imaginary time algorithm. In addition, we also classify the dynamical Lie algebras of these relativistic fermionic models and show that they belong to the same isomorphism class. Our work is a concrete step towards the quantum simulation of real-time dynamics of large $N_f$ fermionic quantum field theories models relevant for chiral symmetry breaking, understanding dimensional transmutation, and exploring the conformal window of field theories on near-term and early fault-tolerant quantum computers.

</details>


### [143] [Optimization-based Unfolding in High-Energy Physics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.22776)
*Simone Gasperini,Gianluca Bianco,Marco Lorusso,Carla Rieger,Michele Grossi*

TL;DR: 该研究将高能物理中的反卷积（unfolding）问题重新表述为带正则化的二次优化问题，开发了经典与量子兼容的求解框架，并实现了开源工具QUnfold进行性能评估。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高能物理中反卷积（unfolding）是从探测器畸变测量中重建物理可观测量真实分布的关键过程。当前需要建立统一优化视角并探索量子增强方法在实验数据分析中的应用。

Method: 将反卷积问题重新表述为带正则化的二次优化问题，推导出二次无约束二进制优化（Quadratic Unconstrained Binary Optimization, QUBO）表示形式。该方法允许在量子退火和混合量子-经典求解器上直接实现，并在QUnfold开源Python包中集成了经典混合整数求解器和D-Wave混合量子求解器。

Result: 在具有受控畸变效应的合成数据集上，该方法与RooUnfold中广泛使用的反卷积技术（包括响应矩阵求逆、迭代贝叶斯反卷积和奇异值分解反卷积）进行了基准测试。结果显示基于优化的方法在多个分布上实现了具有竞争力的重建精度，同时自然地在目标函数中融入了正则化。

Conclusion: 该工作建立了反卷积问题的统一优化视角，并为在实验高能物理数据分析中探索量子增强方法提供了实用途径。QUnfold框架展示了量子兼容方法在该领域的应用潜力。

Abstract: In High-Energy Physics, unfolding is the process of reconstructing true distributions of physical observables from detector-distorted measurements. Starting from its reformulation as a regularized quadratic optimization, we develop a framework to tackle this problem using both classical and quantum-compatible methods. In particular, we derive a Quadratic Unconstrained Binary Optimization (QUBO) representation of the unfolding objective, allowing direct implementation on quantum annealing and hybrid quantum-classical solvers. The proposed approach is implemented in QUnfold, an open-source Python package integrating classical mixed-integer solvers and D-Wave's hybrid quantum solver. We benchmark the method against widely used unfolding techniques in RooUnfold, including response Matrix Inversion, Iterative Bayesian Unfolding, and Singular Value Decomposition unfolding, using synthetic dataset with controlled distortion effects. Our results demonstrate that the optimization-based approach achieves competitive reconstruction accuracy across multiple distributions while naturally accommodating regularization within the objective function. This work establishes a unified optimization perspective on unfolding and provides a practical pathway for exploring quantum-enhanced methods in experimental HEP data analysis.

### [144] [Gravitational decoherence and recoherence of a composite particle: the interplay between gravitons and a classical Newtonian potential](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.22517)
