<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 引力环境的不可屏蔽性使其在退相干机制和量子-经典转变中具有重要理论意义。尽管过去研究认为引力子诱导的空间叠加态退相干仅发生于宏观系统，但近期发现系统的动态内部结构可增强此机制。

Method: 扩展了先前分析，将经典牛顿势（classical Newtonian potential）的相互作用纳入考虑。研究了引力子浴（graviton bath）与系统内部自由度（internal degrees of freedom）之间的相互作用机制。

Result: 引力子浴在量子空间叠加态尺寸确定的时间尺度内主导退相干机制。然而，引力子与系统内部自由度的相互作用使得即使在微观质量情况下，长时间极限下退相干也必然发生。经典牛顿势的相互作用会略微减缓此机制。

Conclusion: 对于无动态内部自由度的系统，经典牛顿势的相互作用至少在理论上可导致重相干（recoherence）。引力子与内部自由度的相互作用是微观系统退相干的关键机制。

Abstract: The fact that gravitational environments cannot be shielded (since gravity is universal) makes them of great theoretical interest to decoherence mechanisms and to the quantum-to-classical transition. While past results seemed to indicate that graviton-induced decoherence of spatial superpositions happens only for macroscopic systems, recently it was shown that this mechanism can be enhanced through the system's own dynamical internal structure. In this work, we extend this analysis by including the interaction with a classical Newtonian potential. We show that, although the graviton bath alone dominates the mechanism for short times compared to a timescale established by the size of the quantum spatial superposition, the interplay between the gravitons and the internal degrees of freedom of the system renders decoherence inevitable in the long-time limit, even for microscopic masses. We also show that this mechanism is slightly slowed down by the interplay with the classical Newtonian potential, which, for systems without dynamical internal degrees of freedom, can even lead to recoherence, at least in principle.

### [145] [Schwinger-Keldysh field theory for operator Rényi entropy and entanglement growth in non-interacting systems with sub-ballistic transports](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.22331)

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种基于子系统算子Rényi熵的算子增长度量，建立了量子动力学中算子增长与输运、纠缠生成之间的联系。通过构建统一的Schwinger-Keldysh场论形式，分析了准周期和随机无序系统中的算子与纠缠增长行为。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 定义了基于子系统算子Rényi熵（subsystem operator Rényi entropy）的算子增长度量，构建了统一的Schwinger-Keldysh（SK）场论形式来描述算子Rényi熵和初始纯态纠缠熵的时间演化。该方法利用无限温度和真空Keldysh格林函数分别计算非相互作用系统中的算子Rényi熵和态纠缠熵。

Abstract: The notion of operator growth in quantum systems furnishes a bridge between transport and the generation of entanglement between different parts of the system under quantum dynamics. We define a measure of operator growth in terms of subsystem operator Rényi entropy, which provides a state-independent measure of operator growth, unlike entanglement entropies, and the usual measures of operator growth like out-of-time-order correlators. We show that the subsystem operator Rényi entropy encodes both spatial and temporal information, and thus can directly connect to transport for a local operator related to a conserved quantity. We construct a unified Schwinger-Keldysh (SK) field theory formalism for the time evolution of operator Rényi entropy and entanglement entropies of initial pure states. We use the SK field theory to obtain the operator Rényi and state entanglement entropies in terms of infinite-temperature and vacuum Keldysh Green's functions, respectively, for non-interacting systems. We apply the method to explore the connection between operator and entanglement growth, and transport in non-interacting systems with quasiperiodic and random disorder, like the one- and two-dimensional Aubry-André models and the two-dimensional Anderson model. In particular, we show that the growth of subsystem operator Rényi entropy and state von Neumann and Rényi entanglement entropies can capture both ballistic and sub-ballistic transport behaviors, like diffusive and anomalous diffusive transport, as well as localization in these systems.

Abstract: Excited-state quantum phase transitions (ESQPTs) have been extensively studied in two-level models, but their characterization remains challenging in systems displaying mixed regular and chaotic dynamics. In this work, we investigate ESQPTs within the three-level Lipkin-Meshkov-Glick model, where an enlarged Hilbert space and multiple separatrices give rise to rich spectral structures strongly influenced by chaos. To investigate the different dynamical regions, we have calculated Poincaré sections and Peres lattices. In addition, by combining chaos-sensitive measures with standard ESQPT diagnostics, we provide a static analysis of ESQPT signatures in this model and establish a robust framework for future studies of its dynamical behavior. The degree of chaos and the Kullback-Leibler divergence are found to be very effective chaos-sensitive measures, which are complementary to ESQPT diagnostics such as the mean field limit and the participation ratio. Hence we provide a standard framework to work with ESQPTs in chaotic three-level systems.

Abstract: Adiabatic (or reversible) processes are the key concept unifying our understanding of thermodynamics and dynamical systems. ### [151] [Symmetry-protected control of Liouvillian topological phases via Hamiltonian band topology](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.22323)
*Shu Long,Chao Yang,Sen Mu,Linhu Li*

TL;DR: 该研究建立了相干哈密顿量的能带拓扑与开放量子系统Lindblad描述中刘维尔算符谱缠绕之间的对称性保护对应关系，揭示了哈密顿量拓扑可作为控制刘维尔算符拓扑和非平衡动力学的主动调控手段。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在揭示哈密顿量拓扑与开放量子系统中刘维尔算符拓扑之间的主动控制关系，而非传统上系统-环境交换对哈密顿量的被动影响。这为理解哈密顿量与耗散动力学中的拓扑提供了统一视角。

Method: 通过在一类一维耗散晶格中精确求解刘维尔算符谱（Liouvillian spectrum），研究分析了哈密顿量能带拓扑（band topology）对刘维尔算符谱缠绕（spectral winding）的约束作用。该方法要求哈密顿量与量子跃迁算符（quantum jump operators）保持相同的手征对称性（chiral symmetry）。

Result: 研究发现哈密顿量能带拓扑约束了刘维尔算符谱缠绕，并决定了刘维尔皮肤效应（Liouvillian skin effect）。晶格宇称（lattice parity）进一步控制了相关的体-边对应关系（bulk-boundary correspondence）和稳态的相干性质（coherence properties）。

Conclusion: 该研究揭示了开放量子系统中谱和空间组织的对称性增强拓扑控制机制，为哈密顿量与耗散动力学中的拓扑提供了统一的理论框架。这一发现表明哈密顿量拓扑可作为主动调控开放系统非平衡动力学的有效手段。

Abstract: We establish a symmetry-protected correspondence between band topology of coherent Hamiltonians and Liouvillian spectral winding in Lindblad descriptions of open quantum systems. This allows the Hamiltonian topology to act as a knob for controlling Liouvillian topology and corresponding non-equilibrium dynamics, rather than being passively manipulated by system-environment exchanges. In particular, by exactly solving the Liouvillian spectrum in a class of one-dimensional dissipative lattices, we find that the Hamiltonian band topology constrains the Liouvillian spectral winding and determines the Liouvillian skin effect, provided the Hamiltonian and quantum jump operators respect the same chiral symmetry. We further demonstrate that lattice parity controls the associated bulk-boundary correspondence and the coherence properties of the steady state. Our results unveil a symmetry-enforced topological control of spectral and spatial organization in open quantum systems, providing a unified perspective on topology in Hamiltonian and dissipative dynamics.

</details>


### [152] [Numerical Experiments with Parameter Setting of Trotterized Quantum Phase Estimation for Quantum Hamiltonian Ground State Computation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.22349)
*Elijah Pelofske,Stephan Eidenbenz*

TL;DR: 该研究通过数值模拟分析了量子相位估计算法（QPE）在计算量子磁体基态能量任务中的性能，重点关注了时间演化、Trotter阶数、Trotter步数和初始态等输入参数对算法运行的实际影响，并提出了量子算法输入和调优指南。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究方法包括对相对较小的量子哈密顿量（3个量子比特）进行QPE电路计算的经典数值模拟，精度达到10个相位比特，Trotter阶数最高为10。系统研究了QPE的输入参数：时间演化、Trotter阶数、Trotter步数和初始态。

Result: 研究发现QPE对最优数字化相位的采样收敛于固定速率，导致最优相位采样速率出现显著的边际效益递减现象，这种现象在Trotter误差较高时可能出现。研究阐明了这些输入参数如何实际决定QPE的运行方式。

Conclusion: 基于研究结果，作者提出了一套连贯的量子算法输入和调优指南，为量子相位估计算法的实际应用提供了系统性的参数选择和优化框架。

Abstract: We numerically investigate quantum circuit elementary-gate level instantiations of the standard Quantum Phase Estimation (QPE) algorithm for the task of computing the ground-state energy of a quantum magnet; the disordered fully-connected quantum Heisenberg spin glass model. We consider (classical simulations of) QPE circuit computations on relatively small quantum Hamiltonians ($3$ qubits) with up to $10$ phase bits of precision, using up to Trotter order $10$. We systematically study the inputs of QPE, specifically time evolution, Trotter order, Trotter steps, and initial state, and illustrate how these inputs practically determine how QPE operates. From this we outline a coherent set of quantum algorithm input and tuning guidelines. One of the notable properties we characterize is that QPE sampling of the optimal digitized phase converges to a fixed rate. This results in strong diminishing returns of optimal phase sampling rates which can occur when the Trotter error is surprisingly high.

</details>

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 本教程提供了MQED及其向活性介质（active media）扩展的概述。方法重点在于利用场关联理论框架，分析增益介质如何修改场关联特性。

Result: 涨落诱导力（fluctuation-induced forces）被识别为增益修正场关联的具体表现形式。这表明活性介质中的增益效应能够显著改变量子电磁场的统计特性，进而影响相关的物理现象。

Conclusion: MQED框架为理解宏观环境中量子电磁现象提供了统一的理论基础，其向活性介质的扩展揭示了增益修正场关联在涨落诱导力中的关键作用，为研究复杂介质中的量子电动力学现象开辟了新方向。

Abstract: Macroscopic quantum electrodynamics (MQED) provides a unified framework to describe quantum electromagnetic fields in the presence of arbitrary macroscopic environments. Central to this theory is the field correlation, which governs both radiative (e.g., Lamb shifts and the Purcell effect) and mechanical phenomena, such as van der Waals and Casimir forces. In this tutorial, we provide an overview of MQED and its extension to active media, highlighting fluctuation-induced forces as manifestations of gain-modified field correlations.

### [154] [Thermodynamic Uncertainty Relation with Quantum Feedback](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.22651)
*Ryotaro Honma,Tan Van Vu*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该研究推导了开放量子系统中包含反馈控制的有限时间热力学不确定性关系（TUR），揭示了反馈控制如何通过量子互信息（quantum mutual information）抑制涨落并建立基于信息控制的基本精度界限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 涨落是微观系统的固有特性，对非平衡精度施加了基本限制，如热力学不确定性关系（thermodynamic uncertainty relation, TUR）所描述。然而，反馈控制在TUR框架中的作用尚不明确，特别是在量子系统中，控制本质上是信息驱动的。

Method: 研究考虑弱耦合于热环境的开放量子系统，其中量子跃迁（quantum jumps）被连续监测，并应用马尔可夫反馈（Markovian feedback）。使用量子互信息（quantum mutual information）量化反馈引起的信息贡献，推导了任意时间积分电流（time-integrated currents）的有限时间TUR。

Result: 研究揭示了反馈控制如何与热力学成本共同抑制涨落，并建立了基于信息控制的基本精度界限。通过分析量子钟模型（quantum clock model），证明了在单个热库存在下，反馈控制可以增强时钟精度。

Conclusion: 该工作阐明了反馈控制在量子热力学不确定性关系中的作用，建立了包含信息贡献的精度界限，为量子信息-热力学交叉领域提供了理论基础。

Abstract: Fluctuations are intrinsic to microscopic systems and impose fundamental limits on nonequilibrium precision, as captured by the thermodynamic uncertainty relation (TUR), which links current fluctuations to entropy production. While feedback control is expected to further suppress fluctuations, its role within the TUR framework has remained unclear, particularly in quantum systems where control is inherently information-driven. In this Letter, we consider open quantum systems weakly coupled to a thermal environment, in which quantum jumps are continuously monitored, and Markovian feedback is applied. Using quantum mutual information to quantify the information contribution induced by feedback, we derive a finite-time TUR for arbitrary time-integrated currents in terms of entropy production and mutual information. Our results uncover how feedback control suppresses fluctuations together with thermodynamic cost and establishes a fundamental precision bound imposed by information-based control. As an application, we analyze a quantum clock model and demonstrate that the clock precision can be enhanced by feedback control in the presence of a single thermal reservoir.

Abstract: We investigate the steady state of two single-mode uniform spatially separated polaritonic conden- sates exposed to resonant pumping with entangled pairs of photons. Estimates are provided for the flux of entangled particles required to drive the system into a steady state that violates the partial-transpose criterion for entanglement. Furthermore, we trace the evolution of the system after a sudden disappearance of the entangled pumping. Our analysis provides estimates for the entanglement lifetime in a system of two exciton-polariton condensates

Leveraging this mechanism, we assemble array units as functional pixels and demonstrate a scalable polarization-selective quantum light modulator. Our work establishes a dynamically reconfigurable atomic-photonic platform for versatile subwavelength quantum optical elements.

### [158] [Confined and Deconfined Phases of Qubit Regularized Lattice Gauge Theories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.22515)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究旨在构建无符号问题的量子比特正则化格点规范理论，以探索受限与去受限相之间的相变，并为定义连续极限提供非微扰途径。

Method: 采用单体-二聚体-张量网络（monomer--dimer--tensor-network, MDTN）基构建简单量子比特正则化哈密顿量格点规范理论，并使用经典蒙特卡洛方法（classical Monte Carlo methods）研究有限温度相变。

Result: 所构建模型在纯规范场部分无符号问题，能自然实现受限相和去受限相；有限温度相变展现出与传统SU(N)格点规范理论在各种时空维度中相同的普适性类（universality classes）。

Conclusion: 受限相与去受限相之间可能存在二阶量子相变，这为定义量子比特正则化规范理论的连续极限提供了非微扰途径，使得杨-米尔斯理论（Yang--Mills theory）及相关连续规范理论可从有限维格点构造中涌现。

Abstract: We construct simple qubit-regularized Hamiltonian lattice gauge theories formulated in the monomer--dimer--tensor-network (MDTN) basis that are free of sign problems in the pure gauge sector. These models naturally realize both confined and deconfined phases. Using classical Monte Carlo methods, we investigate the associated finite-temperature phase transitions and show that they exhibit the expected universality classes of conventional SU(N) lattice gauge theories in various spacetime dimensions. Furthermore, we argue that second-order quantum phase transitions separating the confined and deconfined phases are likely to exist. Such critical points would provide a nonperturbative route to defining continuum limits of qubit-regularized gauge theories, potentially allowing Yang--Mills theory and related continuum gauge theories to emerge from finite-dimensional lattice constructions.

### [159] [Generalization of lattice Dirac operator index](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.22858)
*Shoto Aoki,Hajime Fujita,Hidenori Fukaya,Mikio Furuta,Shinichiroh Matsuo,Tetsuya Onogi,Satoshi Yamaguchi*

Main category: hep-lat

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于K理论和谱流（spectral flow）的狄拉克算子（Dirac operator）指标（indices）的格点（lattice）表述，相比传统的Ginsparg-Wilson关系定义的指标具有更广泛的适用性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统基于Ginsparg-Wilson关系的重叠狄拉克算子（overlap Dirac operator）指标定义仅限于偶数维平坦环面（flat tori），需要更通用的格点表述来克服这些限制。

Method: 采用K理论（K-theory）通过威尔逊狄拉克算子（Wilson Dirac operator）的谱流（spectral flow）进行分类，构建了统一的格点表述框架。

Result: 该表述具有三个关键优势：1) 可直接应用于带边界流形的Atiyah-Patodi-Singer指标；2) 允许弯曲边界并包含引力背景效应；3) 可在偶数和奇数维度自然定义模2指标（mod-2 index）。

Conclusion: 提出的格点表述为狄拉克算子指标提供了更通用和灵活的数学框架，并通过数学证明和数值证据验证了其有效性。

Abstract: We provide a comprehensive lattice formulation of various types of the Dirac operator indices, employing $K$-theory to classify the Wilson Dirac operator via its spectral flow. In contrast to the index of the overlap Dirac operator defined through the Ginsparg-Wilson relation, which is restricted to flat tori in even dimensions, our formulation offers several key advantages: 1) It can be applied straightforwardly to the Atiyah-Patodi-Singer index for manifolds with boundary. 2) The boundary can be curved, allowing for the inclusion of gravitational background effects. 3) The mod-2 index in both even and odd dimensions can be defined as a natural extension of the same formulation. In this talk, we present the mathematical proof and provide numerical evidence supporting the formulation.

</details>


### [160] [Spatially inhomogeneous confinement-deconfinement phase transition in rotating QGP](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.23094)
*V. V. Braguta,M. N. Chernodub,Ya. A. Gershtein,A. A. Roenko*

Main category: hep-lat

TL;DR: 通过第一性原理数值模拟，在旋转胶子等离子体中发现了一种新的空间非均匀相，该相同时包含禁闭态和解禁闭态区域，由空间相变分隔。边界位置由局域临界温度决定，且禁闭相位于旋转系统外围，解禁闭相靠近旋转轴。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旋转胶子等离子体中的相结构，探索在旋转条件下禁闭-解禁闭相变的空间分布特性。传统基于Tolman-Ehrenfest定律的简单图像无法解释这种非均匀相的空间结构，需要新的理论框架。

Method: 采用第一性原理数值模拟（first-principles numerical simulations），计算局域临界温度作为角速度和半径的函数。使用完整（虚）旋转系统和局域热化近似两种方法，并进行解析延拓到实角频率域。首次对旋转$N_f=2$ QCD进行格点模拟（lattice simulation）。

Result: 发现了一种新的空间非均匀相，同时包含禁闭（confining）和解禁闭（deconfining）状态区域，由空间相变分隔。两种计算方法结果高度一致。解析延拓表明禁闭相位于旋转系统外围，解禁闭相靠近旋转轴。弯曲共转背景中胶子作用量的各向异性可以定量解释这种空间结构违背Tolman-Ehrenfest定律的现象。

Conclusion: 旋转胶子等离子体中存在新的空间非均匀相，其结构特征由局域临界温度决定。弯曲共转背景的各向异性效应是关键物理机制，且这一现象在包含动力学夸克的$N_f=2$ QCD理论中同样存在。

Abstract: Using first-principles numerical simulations, we find a new spatially inhomogeneous phase in a rotating gluon plasma. This mixed phase simultaneously contains regions of both confining and deconfining states in thermal equilibrium, separated by a spatial transition. The position of the boundary between the two phases is determined by the local critical temperature. We calculate the critical temperature of the local transition as a function of angular velocity and radius for a full (imaginary) rotating system and within a local thermalization approximation, and find an excellent agreement between these approaches. An analytic continuation of the results to the domain of real angular frequencies indicates that the confinement phase localizes at the periphery of the rotating system and the deconfinement phase appears closer to the rotation axis. We argue that the anisotropy of the gluon action in the curved co-rotating background can quantitatively explain the remarkable property that the spatial structure of this inhomogeneous phase disobeys the picture based on a straightforward implementation of the Tolman-Ehrenfest law. We also perform the first lattice simulation of rotating $N_f=2$ QCD which confirms that a similar picture is expected for theory with dynamical quarks.

</details>


### [161] [Universal and non-universal finite-volume effects in the vicinity of chiral phase transition in (2+1)-flavor QCD](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.23118)
*Sabarnya Mitra,Jishnu Goswami,Frithjof Karsch*

TL;DR: 本文通过有限尺寸标度分析，研究了具有两个无质量夸克的QCD中手征相变序参数，使用HISQ格点QCD数据验证了O(2)标度行为，并量化了有限尺寸效应的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在通过有限尺寸标度分析，提高从直接格点QCD模拟中获取的手征序参数无限体积外推估计的可靠性，并更精确地确定手征相变温度。

Method: 采用高度改进的交错夸克（highly improved staggered quarks, HISQ）进行格点QCD计算，在欧几里得格点上使用时间维度Nτ=8，空间体积Nσ满足3Nτ≤Nσ≤10Nτ，轻夸克质量范围1/240≤mℓ/ms≤1/27。

Result: 无限体积外推的序参数数据与预期的O(2)标度行为吻合良好，即使在物理的轻-奇异夸克质量比下也是如此；研究量化了渐近标度的偏差，并详细分析了固定格点截断下温度和夸克质量对有限尺寸效应的影响。

Conclusion: 有限尺寸标度分析对于提高手征序参数无限体积外推估计的可靠性至关重要，有助于从直接格点QCD模拟中更精确地确定手征相变温度。

Abstract: In this proceeding, we discuss the finite-size scaling analysis of the order parameter related to the chiral phase transition in QCD with two massless quarks. We use data obtained in lattice QCD calculations performed with highly improved staggered quarks (HISQ) for a range of light quark masses, $1/240 \leq m_\ell/m_s \leq 1/27$ for different spatial volumes ($N_σ$) on Euclidean lattices with temporal extent $N_τ=8$, satisfying $3\,N_τ\leq N_σ\leq 10\,N_τ$. We observe that infinite volume extrapolated data for the order parameter agree reasonably well with the expected $O(2)$ scaling behavior even for physical ratios of the light-to-strange quark mass ratio. We quantify deviations from asymptotic scaling and perform a detailed analysis of the influence of finite-size effects in terms of temperature and quark masses at a fixed lattice cutoff. This is crucial for improving the reliability of the infinite-volume extrapolated estimate of the chiral order parameter and for a more precise determination of chiral phase transition temperature from direct Lattice QCD simulations.

</details>


### [162] [Symmetric Mass Generation via Multicriticality in a 3D Lattice Gross-Neveu Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.23158)
*Sandip Maiti,Debasish Banerjee,Shailesh Chandrasekharan,Marina K. Marinkovic*

Main category: hep-lat

TL;DR: 本研究通过大规模蒙特卡洛模拟，在三维晶格模型中探索了两种无质量交错费米子通过两个四费米子相互作用耦合的相图，揭示了传统与非传统费米子质量生成机制的统一框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索两种无质量交错费米子（massless staggered fermions）通过两个独立的四费米子相互作用（four-fermion interactions）耦合时的相结构，旨在理解传统与非传统费米子质量生成机制在单一模型中的统一性。

Method: 采用大规模费米子袋蒙特卡洛模拟（large-scale fermion-bag Monte Carlo simulations）方法，在$(U_I, U_B)$参数空间中绘制相图，识别不同相之间的转变特征。

Result: 研究识别出三个不同相：无质量费米子相、对称性破缺有质量相和对称有质量相。当$U_B=0$时，系统经历单一连续转变直接连接无质量相和对称有质量相，这与非传统费米子质量生成相关。非零$U_B$将此直接转变分离为两个连续转变，中间出现对称性破缺相。

Conclusion: 从无质量相到破缺相的转变属于Gross-Neveu普适类（Gross-Neveu universality class），而从破缺相到对称有质量相的转变属于三维XY普适类（three-dimensional XY universality class）。零耦合的特殊点作为多临界点（multicritical point）组织周围相结构，为传统与非传统费米子质量生成机制提供了统一的晶格视角。

Abstract: We investigate a three-dimensional lattice model of two flavors of massless staggered fermions coupled through two independent four-fermion interactions, $U_I$ and $U_B$. Using large-scale fermion-bag Monte Carlo simulations, we map out the phase diagram in the $(U_I, U_B)$ parameter space and identify three distinct phases: a massless fermion phase, a symmetry-broken massive phase, and a symmetric massive phase. When one of the interactions is absent ($U_B=0$), the system undergoes a single continuous transition directly connecting the massless and symmetric massive phases, a feature previously associated with unconventional fermion mass generation. We find that turning on a nonzero $U_B$ separates this direct transition into two successive transitions with an intermediate symmetry-broken phase. The transition from the massless to the broken phase belongs to the Gross-Neveu universality class, while the transition from the broken to the symmetric massive phase falls into the three-dimensional XY universality class. Our results indicate that the special point at vanishing coupling, where the direct transition occurs, plays the role of a multicritical point organizing the surrounding phase structure. These findings provide a unified lattice perspective on conventional and unconventional mechanisms of fermion mass generation within a single model.

</details>

### [163] [Black hole Limits Redefined: Extreme Efficiency in Black Hole Jets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.22824)
*Antonios Nathanail*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本文通过先进的一般相对论磁流体动力学（GRMHD）模拟，首次实现了持续约10,000动力学时间的准稳态磁滞吸积盘状态，在该状态下喷流功率超过吸积能量输入两个数量级以上，挑战了黑洞能量提取的传统极限假设。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 黑洞的相对论性喷流（relativistic jets）不仅可以从吸积过程中提取能量，还能通过Blandford-Znajek机制直接从黑洞自旋中提取能量。一个长期存在的问题是：磁场通量（magnetic flux）能否在事件视界附近积累到完全停止吸积的程度，从而实现纯粹从自旋中提取能量。尽管先前研究表明吸积会通过不稳定性持续进行，且喷流功率仅略高于吸积能量预算，但一些观测结果暗示可能存在更高的效率。

Method: 本研究采用最先进的一般相对论磁流体动力学（general relativistic magnetohydrodynamic, GRMHD）模拟，维持了准稳态的磁滞吸积盘（magnetically arrested disk）状态约10,000个动力学时间（dynamical times）。

Result: 模拟结果显示，在整个方位角范围内吸积被全局抑制（globally suppressed）。在这种状态下，喷流功率（jet power）超过吸积能量输入两个数量级以上，达到了先前未实现的效率水平。

Conclusion: 这些结果挑战了关于黑洞能量提取极限的传统假设，为解释强大喷流系统提供了新的理论框架。研究结果提出了关于此类状态长期稳定性和Blandford-Znajek过程基本极限的重要问题。

Abstract: Relativistic jets from black holes can extract energy not only from accretion but also directly from the black hole's spin, as described by the Blandford-Znajek mechanism. A longstanding question is whether magnetic flux can accumulate near the event horizon to such an extent that it halts accretion entirely, enabling energy extraction purely from spin. Previous studies have shown that accretion persists through instabilities and that jet power only modestly exceeds the accretion energy budget, yet some observational results suggest much higher efficiencies. Here we present state-of-the-art general relativistic magnetohydrodynamic (GRMHD) simulations that sustain a quasi-steady magnetically arrested disk state for approximately 10,000 dynamical times, during which accretion is globally suppressed across the full azimuthal extent. In this regime, jet power exceeds the accretion energy input by more than two orders of magnitude, demonstrating a previously unachieved level of efficiency. These results challenge conventional assumptions about the limits of black hole energy extraction and suggest a new framework for interpreting powerful jet systems. Our findings raise important questions about the long-term stability of such states and the fundamental limits of the Blandford-Znajek process.

</details>


### [164] [A Lorentz-Covariant Spectral Universality of Stochastic Fields](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.23195)
*Alexander G. Tevzadze*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本文推导了闵可夫斯基时空中平稳随机场的洛伦兹协变谱普适性（Lorentz-covariant spectral universality），证明在超过一维空间时，不存在协变的局部映射能够关联时间和空间功率谱。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于建立相对论性谱推断（relativistic spectral inference）的洛伦兹协变（Lorentz-covariant）表述。当前需要理解在闵可夫斯基时空中，平稳随机场的谱特性如何受洛伦兹对称性约束。

Method: 方法基于推导闵可夫斯基时空中平稳随机场的洛伦兹协变谱普适性。通过分析洛伦兹齐次谱（Lorentz homogeneous spectra），研究时间指数（temporal index）的对称性保护特性及其与空间指数的关系。

Result: 结果表明：对于洛伦兹齐次谱，时间指数具有对称性保护（symmetry protected）和观测者不变性（observer invariant），且与空间指数（spatial index）的偏移由有效动量空间维度（effective momentum space dimensionality）设定的普适几何因子决定。谱普适性在各项异性标度（anisotropic scaling）和色散主导谱（dispersion dominated spectra）情况下会失效。

Conclusion: 结论强调了建立相对论性谱推断的洛伦兹协变表述的必要性。谱普适性的存在与破坏条件为理解相对论框架下的随机场统计特性提供了理论基础。

Abstract: We derive a Lorentz-covariant spectral universality for stationary stochastic fields in Minkowski spacetime. We show that no covariant local mapping can relate temporal and spatial power spectra in more than one spatial dimension. For Lorentz homogeneous spectra, the temporal index is symmetry protected, observer invariant, and offset from the spatial index by a universal geometric factor set by effective momentum space dimensionality. We show how spectral universality breaks down for anisotropic scaling and dispersion dominated spectra, establishing the necessity of a Lorentz-covariant formulation of relativistic spectral inference.

</details>


### [165] [The Axion-Photon Mixing and the Extragalactic Magnetic Background: Plateau Regimes, Resonances, and Non-Gaussian Boosts](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.23249)
*Andrea Addazi,Yi-Fu Cai,Salvatore Capozziello,Qingyu Gan,Gaetano Lambiase*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 该研究对轴子类粒子（ALP）-光子混合过程进行了分析处理，考虑了河外背景光（EBL）衰减效应，适用于恒定、高斯随机和非高斯磁场配置，对LHAASO、HAWC和CTA等甚高能（VHE）伽马射线观测具有直接意义。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于分析甚高能（VHE）伽马射线观测中轴子类粒子（ALP）-光子混合过程，特别是考虑河外背景光（EBL）衰减效应，以理解不同磁场配置（恒定、高斯随机、非高斯）对观测结果的影响。

Method: 研究方法包括：对于恒定磁场，推导精确概率并识别微扰平台区域；对于高斯随机磁场，首次获得强衰减区域中非指数衰减分量的解析公式；对于非高斯磁场，扩展分析框架，研究非高斯性对光子存活概率的影响。

Result: 研究结果显示：在恒定磁场中，光子存活概率与磁场的四次方成正比；在高斯随机磁场中，光子存活概率比广泛使用的域状模型低4-6个数量级；在非高斯磁场中，非高斯性可使光子存活概率相对高斯情况提高数个数量级。

Conclusion: 研究结论表明：随机磁场不能简化为域状相干模型而不丢失基本物理；甚高能（VHE）伽马射线光谱编码了关于河际磁场功率谱和非高斯结构的可观测信息，这对下一代PeV灵敏度观测站至关重要。

Abstract: We present an analytical treatment of Axion-Like-Particle (ALP)--photon mixing with extragalactic background light (EBL) attenuation for constant, Gaussian-stochastic, and non-Gaussian magnetic field configurations--with direct implications for Very High Energy (VHE) gamma-ray observations such as LHAASO, HAWC, and CTA experiments. For constant fields, we derive exact probabilities and identify a perturbative plateau regime where photon survival scales as quartic order of magnetic field, isolating the four-point magnetic correlation as a sensitive probe of non-Gaussianity. For Gaussian stochastic fields, we obtain--for the first time--analytical formulas for non-exponential-decay components in the strong-attenuation regime. Contrary to the widely used domain-like model, photon survival is suppressed by 4-6 orders of magnitude, while both conversion and survival probabilities exhibit distinct multi-peak structures from mass-equal resonance, stochastic resonance, and EBL attenuation. Extending to non-Gaussian fields, we show that non-Gaussianity can enhance photon survival by several orders of magnitude relative to the Gaussian case, potentially explaining the unexpectedly VHE photon event observed by LHAASO. Our results demonstrate that stochastic magnetic fields cannot be reduced to domain-like coherence without losing essential physics, and that VHE gamma-ray spectra encode observable information about both the power spectrum and non-Gaussian structure of intergalactic magnetic fields--critical as next-generation observatories push toward PeV sensitivities.

</details>

### [166] [Zatom-1: A Multimodal Flow Foundation Model for 3D Molecules and Materials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.22251)
*Alex Morehead,Miruna Cretu,Antonia Panescu,Rishabh Anand,Maurice Weiler,Tynan Perez,Samuel Blau,Steven Farrell,Wahid Bhimji,Anubhav Jain,Hrushikesh Sahasrabuddhe,Pietro Lio,Tommi Jaakkola,Rafael Gomez-Bombarelli,Rex Ying,N. Benjamin Erichson,Michael W. Mahoney*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: Zatom-1是首个统一3D分子与材料生成与预测学习的基础模型（foundation model），通过多模态流匹配（multimodal flow matching）目标联合建模离散原子类型与连续3D几何结构，在生成与预测任务上均表现优异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有AI方法通常针对单一化学领域（分子或材料）和单一任务（生成或预测）进行优化，这限制了表征共享与迁移。需要开发能够统一处理3D化学建模中分子与材料、生成与预测的通用方法。

Method: Zatom-1采用Transformer架构，通过多模态流匹配（multimodal flow matching）目标联合建模离散原子类型与连续3D几何结构。该方法支持可扩展的预训练，并利用联合生成预训练作为下游多任务预测的通用初始化。

Result: Zatom-1在生成与预测基准测试中匹配或超越了专业基线模型，同时将生成推理时间减少了一个数量级以上。实验表明联合生成预训练在化学领域间产生了正向预测迁移：预训练中建模材料提高了分子性质预测的准确性。

Conclusion: Zatom-1成功实现了3D分子与材料生成与预测学习的统一，证明了联合生成预训练作为通用初始化的有效性，并为跨化学领域的表征共享与迁移提供了新途径。

Abstract: General-purpose 3D chemical modeling encompasses molecules and materials, requiring both generative and predictive capabilities. However, most existing AI approaches are optimized for a single domain (molecules or materials) and a single task (generation or prediction), which limits representation sharing and transfer. We introduce Zatom-1, the first foundation model that unifies generative and predictive learning of 3D molecules and materials. Zatom-1 is a Transformer trained with a multimodal flow matching objective that jointly models discrete atom types and continuous 3D geometries. This approach supports scalable pretraining with predictable gains as model capacity increases, while enabling fast and stable sampling. We use joint generative pretraining as a universal initialization for downstream multi-task prediction of properties, energies, and forces. Empirically, Zatom-1 matches or outperforms specialized baselines on both generative and predictive benchmarks, while reducing the generative inference time by more than an order of magnitude. Our experiments demonstrate positive predictive transfer between chemical domains from joint generative pretraining: modeling materials during pretraining improves molecular property prediction accuracy.

</details>

### [167] [Dynamic Level Sets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.22530)
*Michael Stephen Fiske*

Main category: cs.CC

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 识别出一个名为"动态水平集（dynamic level sets）"的新数学概念，该概念在标准数学文献中不存在，并且解释了为何经典结果如de Leeuw-Moore-Shannon-Shapiro定理未能捕捉到这一概念。

Conclusion: 论文成功识别并分析了一个先前隐含的数学概念"动态水平集"，该概念代表了动力系统、拓扑学和可计算性理论交叉领域的一个新数学对象，填补了现有理论框架的空白。

Abstract: A mathematical concept is identified and analyzed that is implicit in the 2012 paper Turing Incomputable Computation, presented at the Alan Turing Centenary Conference (Turing 100, Manchester). The concept, called dynamic level sets, is distinct from mathematical concepts in the standard literature on dynamical systems, topology, and computability theory. A new mathematical object is explained and why it may have escaped prior characterizations, including the classical result of de Leeuw, Moore, Shannon, and Shapiro (1956) that probabilistic Turing machines compute no more than deterministic ones.

### [168] [Collective Dynamics in Spiking Neural Networks Beyond Dale's Principle](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.23202)
*Ross Ah-Weng,Hardik Rajpal*

Main category: q-bio.NC

TL;DR: 本文提出一个违反戴尔原则（Dale's Principle）的"双语"神经元最小模型，该模型能够同时产生兴奋性和抑制性效应，并展示了其在同步-异步动力学转换中的独特信息处理特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统神经科学遵循戴尔原则（Dale's Principle），认为每个神经元的所有突触释放相同的神经递质集合，但最近的实验证据表明存在违反该原则的共释放机制。现有脉冲神经网络模型大多基于神经元非兴奋即抑制的二分假设，需要建立新模型来研究违反戴尔原则的神经元动力学特性。

Method: 引入一个违反戴尔原则的"双语"神经元最小模型，该模型能够同时施加兴奋性和抑制性效应。通过识别参数区域，比较该架构与匹配的单语控制架构在同步和异步动力学之间的转换差异。

Result: 该架构在参数区域中表现出与单语控制架构定量不同的同步-异步动力学转换。在相变附近，神经元层面和神经元间高阶相互作用都显示出独特的信息处理特征。

Conclusion: 违反戴尔原则的神经元群体可能为调节神经回路中的大规模振荡活动提供替代机制，这些发现对理解神经信息处理具有重要启示。

Abstract: Dale's Principle has historically guided neuroscience research as a valuable rule of thumb, namely that all synapses on each neuron release the same set of neurotransmitters. Most existing Spiking Neuron Network models share this dichotomous assumption that neurons are either excitatory or inhibitory; however, recent experimental evidence points towards co-release mechanisms that violate this assumption. Here, we introduce a minimal model of "Bilingual" neurons violating Dale's principle that can exert both excitatory and inhibitory effects. We identify parameter regimes in which this architecture exhibits transitions between synchronous and asynchronous dynamics that differ quantitatively from those observed in a matched monolingual control architecture. We report distinct information-processing signatures both at the level of neurons and higher-order interactions between them near the phase transitions. These results suggest that the population of neurons violating Dales principle may provide an alternative mechanism for regulating large-scale oscillatory activity in neural circuits.

</details>

### [169] [Field-induced phase transitions in ferro-antiferromagnetic diblock copolymers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.22382)
*Alberto Raiola,Emanuele Locatelli,Davide Marenduzzo,Enzo Orlandini*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究通过平均场方法和蒙特卡洛模拟，探索了磁性二嵌段共聚物在外部磁场下的相行为，发现了包括溶胀相、混合致密相、分离致密相和杂化分离相在内的丰富相图。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究磁性二嵌段共聚物的平衡性质，其中每个单体带有伊辛型自旋。自旋在嵌段内铁磁相互作用，在嵌段间反铁磁相互作用，导致磁有序与空间组织之间的竞争（frustration）。

Method: 采用平均场方法（mean-field approach）和立方晶格上自回避行走（self-avoiding walks）的蒙特卡洛模拟（Monte Carlo simulations），研究系统对外部磁场的响应。

Result: 发现了丰富的相图，包括：两个丝状结构磁无序且空间扩展的溶胀相（swollen phase）；两个丝状结构强烈缠绕的单一球状混合致密相（mixed compact phase）；两个磁有序且空间分离的球状嵌段组成的分离致密相（segregated compact phase）。当嵌段内铁磁相互作用强度不同时，还观察到杂化分离相（hybrid segregated phase），其中一个扩展嵌段与一个塌缩嵌段共存。

Conclusion: 平均场预测与蒙特卡洛模拟在相边界位置方面定量一致。这些发现为磁场控制的可调谐图案自组装提供了最小统计力学框架，也可作为研究内部表观遗传样状态与染色质折叠耦合的简单平台。

Abstract: We study the equilibrium properties of a model of magnetic diblock copolymer where each monomer is decorated with an Ising-like spin. Spins interact ferromagnetically within each block and antiferromagnetically across blocks, generating frustration between magnetic ordering and spatial organization. By employing a mean-field approach and Monte Carlo simulations for self-avoiding walks on the cubic lattice, we investigate the system's response to an external magnetic field. We discover a rich phase diagram that includes: a swollen phase with both filaments magnetically disordered and spatially extended; a mixed compact phase characterized by a single globule in which the two filaments are strongly intertwined; a segregated compact phase composed of two globular, magnetically ordered, and spatially separated blocks. Further, if the magnitude of the intra-block ferromagnetic interaction differs between the two blocks, we observe a hybrid segregated (``tadpole'') phase where one extended block coexists with a collapsed one. Mean-field predictions are in quantitative agreement with Monte Carlo results for the location of the phase boundaries. These findings provide a minimal statistical-mechanical framework for field-controlled self-assembly of tunable patterns by magnetically heterogeneous polymers. They may also serve as a simple platform to investigate the coupling between internal epigenetic-like states and chromatin folding.

</details>

*Praveen Kumar Singh,Salman Ahmad Khan,Soumik Das*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 生物系统常在有序与混沌边界运行，通过从定向到不规则动力学的转变实现适应性和鲁棒性。在人工软物质中重现此类转变仍是一个核心挑战。

Method: 研究在非手性向列相液晶（achiral nematic liquid crystals）中建立了生物启发的directron动力学体系，通过多directron相互作用驱动系统演化。进一步引入了基于偶极子的最小模型（minimal dipole-based model）来定性捕捉这一转变的物理机制。

Result: 系统发展出共存的directron家族，具有竞争性轨迹，表现出随机化运动、动态组装形成以及高能到低能子directron的自发裂变，模拟了生物群体中观察到的表型多样性。超过临界电场时，这些相互作用驱动系统进入混沌状态，与先前报道的定向行为不同。

Conclusion: 该研究建立了一个人工活性系统，其中混沌从相互作用中内在涌现，为研究生物动力学提供了多功能平台，并为涉及自适应传输、货物递送和能量转导的液晶基软物质应用开辟了新途径。

Abstract: Biological systems often operate at the boundary between order and chaos, transitioning from directed to irregular dynamics to achieve adaptability and robustness. Reproducing such transitions in artificial soft matter remains a central challenge. Here, we report a biomimetic regime of directron dynamics in achiral nematic liquid crystals, in which coherent, directed motion collectively evolves into chaos. Driven by multi-directron interactions, the system develops coexisting directron families with competing trajectories, displaying randomized motion, dynamic assembly formation and spontaneous fission of high energy to low energy daughter directrons - all of which mimics the phenotypic diversity observed in biological groups. Above a critical electric field, these interactions drive the system into a chaotic state that is distinct from the directed behaviours reported previously. We further introduce a minimal dipole-based model that qualitatively captures the underlying physics of this transition. Together, our results establish an artificial active system in which chaos emerges intrinsically from interactions, offering a versatile platform to study biological dynamics and opening new avenues for liquid-crystal-based soft-matter applications involving adaptive transport, cargo delivery, and energy transduction

Abstract: Morphogenesis involves complex shape changes of biological tissues. Yet, tissue shape changes depend on tissue rheology, which in turn arises from the interplay of large numbers of cells. Here, we link cell- and tissue-scale mechanics by constructing mean-field rheological relations for the vertex model. In contrast to past work in the field, we study a vertex model with an explicit viscous friction. We also include two different cellular mechanisms creating active, anisotropic stresses. Our mean-field model accounts for cell shape and the non-linear elastic and visco-plastic regimes. We validate our results by predicting the response to large-amplitude oscillatory shear. There are several vertex model variants, and comparing to results from the literature, we show that their rheology depends on a number of model details. Our approach should be sufficiently general to construct non-linear mean-field constitutive relations for any cell-based tissue model.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: We investigate the steady uniform shear flow of a granular gas composed of inelastic and rough Maxwell particles. The rotational-to-translational temperature ratio and the proportionality between the spin-spin and stress tensors are shown to be independent of the coefficient of normal restitution and determined solely by roughness and moment of inertia. The reduced normal stresses, shear stress, and shear rate are obtained explicitly in terms of two effective parameters generalizing the cooling and stress relaxation rates of the smooth model. From these results we derive exact expressions for the non-Newtonian shear viscosity, the first viscometric function, and the friction coefficient. The dependence of the rheological properties on the normal and tangential restitution coefficients is analyzed in detail, revealing strong non-Newtonian behavior and nonmonotonic effects of roughness. The results reduce, in the appropriate limits, to those of the inelastic Maxwell model for smooth particles and to the Pidduck gas in the elastic perfectly rough case.

### [173] [Coupling between Phase Separation and Geometry on a Closed Elastic Curve: Free Energy Minimization and Dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.22977)
*Hanchun Wang,Ronojoy Adhikari,Michael E. Cates*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了闭合弹性细丝（二维空间中的一维曲线）的自由能与动力学，其中局部内态由曲率、拉伸和代表吸附物种浓度的标量密度场描述。密度场倾向于相分离，而局部自发曲率与浓度相关。研究通过数值模拟揭示了几何形状与密度场之间的强耦合效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于深入理解闭合弹性细丝系统中几何形状与密度场的耦合动力学。先前研究通常局限于Monge规范（Monge gauge），而本研究旨在处理完整微分几何框架下的耦合动力学问题，特别是关注近乎不可拉伸（nearly inextensible）体系中的相分离与曲率耦合效应。

Method: 研究方法包括：1）构建闭合细丝完整微分几何框架下的耦合动力学模型，结合Willmore流（Willmore flow）和Cahn-Hilliard梯度流（Cahn-Hilliard gradient flow）；2）采用数值策略进行全局自由能最小化（global free energy minimization）；3）模拟大范围模型参数下的平衡形状与密度分布；4）对选定参数进行完全动力学模拟，追踪各自由能贡献的时间演化。

Result: 主要结果包括：1）相图（phase diagram）由少量简单形状主导，这些形状表现出局部曲率与浓度的强耦合；2）发现某些参数区间中，曲能和/或拉伸能完全抑制相分离；3）动力学模拟常到达亚稳态最小值（metastable minima）而非平衡态，例如出现多于最小相界面数的状态；4）这些亚稳态在刚性圆形域上的相分离中不存在，表明其直接源于几何与密度的耦合。

Conclusion: 研究结论表明，闭合弹性细丝系统中几何形状与密度场的耦合导致独特的相行为与动力学特征。曲率和拉伸能可抑制相分离，而动力学过程常陷入亚稳态，这些现象在刚性几何中不存在，凸显了可变形几何对相分离过程的重要影响。

Abstract: We study the free energy and dynamics of a closed elastic filament (a one-dimensional curve in two dimensions) whose local internal state is specified by curvature, stretch, and a scalar density field representing, for example, the concentration of an absorbed species. The density variable has a tendency to phase-separate whereas the local spontaneous curvature is concentration-dependent. There is also a coupling between concentration and the stretching of the filament, although our main interest is in the nearly inextensible regime. We formulate and simulate the dynamics, comprising a coupled Willmore flow and Cahn-Hilliard gradient flow on the full differential geometry of a closed filament, addressing issues that previous work typically sidestepped by restricting to the Monge gauge. We use a numerical strategy for global free energy minimization, presenting the equilibrium shapes and density profiles across a wide range of model parameters. The phase diagram is dominated by a relatively small number of simple shapes that exhibit, as expected, strong coupling between local curvature and concentration. We also find regimes where curvature and/or stretching energies suppress phase separation altogether. For selected parameter values we present fully dynamical results, tracking the time evolution of the various contributions to the free energy. The dynamics often arrive at metastable minima rather than the equilibrium state - for example, at states with more than the minimum number of interfaces between coexisting phases. The metastability of these states is absent for phase separation on a rigid circular domain and thus a direct result of the coupling between geometry and density.

### [174] [Depth-dependent interplay of dynamical heterogeneity and chain dynamics at the surface of glass-forming polymers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.23106)
*Bao T. Ma,David S. Simmons*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究通过分子动力学模拟揭示聚合物薄膜中界面与体相动态异质性对链松弛的相反影响：自由表面加速的链段松弛抑制Rouse标度指数，而体相增强的Rouse标度指数，两者通过线性梯度分离。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 自由表面附近加速的链段迁移率将Rouse标度指数抑制至γ=0.4的低值，这反映了界面迁移率梯度引起的瞬态局域化而非拓扑缠结。相反，薄膜内部表现出增强的Rouse标度指数，与异质Rouse模型（Heterogeneous Rouse Model, HRM）预测一致，表明体相动态异质性压缩了Rouse区域。最小标度指数γ_min的深度映射揭示了一个线性梯度，将体相增强区域与表面抑制区域分离。

Conclusion: 体相和界面动态异质性以相反方式改变链松弛行为，Rouse标度可作为聚合物中玻璃态动态异质性和界面动态梯度的敏感空间分辨探针。这些发现建立了链尺度动力学与局部动态异质性之间的定量联系。

Abstract: Polymer thin films exhibit pronounced interfacial mobility gradients that modify chain relaxation, yet how these gradients govern chain-scale dynamics across depth remains incompletely understood. Using molecular dynamics simulations of freestanding glass-forming polymer films, we resolve how depth-dependent variations in segmental relaxation shape chain dynamics across a wide range of displacement scales. Near the free surface, accelerated segmental mobility suppresses Rouse-regime scaling exponents to values as low as gamma = 0.4, reflecting transient localization induced by interfacial mobility gradients rather than topological entanglement. In contrast, the film interior exhibits enhanced Rouse scaling exponents consistent with predictions of the Heterogeneous Rouse Model (HRM), indicating that bulk dynamic heterogeneity compresses the Rouse regime. Mapping the minimum scaling exponent gamma_min across depth reveals a linear gradient that separates the bulk-like enhancement regime from the surface-induced suppression regime of chain dynamical scaling. Together, these results demonstrate that bulk and interfacial dynamic heterogeneity modify chain relaxation in opposite ways and establish Rouse scaling as a sensitive, spatially resolved probe of glassy dynamical heterogeneity and interfacial dynamical gradients in polymers.

### [175] [Rheological properties and shear-induced structures of ferroelectric nematic liquid crystals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.23150)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 最近发现的铁电向列相（ferroelectric nematic, NF）液晶是具有极性取向序的流体，其电极化矢量可通过电场和表面锚定进行排列。本研究旨在探索剪切流如何影响NF材料的极化场和有效粘度，以增进对这些材料的理解并促进其应用。

Method: 研究探索了三种NF材料：RM734、DIO和室温铁电向列相FNLC919，这些材料均表现出顺电向列相（paraelectric nematic, N）和NF相。通过测量不同剪切速率下的粘度变化，分析温度依赖性和剪切诱导的结构效应。

Result: 所有材料在冷却时粘度均增加，呈现阿伦尼乌斯（Arrhenius）行为。DIO和FNLC919的反铁电SmZA相的有效粘度对剪切速率有强烈依赖性：高剪切速率下粘度低于N和NF相，但低剪切速率下则高得多。所有介晶相在低剪切速率下均表现出剪切稀化行为，高剪切速率下则呈现近牛顿行为。在取向方面，N和NF相观察到三种状态：低剪切速率下的流动取向、高剪切速率下指向矢和极化沿涡旋轴的滚动状态，以及中间速率下的多畴结构。

Conclusion: 在流动取向状态下，NF极化不会偏离剪切方向，这与N相指向矢的流动诱导倾斜形成鲜明对比。这一效应归因于避免流动NF中的展曲变形和相关空间电荷。粘度的温度和剪切速率依赖性以及揭示的剪切诱导结构效应，推进了对NF材料的理解并可能促进其应用。

Abstract: Recently discovered ferroelectric nematic (NF) liquid crystals are fluids with a polar orientational order. The electric polarization vector can be aligned by an electric field and by surface anchoring. Here, we explore how the polarization field and effective viscosity of the NF materials are affected by shear flows. We explore three NF materials, abbreviated RM734, DIO, and a room-temperature FNLC919, all of which exhibit a paraelectric nematic (N) and the NF phase. All materials show an increase of the viscosity upon cooling, with an Arrhenius behavior. In DIO and FNLC919, the antiferroelectric SmZA phase shows a strong dependence of the effective viscosity on the shear rate: this viscosity is lower than the viscosity of the N and NF phases at high shear rates but is much higher when the shear rate is low. The behavior is associated with the layered structure of the SmZA phase. All mesophases exhibit shear-thinning behavior at low shear rates and a nearly Newtonian behavior at higher shear rates. In terms of alignment, we observe three regimes in the N and NF phases: flow-alignment at low shear rates, log-rolling regime with the director and polarization along the vorticity axis at high shear rates, and polydomain structures at intermediate rates. In the flow-aligning regime, the NF polarization does not tilt away from the shear direction, which is in sharp contrast to the flow-induced tilt of the N director. The effect is attributed to the avoidance of splay deformations and associated space charge in the flowing NF. The temperature and shear rate dependencies of the viscosity and the uncovered shear-induced structural effects of NF advance our understanding of these materials and potentially facilitate their applications.

### [176] [Persistence-Driven Void Formation in Active-Passive Mixtures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.23178)
*Giulia Janzen,Liesbeth M. C. Janssen,Nuno A. M. Araújo,Rastko Sknepnek,D. A. Matoz-Fernandez*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了在活性-被动粒子混合物中，活性掺杂剂（active dopants）的持久性（persistence）增强会驱动从均匀流体化（homogeneous fluidization）到局部机械不稳定性（localized mechanical instability）的转变，而非简单地增强有效熔化效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 虽然已知稀薄活性掺杂剂能通过增强笼子破碎（cage breaking）和加速结构弛豫（structural relaxation）来熔化被捕获的非晶固体（amorphous solid），但尚不清楚增加持久性是仅仅放大这种有效熔化效应，还是从根本上重组了流体化机制本身。

Method: 研究采用了一个最小化的活性-被动混合物（minimal active-passive mixture）模型，通过系统性地增加活性粒子的持久性来观察流体化机制的转变。

Result: 增加持久性驱动了从均匀流体化到局部机械不稳定性的交叉转变（crossover）。持久性掺杂剂会积累应力并成核空穴（nucleate voids），当它们的机械扰动区域重叠时，重排（rearrangements）会局域化在空穴边界，活性与被动粒子表现出可比较的迁移率，产生类似人群mosh pit的动态行为。

Conclusion: 持久性通过应力积累（stress accumulation）和约束（confinement）重组了流体化过程，揭示了无序固体（disordered solids）中一种独特的非平衡局域化机制（nonequilibrium localization mechanism）。

Abstract: It is well established that dilute active dopants can melt an arrested amorphous solid by enhancing cage breaking and accelerating structural relaxation. Yet it remains unclear whether increasing persistence simply amplifies this effective melting or instead reorganizes the fluidization mechanism itself. Here we show that, in a minimal active-passive mixture, increasing persistence drives a crossover from homogeneous fluidization to a localized mechanical instability, demonstrating that sustained active forcing restructures relaxation in space rather than merely strengthening it. Persistent dopants accumulate stress and nucleate voids as their mechanically perturbed regions overlap. In this regime, rearrangements localize at void boundaries, and active and passive particles exhibit comparable mobility, producing dynamics reminiscent of crowd mosh pits. Persistence therefore reorganizes fluidization through stress accumulation and confinement, revealing a distinct nonequilibrium localization mechanism in disordered solids.

</details>
